ChronA (Plummer)
B17.1.
The Parker Chronicle: Plummer 1892-9.



 0.1. ÞY GEARE þE WæS AGAN FRAM CRISTES ACENnesse <foreign>cccc</foreign>
wintra. & <foreign>xciii</foreign> uuintra. þa Cerdic & Cynric his sunu cuom up æt
Cerdices oran. mid <foreign>v</foreign> scipum. & se Cerdic wæs. Elesing. Elesa. Esling.
Esla. Gewising. Giwis. Wiging. Wig. Freawining. Freawine. Friþugaring.
Friþugar. Bronding. Brond Bældæging. Bældæg Wodening.
 0.7. Ond þæs ymb <foreign>vi</foreign> gear þæs þe hie upcuomon geeodon
West Seaxna rice, & þæt uuærun þa ærestan cyningas þe West
Seaxna lond on Wealum geeodon; & he hæfde þæt rice <foreign>xvi</foreign> gear,
& þa he gefor þa feng his sunu Cynric to þam rice, & heold <foreign>xvii</foreign>
winter.
 0.11. Þa he gefor þa feng Ceol to þam rice, & heold <foreign>vi</foreign>
gear.
 0.12. Þa he gefor þa feng Ceolwulf to his broþur, & he
ricsode <foreign>xvii</foreign> gear, & hiera cyn gæþ to Cerdice.
 0.14. Þa feng Cynegils Ceolwulfes broþursunu to rice, ricsode
<foreign>xxxi</foreign> wintra, & he onfeng ærest fulwihte Wesseaxna cyninga; & þa
feng Cenwalh to, & heold <foreign>xxxi</foreign> wintra, & se Cenwalh wæs Cynegilses
sunu; & þa heold Seaxburg his cuen an gear þæt rice æfter him.
 0.17. Þa feng æscwine to rice, þæs cyn gæþ to
Cerdice, & heold <foreign>ii</foreign> gear.
 0.20. Þa feng Centwine to Wesseaxna rice Cynegilsing, &
ricsode <foreign>vii</foreign> gear; þa feng Ceadwalla to þam rice, þæs cyn gæþ to
Cerdice, & heold <foreign>iii</foreign> gear.
 0.22. Ða feng Ine to Seaxna rice, þæs cyn gæþ to
Ceardice, & heold <foreign>xxxvii</foreign> wintra.
 0.24. Þa feng æþelheard to, þæs cyn gæþ to
Ceardice, & heold <foreign>xiiii</foreign> winter.
 0.25. Þa feng Cuþred to, þæs cyn gæþ to Cerdice,
& heold <foreign>xvii</foreign> gear.
 0.26. Þa feng Sigebryht to, þæs cyn gæþ to Cerdice,
& heold an gear.
 0.27. Þa feng Cynewulf to rice, þæs cyn gæþ to
Ceardice, & heold <foreign>xxxi</foreign> wintra.
 0.29. Þa feng Beorhtric to rice, þæs cyn gæþ to
Cerdice, & heold <foreign>xvi</foreign> gear.
 0.30. Þa feng Ecgbryht to þam rice, & heold <foreign>xxxvii</foreign> wintra
& <foreign>vii</foreign> monaþ; & þa feng æþelwulf his sunu to, & heold
nigonteoðe healf gear.
 0.31. Se æþelwulf wæs Ecgbryhting. Ecgbryht. Ealhmunding.
Eahlmund. Eafing. Eafa. Eopping. Eoppa. Ingilding. Ingild. Cenreding. &
Ine. Cenreding. & Cuþburg. Cenreding. & Cuenburg. Cenreding. Cenred.
Ceolwalding. Ceolwald. Cuþwulfing. Cuþwulf Cuþwining. Cuþwine. Celming.
Celm. Cynricing. Cynric. Cerdicing.
 0.39. Ond þa feng æthelbald his sunu to rice, & heold <foreign>v</foreign>
gear.
 0.40. Þa feng æþelbryht his broþur to, & heold <foreign>v</foreign>
gear.
 0.40. Þa feng æþered hiera broþur to rice, & heold <foreign>v</foreign>
gear.
 0.41. Þa feng ælfred hiera broþur to rice, & þa was
agan his ielde <foreign>xxiii</foreign> wintra. & <foreign>ccc</foreign> & <foreign>xcvi</foreign> wintra þæs þe
his cyn ærest Westseaxna lond on Wealum geodon.
 0.45. AER Cristes geflæscnesse <foreign>lx</foreign> wintra. Gaius Iulius se
Casere ærest Romana Bretenlond gesohte. & Brettas mid gefeohte cnysede.
& hie oferswiþde, & swa þeah ne meahte þær rice gewinnan.
 1.1. <foreign>ANNO</foreign> Octauianus ricsode <foreign>lvi</foreign> wintra. & on þam <foreign>xlii</foreign>
geare his rices Crist wæs acenned.
 2.1. Þa tungel witgan of eastdæle cuomon to þon þæt hie
Crist weorþedon, & þa cild on Bethlem ofslægene wærun for Cristes
ehtnesse from Herode.
 3.1. Her swealt Herodus from himselfum ofsticod, & Archilaus
his sunu feng to rice.
 6.1. From frymþe middangeardes oþ þis gear wæron agan <foreign>v</foreign>
þusendu/ wintra. & <foreign>cc</foreign> wintra.
 11.1. Her onfeng Herodes Antipatres sunu to rice in Iudea.
 12.1. & Philippus & Herodes todældun Lysiam, &
Iudeam feowricum todældun.
 16.1. Her feng Tiberius to rice.
 27.1. Her onfeng Pilatus to gymenne ouer þa Iudeas.
 31.1. Her wæs Crist gefulluhtud. & Petrus & Andreas
gehwierfede. & Iacobus & Iohannes & Philippus & þa <foreign>xii</foreign>
apostolas.
 33.1. Her wæs Crist ahangen; from fruman middangeardes ymb <foreign>v</foreign>
þusendo wintra. & <foreign>cc</foreign> & <foreign>xxvi</foreign> wintra.
 34.1. Her wæs Paulus gehwierfed. & Sanctus Stephanus
oftorfod.
 35.1. Her se eadiga Petrus se apostol gesæt biscepsetl in
Antiochia þære ceastre.
 39.1. Her onfeng Gaius rice.
 45.1. Her se eadiga Petrus se apostol gesæt biscepsetl on
Rome.
 46.1. Her Herodes aswalt. se þe Iacobum ofslog ane geare ær
his agnum deaþe.
 47.1. Her Claudius oþer Romana cyninga Bretene lond gesohte,
& þone mæstan dæl þæs ealondes on his gewald onfeng. & eac
swelce Orcadus þa ealond Romanna cynedome underþeodde.
 47.4. Þis was þes feorðes geares his rices. & on þys
ylcan geare gewearð se mycela hunger on Siria þe Lucas recð on þare boc
<foreign>Acta Apostolorum</foreign>.
 62.1. Her Iacobus <foreign>frater Domini</foreign> þrowode.
 63.1. Her Marcus se godspellere forþferde.
 69.1. Her Petrus & Paulus þrowodon.
 70.1. Her Uespassianus onfeng rice.
 71.1. Her Titus Uespessianus sunu in Hierusalem ofslog Iudea <foreign>cxi</foreign>
þusenda;
 81.1. Her Titus feng to rice, se þe sæde þæt he þone
dæg forlure þe he noht to gode on ne gedyde;
 83.1. Her Domitianus Tites broður feng to rice.
 84.1. Her Iohannes se godspellere in Pathma þam ealonde wrat þa
boc Apocalipsis.
 99.1. Her Symon se apostol wæs anhangen. & Iohannes se
godspellere hine gereste in Epheso.
 101.1. Her Clemens papa forþferde.
 110.1. Her Ignatus biscep þrowude.
 155.1. Her Marcus Antonius & Aurelius his broðer fengon to
rice.
 167.1. Her Eleutherius on Rome onfeng biscepdom, & þone
wuldor fæstlice <foreign>xv</foreign> winter geheold; To þam Lucius Bretene kyning sende
stafas, bæd þæt he wære Cristen gedon. & he þurhteah þæt
he bæd. & hi syððon wunodon on rihton geleauon oððe Diaclitianes
rice.
 189.1. Her Seuerus onfeng rice, & ricsode <foreign>xvii</foreign> winter.
 189.2. Se Bretenlond mid dice begyrdde from sæ oþ sæ. &
þa geendode on Euerwic. & Bassianus his sunu feng to rice.
 200.1. Twa hund gæra.
 283.1. Her þrowade Sanctus Albanus martir.
 300.1. Ðreo hund gæra.
 379.1. Her Gratianus feng to rice.
 381.1. Her Maximianus se casere feng to rice.
 381.1. He wæs on Bretenlonde geboren. & þonne for in
Gallia walas. & he ðar ofsloh ðone casere Gratianum. & his broðer
adraf of æðele. se wæs gehaten Ualentinianus.
 381.4. & se Ualentinianus eft gesamnode werod, & ofsloh
Maximum & feng to rice.
 381.5. On þam timan aras Pelagies gedwyld geond middaneard.
 409.1. Her Gotan abræcon Romeburg, & næfre siþan Romane
ne ricsodon on Bretone.
 410.1. Þæt wæs embe <foreign>xi</foreign> hund wintra & <foreign>x</foreign> wintra þes
þe heo getimbred was.
 411.1. Ealles hi rixodon on Brytene feower hundwintra & hund
seouanti wintra. syððan ærost Gaius Iulius þæt lond ærost
gesohte.
 418.1. Her Romane gesomnodon al þa goldhord þe on Bretene
wæron, & sume on eorþan ahyddon. þæt hie nænig mon siþþan
findan ne meahte, & sume mid him on Gallia læddon.
 423.1. Her ðeodosius se gingra feng to rice.
 430.1. Her Palladius vel Patricius se biscep wæs onsended to
Scottum þæt he hiera geleafan trymede. from Cælestino þam papan.
 443.1. Her sendon Brytwalas to Rome. & heom fultomes bædon
wið Piohtas. ac hi þar næfdan nanne, forþan þe hi fyrdedon wið
ætla Huna cyningæ.
 443.3. & þa sendon hi to Anglum. & Angelcynnes
æðelingas ðæs ylcan bædan.
 449.1. Her Martianus & Ualentines onfengon rice. & ricsodon
<foreign>vii</foreign> winter.
 449.2. & on hiera dagum Hengest & Horsa from Wyrtgeorne
geleaþade Bretta kyninge gesohton Bretene on þam staþe þe is genemned
Ypwinesfleot. ærest Brettum to fultume, ac hie eft on hie fuhton.
 449.5. Se cing het hi feohtan agien Pihtas. & hi swa dydan,
& sige hæfdon swa hwar swa hi comon.
 449.5. Hi ða sende to Angle & heton heom sendan mare fultum.
& heom seggan Brytwalana nahtnesse. & ðæs landes cysta.
 449.7. Hy þa sendan heom mare fultum.
 449.8. Ða comon þa men of þrim mægðum Germanie. Of Eald
Seaxum. of Anglum, of Iotum.
 449.9. Of Iotum comon Cantware & Wihtware. þæt ys seo
mæið ðe nu eardað on Wiht & þæt cynn on Westsexum þe man
gyt hæt Iutna cyn.
 449.11. Of Eald Seaxon comon Eastsexa & Suðsexa &
Westsexan.
 449.11. Of Angle comon se a siððan stod westi betwyx Iutum
& Seaxum. East Engla. Midel Angla. Mearca & ealle Norðhymbra.
 455.1. Her Hengest & Horsa fuhton wiþ Wyrtgeorne þam
cyninge, in þære stowe þe is gecueden Agælesþrep, & his
broþur Horsan man ofslog.
 457.1. & æfter þam Hengest feng to rice & æsc his
sunu.
 457.1. Her Hengest & æsc fuhton wiþ Brettas in þære
stowe þe is gecueden Crecganford, & þær ofslogon <foreign>IIII</foreign> wera, &
þa Brettas þa forleton Centlond, & mid micle ege flugon to Lundenbyrg.
 465.1. Her Hengest & æsc gefuhton uuiþ Walas neah
Wippedesfleote, & þær <foreign>xii</foreign> Wilisce aldormenn ofslogon, & hiera
þegn an þær wearþ ofslægen, þam wæs noma Wipped.
 473.1. Her Hengest & æsc gefuhton wiþ Walas, & genamon
unarimedlico herereaf, & þa Walas flugon þa Englan swa fyr.
 477.1. Her cuom ælle on Breten lond, & his <foreign>iii</foreign> suna.
Cymen, & Wlencing, & Cissa. mid <foreign>iii</foreign> scipum, on þa stowe þe is
nemned Cymenes ora, & þær ofslogon monige Wealas, & sume on fleame
bedrifon on þone wudu þe is genemned Andredes leage.
 485.1. Her ælle gefeaht wiþ Walas neah Mearcrædesburnan
stæðe.
 488.1. Her æsc feng to rice, & was <foreign>xxiiii</foreign> wintra Cantwara
cyning.
 491.1. Her ælle & Cissa ymbsæton Andredescester, &
ofslogon alle þa þe þærinne eardedon, ne wearþ þær forþon an
Bret to lafe;
 495.1. Her cuomon twegen aldormen on Bretene. Cerdic & Cynric
his sunu, mid <foreign>v</foreign> scipum. in þone stede þe is gecueden Cerdices ora, &
þy ilcan dæge gefuhtun wiþ Walum.
 501.1. Her cuom Port on Bretene. & his <foreign>ii</foreign> suna Bieda &
Mægla mid <foreign>ii</foreign> scipum. on þære stowe þe is gecueden Portesmuþa,
& ofslogon anne giongne Brettisc monnan, swiþe æþelne monnan.
 508.1. Her Cerdic & Cynric ofslogon ænne Brettisc cyning,
þam was nama Natanleod. & <foreign>v</foreign> þusendu wera mid him, æfter þan
þæt lond wearð nemned Natan leaga oþ Cerdicesford.
 514.1. Her cuomon West Seaxe in Bretene mid <foreign>iii</foreign> scipum. in þa
stowe þe is gecueden Cerdices ora, Stuf & Wihtgær. & fuhtun wiþ
Brettas & hie gefliemdon.
 519.1. Her Cerdic & Cynric West Sexena rice onfengun, &
þy ilcan geare hie fuhton wiþ Brettas þær mon nu nemneþ
Cerdicesford. & siþþan ricsadan West Sexana cynebearn of þan
dæge.
 527.1. Her Cerdic & Cynric fuhton wiþ Brettas. in þære
stowe þe is gecueden Cerdices leaga.
 530.1. Her Cerdic & Cynric genamon Wihte ealond. & ofslogon
feala men on Wihtgaræsbyrg.
 534.1. Her Cerdic forþferde, & Cynric his sunu ricsode forþ
<foreign>xxvi</foreign> wintra, & hie saldon hiera tuæm nefum Stufe & Wihtgare eall
Wiehte/ ealond.
 538.1. Her sunne aþiestrode <foreign>xiiii</foreign> dagum ær <foreign>Kalendæ
Martii</foreign> from ærmergenne oþ undern.
 540.1. Her sunne aþiestrode on <foreign>xii Kalendæ Iulii</foreign>. &
steorran hie ætiewdon fulneah healfe tid ofer undern.
 544.1. Her Uuihtgar forþferde, & hiene mon bebyrgde on
Wihtgara byrg.
 547.1. Her Ida feng to rice, þonon Norþanhymbra cynecyn onwoc
& rixode twelf gear. & he timbrode Bebbanburh. seo wæs ærost mid
hegge betyned. & þaræfter mid wealle.
 549.1. Ida wæs Eopping, Eoppa Esing, Esa wæs Inguing. Ingui
Angenwitting. Angenwit Alocing. Aloc Benocing. Benoc Branding, Brand
Bældæging. Bældæg Wodening. Woden Freoþolafing, Freoþelaf
Freoþulfing. Friþulf Finning. Finn Godulfing. Godulf Geating.
 552.1. Her Cynric gefeaht wiþ Brettas in þære stowe þe is
genemned æt Searobyrg. & þa Bret Walas gefliemde.
 554.1. Cerdic wæs Cynrices fæder. Cerdic Elesing. Elesa
Esling. Esla Giwising. Giwis Wiging. Wig Freawining. Freawine Freoþogaring.
Freoþogar Branding. Brand Bældæging. Bældæg Wodening.
 556.1. Her Cynric & Ceawlin fuhton wiþ Brettas æt
Beranbyrg.
 560.1. Her Ceawlin feng to rice on Wesseaxum, & ælle feng to
Norþanhymbra rice.
 561.1. Idan forðgefarenum. & heora ægðer rixade <foreign>xxx</foreign>
wintra.
 562.1. Ælle wæs Yffing. Yffe Uxfreaing. Uxfrea Wilgisling.
Wilgisl Westerfalcing. Westerfalca Sæfugling. Sæfugl Sæbalding.
Sæbald Sigegeating. Sigegeat Swebdæging. Swebdæg Sigegaring. Sigegar
Wægdæging. Wægdæg Wodening.
 565.1. Her feng æðelbriht to Cantwara rice. & heold <foreign>liii</foreign>
wintra.
 565.1. On his dagum sende Gregorius us fulluht & Columba
mæssepreost com to Pihtum. & hi gecyrde to Cristes geleauan.
 565.3. Þæt synd þonne wærteras be norðum morum. &
heora cyng him gesealde þæt igland þe man Ii nemnað. þar syndon fif
hida. þæs ðe man seggað.
 565.5. Þar se Columban getimbrade mynster, & he þas wæs
abbod <foreign>xxxii</foreign>. wintra & þar forðferde. þa he was <foreign>lxxvii</foreign> wintra.
 565.7. Ða stowe habbað gyt his yrfnuman.
 565.7. Suþ Pihtas wæron ær gefullode of Ninna biscope. se
was on Rome gelæred.
 565.8. His mynster ys Hwiterne on Sanctus Martines naman gehalgod.
þar he resteð mid manegum halgum.
 565.10. Nu sceal beon æfre on Ii abbod, & na biscop. &
þan sculon beon underðeodde ealle Scotta biscopas. for þan þe Columban
was abbod, na biscop.
 565.13. Her Columba presbiter com of Scottum on Bryttas. Peohtas to
lærenne. & on Hii þam ealande mynster worhte.
 568.1. Her Ceaulin & Cuþa gefuhton wiþ æþelbryht.
& hine in Cent gefliemdon, & tuegen aldormen on Wibban dune ofslogon,
Oslaf & Cnebban.
 571.1. Her Cuþwulf feaht wiþ Bretwalas æt Bedcan forda.
& <foreign>iiii</foreign> tunas genom, Lygeanburg. & ægelesburg. Bænesingtun.
& Egonesham.
 571.3. & þy ilcan geare he geforþferde.
 577.1. Her Cuþwine & Ceawlin fuhton wiþ Brettas, & hie
<foreign>iii</foreign> kyningas ofslogon, Coinmail, & Condidan, & Farinmail, in
þære stowe þe is gecueden Deorham. & genamon <foreign>iii</foreign> ceastro

 583.1. Her Mauricius feng to Romana rice.
 584.1. Her Ceawlin & Cuþa fuhton wiþ Brettas, in þam
stede þe mon nemneþ Feþanleag. & Cuþan mon ofslog.
 584.2. & Ceaulin monige tunas genom, & unarimedlice
herereaf, & ierre he hwearf þonan to his agnum.
 588.1. Her ælle cyning forþferde, & æþelric ricsode
æfter him <foreign>v</foreign> gear.
 591.1. Her Ceolric ricsode <foreign>vi</foreign> gear.
 592.1. Her micel wælfill wæs æt Woddes beorge, &

 593.1. Her Ceawlin & Cuichelm & Crida forwurdon, &
æþelfriþ feng to rice on Norðhymbrum.
 595.1. Her Gregorius papa sende to Brytene Augustinum. mid wel
manegum munecum. þe Godes word Englaðeoda godspelledon.
 597.1. Her ongon Ceolwulf ricsian on Wesseaxum, & simle he
feaht. & won, oþþe wiþ Angelcyn, oþþe uuiþ Walas, oþþe
wiþ Peohtas, oþþe wiþ Scottas; Se wæs Cuþaing. Cuþa Cynricing,
Cynric Cerdicing, Cerdic Elesing, Elesa Esling, Esla Gewising, Giwis Wiging,
Wig Freawining, Freawine Friðugaring, Friðugar Bronding, Brond

 601.1. Her sende Gregorius papa Agustino ærcebiscepe pallium in
Bretene, & wel monige godcunde lareowas him to fultome; & Paulinus
biscep gehwerfde Edwine Norðhymbra cyning to fulwihte.
 603.1. Ægðan Scotta cyng feaht wið Dælreoda, & wið
æðelferþe Norþhymra cynge æt Dægstane, & man ofsloh mæst
ealne his here.
 603.2. Her wæs gefeoht æt Egesan stane.
 604.1. Augustinus gehalgode <foreign>ii</foreign> biscopas. Mellitum & Iustum.
 604.2. Her East Seaxe onfengon geleafan & fulwihtes bæð.
under Sæbrihte cinge & Mellite bisceope.
 604.3. Mellitum he sende to bodiende East Seaxum fulluht. ðar was
se cing gehaten Sæbyrht. Ricolan sunu. æðelberhtes swyster. þone
æðelbyrht gesette to cynge.
 604.6. & æðelberht gesealde Mellite biscopsetl on
Lundewic. & Iusto on Hrouecystre. seo ys <foreign>xxiiii</foreign> mila fram Dorwitceastre.
 606.1. Her forðferde Gregorius ymb <foreign>x</foreign> gear þæs þe he us
fulwiht sende;
 607.1. Her Ceolwulf gefeaht wið Suð Seaxe.
 607.1. And her æðelfrið lædde his færde to
Legercyestre, & ðar ofsloh unrim Walena.
 607.2. & swa wearð gefyld Augustinus witegunge. þe he
cwæð. Gif Wealas nellað sibbe wið us. hi sculan æt Seaxana handa
farwurþan.
 607.4. Þar man sloh eac <foreign>cc</foreign> preosta ða comon ðyder þæt
hi scoldon gebiddan for Walena here.
 607.6. Scrocmail was gehaten heora ealdormann. se atbærst
ðanon fiftiga sum.
 611.1. Her Cynegils feng to rice on Wesseaxum, & heold <foreign>xxxi</foreign>
wintra.
 611.2. Se Kynegils wæs Ceoling. Ceola Cuþing. Cuþa
Cynricing.
 614.1. Her Cynegils & Cuichelm gefuhton on Beandune, &
ofslogon <foreign>ii</foreign> þusendo Wala & <foreign>lxv</foreign>.
 616.1. Her æþelbryht Contwara cyning forþferde, &
Eadbald his sunu feng to rice.
 616.2. Se forlet his fulluht, & leouode on hæðenum þeawe
swa þæt he hæfde his fæder laue to wiue.
 616.3. Þa mynte Laurentius ðe þa was ercebiscop on Cent
þæt he wolde suð ofer sæ & eall forlæton.
 616.5. Ac him com to on niht se apostolus Petrus & hine
hetelice swang, for ðan ðe he wolde Godes hyrde forlæton & het hine
gan to þam cynge & bodian him rihtne geleafan.
 616.7. & he swa dyde & se cing gecyrde to rihtan geleauan.
 616.8. On þyses cinges dagum Laurentius ercebiscop se was on Cent
æfter Agustine forþferde <foreign>iiii Nonae Februarii</foreign> & he was bebyred be
Agustine.
 616.9. Æfter him feng Mellitus to arcebiscopdome se was biscop
of Lundinium & þas binnan fif wintre Mellitus forðferde.

ofslægene þa aldormen, & Wilsætan namon sige.

 880.1. Her for se here of Cirenceastre on East Engle, &

 880.2. & þy ilcan geare for se here ofer sæ þe ær on

 885.16. Se hæfde eac þæt westrice, & forþferde þy

 885.18. Se wæs Karles sunu þe æþelwulf West Seaxna cyning

 885.19. & þy ilcan geare gegadrode micel sciphere on

 885.22. Þy ilcan geare feng Carl to þam westrice, & to

 885.24. Se Carl was Hloþwiges sunu, se Hloþwig was Carles

 885.28. & þy ilcan geare forþferde se goda papa Marinus, se

 885.31. & þy ilcan geare se here on East Englum bræc

 886.1. Her for se here eft west þe ær east gelende, & þa

 893.14. Þa sona æfter þæm com Hæsten mid <foreign>lxxx</foreign> scipa

 894.1. On þys geare, þæt wæs ymb twelf monað þæs

 894.6. Þa gegaderade ælfred cyning his fierd, & for

 894.15. Hæfde se cyning his fierd on tu tonumen, swa þæt

 894.17. Ne com se here oftor eall ute of þæm setum þonne

 894.20. Þa hie gefengon micle herehyð, & þa woldon ferian

 894.26. Þa besæt sio fierd hie þær utan þa hwile þe

 894.27. Ac hie hæfdon þa heora stemn gesetenne, & hiora

 894.37. & þa þe suð ymbutan foron. ymb sæton

 894.52. & Hæstenes wif & his suna twegen mon brohte to

 894.55. Hæfdon hi hiora onfangen ær Hæsten to Beamfleote

 894.58. Ac sona swa hie to Bleam fleote comon, & þæt

 894.62. Þa se cyning hine þa west wende mid þære fierde

 894.64. Þa he þær togefaren wæs, þa eodon hie to hiora

 894.66. Þa he þa wið þone here þær wæst abisgod

 894.70. Foron þa up be Temese oþþæt hie gedydon æt

 894.71. Þa gegaderode æþered ealdormon, & æþelm

 894.85. & þær wearð Ordheh cyninges þegn ofslægen,

 894.89. Þa hie on East Seaxe comon to hiora geweorce. & to

 894.95. Þa ne mehte seo fird hie na hindan offaran, ær hie

 894.96. Besæton þeah þæt geweorc utan sume twegen dagas,

 895.1. Ond þa sona æfter þæm on ðys gere for se here of

 896.6. Þa þæs on hærfæste þa wicode se cyng on

 896.8. Þa sume dæge rad se cyng up be þære eæ, &

 896.11. & hie ða swa dydon. worhton ða tu geweorc. on twa

 896.12. Þa hie ða þæt geweorc furþum ongunnen hæfdon,

 896.14. Þa forleton hie hie, & eodon ofer land þæt hie

 896.16. Þa rad seo fird west æfter þæm herige, & þa

 896.19. & þa Deniscan hæfdon hira wif befæst innan East

 897.1. Ða þæs on sumera on ðysum gere tofor se here, sum

 897.5. Næfde se here, Godes þonces. Angelcyn ealles for

 897.6. Ac hie wæron micle swiþor gebrocede on þæm þrim

 897.10. Þara wæs sum Swiðulf biscop on Hrofesceastre, &

 897.17. Þy ilcan geare drehton þa hergas on East Englum &

 897.20. Þa het ælfred cyng timbran lang scipu ongen ða
æscas; þa wæron fulneah tu swa lange swa þa oðru. sume hæfdon
<foreign>lx</foreign> ara. sume ma.
 897.22. Þa wæron ægðer ge swiftran ge unwealtran, ge eac
hieran þonne þa oðru. næron nawðer ne on Fresisc gescæpene ne on
Denisc, bute swa him selfum ðuhte þæt hie nytwyrðoste beon meahten.
 897.26. Þa æt sumum cirre þæs ilcan geares comon þær
sex scipu to Wiht, & þær mycel yfel gedydon, ægðer ge on Defenum
ge welhwær be ðæm sæ riman.
 897.28. Þa het se cyng faran mid nigonum to þara niwena scipa,
& forforon him þone muðan foran on utermere;
 897.30. Þa foron hie mid þrim scipum ut ongen hie, & þreo
stodon æt ufeweardum þæm muðan on drygum, wæron þa men uppe on
londe of agane, þa gefengon hie þara þreora scipa tu æt ðæm
muðan uteweardum, & þa men ofslogon, & þæt an oðwand;
 897.34. On þæm wæron eac þa men ofslægene buton
fifum.
 897.35. Þa comon forðy on weg ðe ðara oþerra scipu
asæton, þa wurdon eac swiðe uneðelice aseten.
 897.37. Þreo asæton on ða healfe þæs deopes ðe ða
Deniscan scipu aseten wæron, & þa oðru eall on oþre healfe,
þæt hira ne mehte nan to oðrum.
 897.39. Ac ða þæt wæter wæs ahebbad fela furlanga from
þæm scipu. þa eodan ða Deniscan from þæm þrim scipum to
þæm oðrum þrim þe on hira healfe beebbade wæron, & hie þa
þær gefuhton.

ær flod to, ær þa Cristnan mehten hira utascufan, & hie forðy ut
oðreowon;
 897.48. Þa wæron hie to þæm gesargode. þæt hie ne
mehton Suð Seaxna lond utan berowan, ac hira þær tu sæ on lond
wearp.

he ær beæftan læfde, and þone æþeling on þære byrig
gemettun þær se cing ofslegen læg, and hi him þa gatu to belocen
hæfdon, and hi þærto eodon.

him þæs rices uþon, and him cyðdon þæt hira magas him mid
wæron þa þe him fram noldon, and þa cwædon hi þæt him nænig
mæg leofra nære ðonne hira hlaford and hi næfre his banan folgian
noldon.

þe ær mid þam cinge wæron.

þe eowre geferan þe mid þam cinge ofslegene wæron.

his feorh generode, and þeah he wæs oft gewundod.

 894.1. On ðys gere, þæt wæs embe <foreign>xii</foreign> monað þæs

 894.14. Ne com se here oftor eall ute of ðam setum þonne tuwa,

 894.44. And Hæstenes wif and his <foreign>ii</foreign> suna man brohte to þam

 894.49. Ac sona swa hi to Beamfleote comon and þæt geweorc

 894.55. Ða he wið þone here ðær west abysgod wæs and

 894.59. Þa gegadrode æþered ealdormann and æðelelm

 894.63. Þa hi ða gegadrode wæron ealle, ða offoron hi

 894.66. Ða hi þa ðær fela wucena sæton on twa healfa

 894.69. Þa eodon hi ut to þam mannum þe on easthealfe

 894.71. And þær wearð Ordeh cinges þegn ofslegen, and eac

 894.74. Þa hi ða on Eastsexe comon to hyra geweorce and to hira
scypum, þa gegadrode seo laf eft of Eastenglum and of Norðhymbrum micelne
here onforan winter, and befæstan hyra wif and hyra scipu and hyra feoh on
Eastenglum, and foron anstreces dæges and nihtes þæt hi gedydon on anre
westre ceastre on Wirhealum seo is Liegecester gehaten.
 894.79. Þa ne mihte seo fyrd hi na hindan offaran ær hi
wæron inne on þam geweorce, besæton ðeah þæt geweorc sume <foreign>ii</foreign>
dagas, and genamon ceapes eall þæt ðær butan wæs, and þa menn

 1006.39. Þa sende se cyning to þam here and him cyðan het
þæt he wolde þæt him grið betweonan beon sceolde and him mon gafol
gulde and metsunge syllan sceolde, and hi ða ealle þæt underfengon, and
him ametsode þa geond Angelcyn.
 1007.1. Her on ðissum geare wæs þæt gafol gelæst þam
here, þæt wæs <foreign>xxxvi</foreign> þusend punda.
 1007.2. On þissum geare eac wæs Eadric geset to ealdormen
geond Myrcnarice.
 1008.1. Her bebead se cyng þæt man sceolde ofer eall Angelcyn
scypu fæstlice wyrcan, þæt is ðonne of þrim hund hidum and of tynum
ænne scegð and of <foreign>vii</foreign> hidum helm and byrnan.
 1009.1. Her on þissum geare wurdan þa scypu gearwe ðe we
ær ymbbe spræcon, and hiora wæs swa feala swa næfre ær, þæs
ðe us bec secgað, on Angelcynne ne gewurdon on nanes cyninges dæge, and
hi man ða ealle togædere ferode to Sandwic, and ðær sceoldan licgan
and þisne eard healdan wið ælcne uthere.
 1009.5. Ac we ða gyt næfdon þa gesælða ne þone
wyrðscype þæt seo scypfyrd nyt wære þissum earde þe ma ðe heo
ofter ær wæs.
 1009.7. Þa gewearð hit on þissum ylcan timan oþþe lytle
ær þæt Brihtric, Eadrices broðor ealdormannes, forwregde Wulfnoð
cild to þam cyninge, and he þa ut gewende and him þa to aspeon þæt
he hæfde <foreign>xx</foreign> scypa and he ða heregode æghwær be ðam suðriman
and ælc yfel worhton.
 1009.11. Þa cydde man into þære scypfyrde þæt man hi
eaðe befaran mihte, gif man embe wære.
 1009.12. Þa genam se Brihtric him to hundeahtatig scypa and
ðohte þæt he him micles wordes wyrcan sceolde, þæt he Wulfnoð
cucone oþþe deadne begytan sceolde.
 1009.15. Ac þa hi ðiderwerd wæron, þa com him swilc wind
ongean swilc nan man ær ne gemunde, and þa scypo ða ealle tobeot and
toþærsc and on land awearp, and com se Wulfnoð sona and þa scypo
forbærnde.
 1009.18. Þa ðis þus cuð wæs to þam oþerum scipum
þær se cyng wæs, hu ða oþre geferdon, hit wæs þa swilc hit
eall rædleas wære, and ferde se cyning him ham and þa ealdormen and
ða heahwitan and forleton þa scipo ðus leohtlice.
 1009.21. And þæt folc þa þæt on ðam scipon wæron
fercodon eft to Lundene and leton ealles þeodscypes geswinc ðus leohtlice
forwurðan.
 1009.23. And næs se sige na betere þe eal Angelcyn to hopode.
 1009.24. Ða þeos scypfyrd þus geendod wæs, þa com sona
æfter lafmæssan se ungemætlica unfriðhere þe we heton ðurkilles
here to Sandwic, and sona wendon hiora fore to Cantwarebyrig and ða buruh
raðe geeodon, gif hi ðe hraðor to him friðes ne gyrndon, and ealle
Eastcentingas frið wið þone here genamon and him gesealdon <foreign>iii</foreign> þusend
pund.
 1009.29. And se here þa sona æfter ðam wende oþ he com to
Wihtlande, and þær æghwær on Suðsexum and on Hamtunscire and eac
on Bearrocscire heregodon and bærndon swa hiora gewuna is.
 1009.32. Þa het se cyning abannan ut ealne þeodscype þæt
man on ælce healfe wið hi healdan sceolde, ac þeahhwæðere hi ferdon
loca hu hi woldon.
 1009.34. Þa sume siðe hæfde se cyning hi forne forgan mid
ealre fyrde, þa hi to scypon woldan, and eal folc gearu wæs him on to
fonne, ac hit wæs þa ðuruh Eadric ealdorman gelet swa hit gyt æfre
wæs.
 1009.38. Ða æfter Sanctus Martines mæssan þa ferdon hi
eft agen to Cent and namon him wintersetl on Temesan and lifdon him of
Eastseaxum and of ðam scirum þe ðær nexð wæron on twam healfum
Temese, and oft hi on þa buruh Lundene fuhton, ac si Gode lof þæt heo
gyt gesund stent, and hi þær æfre yfel geferdon.
 1009.42. And þa æfter middan wintra ða namon hi ænne
upgang/ ut þuruh Ciltern and swa to Oxenaforda, and ða buruh forbærndon,
and namon hit ða on twa healfa Temese to scypeweard.
 1009.45. Þa gewarnode man hi þæt ðær wæs fyrd
gegaderod æt Lundene ongean hi, wendon him ða ofer æt Stane and ðus
ferdon ealne þone winter, and þæt lencten wæron him on Cent and
betton hiora scypu.
 1010.1. Her on ðissum geare com se foresprecena here ofer Eastron
to Eastenglum and wendon up æt Gypeswic and eodon anreces þær hi
geacsodon Ulfcytel mid his fyrde, þis wæs on ðam dæge <foreign>Prima Ascensio
Domini</foreign>, and þa sona flugon Eastengle, þa stod Grantabricscir fæstlice
ongean.
 1010.5. Þær wæs ofslagen æþelstan ðæs cynges
aþum and Oswig and his sunu and Wulfric Leofwines sunu and Eadwig æfices
broðor and feala oþera godra þegna and folces ungerim.
 1010.8. Þone fleam ærest astealde þurcytel Myranheafod, and
þa Denan ahton wælstowe geweald and þone eard <foreign>iii</foreign> monþas hergodon
and bærndon.
 1010.11. Ge fyrðon on þa wildan fennas hi ferdon, and men and
yrfe hi slogon and bærndon geond þa fennas, and þeodford hi
forbærndon and Grantabricge, and syððan wendon eft suðwerd into
Temese, and ridan þa gehorsedan men ongean þa scipo.
 1010.14. And siððan eft hrædlice wendon westweard on
Oxenafordscire, and þanon on Buccingahamscire, and swa andlang Usan oð hi
comon to Bedeforda, and swa forð oþ Temesanford, and a bærndon swa hi
geferdon.
 1010.18. Wendon þa eft to scipon mid hiora herehyðe and þonne
hi to scipon ferdon, þonne sceolde fyrd ut eft ongean þæt hi up woldan,
þonne ferde seo fyrd ham.
 1010.20. And þonne hi wæron be easton, þonne heold man fyrde
be westan, and þonne hi wæron be suðan, þonne wæs ure fyrd be
norðan.
 1010.22. Þonne bead man eallan witan to cynge, and man sceolde
þonne rædan hu man þisne eard werian sceolde, ac, þeah mon þonne
hwæt rædde, þæt ne stod furðon ænne monað.
 1010.24. Æt nextan næs nan heafodman þæt fyrde gaderian
wolde, ac ælc fleah swa he mæst mihte, ne furðon nan scir nolde oþre
gelæstan æt nextan.
 1010.27. Ða ætforan Sanctus Andreas mæssan þa com se here
to Hamtune and þæt port sona forbærndon, and ðær namon abutan swa
mycel swa hi sylfe woldon, and þanon wendon ofer Temese into Wesseaxum, and
swa wið Caneganmersces and þæt eall forbærndon.
 1010.31. Þa hi swa feor gegan hæfdon swa hi ða woldan, comon
þa to ðam middan wintra to hiora scipon.
 1011.1. Her on þissum geare sende se cyning and his witan to
ðam here and gyrndon friðes, and him gafol and metsunge beheton wið þam
ðe hi hiora hergunge geswicon.
 1011.3. Hi hæfdon þa ofergan, <foreign>i</foreign> Eastengle and <foreign>ii</foreign> Eastsexe
and <foreign>iii</foreign> Middelsexe and <foreign>iiii</foreign> Oxenafordscire and <foreign>v</foreign> Grantabricscire and <foreign>vi</foreign>
Heortfordscire and <foreign>vii</foreign> Buccingahamscire and <foreign>viii</foreign> Bedefordscire and <foreign>ix</foreign>
healfe Huntadunscire and micel <foreign>x</foreign> on Hamtunscire, and be suþan Temese ealle
Kentingas and Suðsexe and Hæstingas and Suðrige and Bearrocscire and
Hamtunscire and micel on Wiltunscire.
 1011.10. Ealle þas ungesælða us gelumpon þuruh unrædas
þæt man nolde him a timan gafol beodon oþþe wið gefeohtan, ac
þonne hi mæst to yfele gedon hæfdon, þonne nam mon frið and grið
wið hi, and naþelæs, for eallum þissum griðe and gafole, hi ferdon
æghweder flocmælum and heregodon ure earme folc, and hi rypton and
slogon.
 1011.15. And þa on ðissum geare betweox Natiuitas Sancte
Marie and Sancte Michaeles mæssan hi ymbsæton Cantwareburuh, and hi
into comon þuruh syruwrencas, forðan ælmær hi becyrde, þe se
arcebisceop ælfeah ær generede æt his life.
 1011.18. And hi þær ða genaman þone arcebisceop Ælfeah
and Ælfweard cynges gerefan and Leofrune <foreign>abbatissam</foreign> and Godwine bisceop,
and Ælfmær abbud hi leton aweg.
 1011.21. And hi ðær genamon inne ealle þa gehadodan men and
weras and wif, þæt wæs unasecgendlic ænigum men hu micel þæs
folces wæs, and on þære byrig syþþan wæron swa lange swa hi
woldon.
 1011.23. And hi ða hæfdon þa buruh ealle asmeade, wendon him
þa to scypan and læddon þone arcebisceop mid him.
 1011.26. Wæs ða ræpling, se ðe ær wæs heafod
Angelkynnes and Cristendomes.
 1011.28. Þær man mihte ða geseon yrmðe þær man oft
ær geseah blisse on þære earman byrig þanon com ærest Cristendom
and blis for Gode and for worulde.
 1011.32. And hi hæfdon þone arcebisceop mid him swa lange oð
þæne timan þe hi hine gemartiredon.
 1012.1. Her on þissum geare com Eadric ealdorman and ealle þa
yldestan witan, gehadode and læwede, Angelcynnes to Lundenbyrig toforan
þam Eastron, þa wæs Easterdæg on þam <foreign>datarum Idus Aprilis</foreign>.
 1012.4. And hi ðær þa swa lange wæron oþ þæt gafol
eal gelæst wæs ofer ða Eastron, þæt wæs ehta and feowertig
þusend punda.
 1012.5. Ða on þæne Sæternes dæg wearð þa se here
swyðe astyred angean þone bisceop, forþam ðe he nolde him nan feoh
behaten, ac he forbead þæt man nanþing wið him syllan ne moste.
 1012.8. Wæron hi eac swyþe druncene, forðam þær wæs
broht win suðan.
 1012.9. Genamon þa ðone bisceop, læddon hine to hiora
hustinge on ðone Sunnan æfen <foreign>octabas Pasce</foreign>, þa wæs <foreign>xiii Kalendas
Maius</foreign>, and hine þær ða bysmorlice acwylmdon, oftorfedon mid banum and
mid hryþera heafdum, and sloh hine ða an hiora mid anre æxe yre on
þæt heafod, þæt mid þam dynte he nyþer asah, and his halige blod
on þa eorðan feol, and his haligan sawle to Godes rice asende.
 1012.15. And mon þone lichaman on mergen ferode to Lundene, and
þa bisceopas Eadnoþ and ælfun and seo buruhwaru hine underfengon mid
ealre arwurðnysse and hine bebyrigdon on Sancte Paules mynstre, and þær
nu God sutelað þæs halgan martires mihta.
 1012.19. Ða þæt gafol gelæst wæs and frið aþas
asworene wæron, þa toferde se here wide swa he ær gegaderod wæs.
 1012.20. Ða bugon to þam cynge of ðam here fif and feowertig
scypa, and him beheton þæt hi woldon þysne eard healdan, and he hi fedan
sceolde and scrydon.
 1013.1. On ðam æftran geare þe se arcebisceop wæs
gemartyrod se cyning gesette Lyfinc bisceop to Cantwarabyrig to ðam
arcestole.
 1013.3. And on þissum ylcan geare toforan þam monðe Augustus
com Swegen cyning mid his flotan to Sandwic, and wende þa swiðe raðe
abutan Eastenglum into Humbra muþan, and swa upweard andlang Trentan oð he
com to Genesburuh.
 1013.6. And þa sona beah Uhtred eorl and ealle Norðhymbre to
him and eal þæt folc on Lindesige, and siððan þæt folc into
Fifburhingum, and raðe þæs eall be norðan Wæclinga stræte, and
him man sealde gislas of ælcere scire.
 1013.9. Syððan he undergeat þæt eall folc him to gebogen
wæs, þa bead he þæt man sceolde his here mettian and horsian, and he
ða wende syþþan suðweard mid fulre fyrde and betæhte þa scipu and
ða gislas Cnute his suna.
 1013.12. And syððan he com ofer Wæclinga stræte, worhton
þæt mæste yfel þæt ænig here don mihte.
 1013.14. Wende þa to Oxenaforda, and seo buruhwaru sona beah and
gislude, and þanon to Winceastre, and hi þæt ylce dydon.
 1013.16. Wende þa þanon eastwerd to Lundene, and mycel his
folces adrang on Temese forðam þe hi nanre bricge ne cepton.
 1013.17. Þa he to ðære byrig com, þa nolde seo buruhwaru
bugan, ac heoldan mid fullan wige ongean, forðan þær wæs inge se cyng
æþelred and þurcyl mid him.
 1013.20. Þa wende Swegen cyng þanon to Wealingaforda and swa
ofer Temese westweard to Baþan and sæt ðær mid his fyrde.
 1013.21. And com æþelmær ealdorman þyder and þa
westernan þegenas mid him, and bugon ealle to Swegene and hi gisludon.
 1013.23. Þa he ðus gefaren hæfde, wende þa norðweard to
his scipum and eal þeodscype hine hæfde þa for fulne cyng, and seo
buruhwaru æfter ðam on Lundene beah and gislude, forðon hi ondredon
þæt he hi fordon wolde.
 1013.26. Þa bead Swegen ful gyld and metsunge to his here ðone
winter, and þurkyl bead þæt ylce to ðam here þe læg æt
Grenawic, and for eallon þam hi heregodon swa oft swa hi woldon.
 1013.29. Þa ne dohte naðer þisse leode ne suðan ne
norðan.
 1013.30. Þa wæs se cyning æþelred sume hwile mid þam
flotan þe on Temese læg, and seo hlæfdige gewende þa ofer sæ to
hire breðer Ricarde and ælfsige abbud of Buruh mid hire, and se cyning
sende ælfun bisceop mid þam æþelingum Eadwerde and ælfrede ofer
sæ þæt he hi bewitan sceolde.
 1013.34. And se cyning gewende þa fram ðam flotan to þam
middan wintra to Wihtlande, and wæs ðær þa tid, and æfter
þære tide wende ofer ða sæ to Ricarde and wæs ðær mid him
oþ þone byre þæt Swegen wearð dead.
 1014.1. Her on þissum geare Swegen geendode his dagas to
candelmæssan <foreign>iii Nonas Februarius</foreign>, and se flota þa eal gecuron Cnut to
cyninge.
 1014.3. Þa geræddon þa witan ealle þe on Englalande
wæron, gehadode and læwede, þæt man æfter þam cyninge
æþelrede sende, and cwædon þæt him nan hlaford leofra nære
þonne hiora gecynda hlaford gif he hi rihtlicor healdan wolde þonne he
ær dyde.
 1014.6. Þa sende se cyning his sunu Eadweard hider mid his
ærenddracum and het gretan ealne his leodscype, and cwæð þæt he
him hold hlaford beon wolde and ælc þæra ðinga betan þe hi ealle
ascunudon, and ælc þara ðinga forgyfen beon sceolde þe him gedon
oþþe gecweden wære, wið þam ðe hi ealle anrædlice butan
swicdome to him gecyrdon.
 1014.11. And man þa fulne freondscipe gefæstnode mid worde and
mid wedde on ægþre healfe, and æfre ælcne Deniscne cyng utlah of
Englalande gecwædon.
 1014.14. Þa com Æþelred cyning innon ðam lengtene ham to
his agenre þeode, and he glædlice fram him eallum onfangen wæs.
 1014.15. Þa syððan Swegen dead wæs, sæt Cnut mid his
here on Genesburuh oþ þa Eastron, and gewearð him and þam folce on
Lindesige anes þæt hi hine horsian woldon and syþþan ealle
ætgædere faran and heregian.
 1014.18. Ða com se cyning æþelred mid fulre fyrde þyder,
ær hi gearwe wæron, to Lindesige, and man þa hergode and bærnde and
sloh eal þæt mancynn þæt man ræcan mihte.
 1014.21. And Cnut gewende him aweig ut mid his flotan, and wearð
þæt earme folc þus beswicen ðuruh hine, and wende þa suðweard oþ
he com to Sandwic, and let don up þær ða gislas þe his fæder
gesealde wæron and cearf of hiora handa and earan and nosa.
 1014.25. And buton eallum þissum yfelum se cyng het gyldan þam
here ðe on Grenawic læig <foreign>xxi</foreign> þusend pund.
 1014.26. And on þissum geare on Sancte Michaeles mæsseæfen
com þæt mycle sæflod gynd wide þysne eard and arn swa feor up swa
næfre ær ne dyde and adrencte feala tuna and mancynnes unarimedlic
getel.
 1015.1. Her on þissum geare wæs þæt mycle gemot on
Oxenaforda, and ðær Eadric ealdorman beswac Siferð and Morcore, þa
yldestan þegenas into Seofonburgum, bepæhte hi into his bure and hi man
þærinne ofsloh ungerisenlice.
 1015.4. And se cyng þa genam ealle hiora æhta and het niman
Siferðes lafe and gebringan hi binnan Ealdelmesbyrig.
 1015.6. Þa æfter lytlum fæce ferde Eadmund æþelinc to
and genam þæt wif ofer ðæs cynges gewil and hæfde him to wife.
 1015.7. Ða toforan Natiuitas Sancte Marie ferde se
æþeling þanon westan norð into Fifburgum and gerad sona ealle
Sigeferðes are and Morcores, and þæt folc eal him to beah.
 1015.11. And ða on þam ilcan timan com Cnut cyng to Sandwic and
wende þa sona abutan Centland into Westseaxum oð he com to From muðan and
heregode þa on Dorsætum and on Wiltunscire and on Sumersætum.
 1015.14. Þa læig se cyng seoc æt Cosham.
 1015.14. Þa gadarade Eadric ealdorman fyrde and se æþeling
Eadmund be norðan.
 1015.15. Þa hi togædere comon, ða wolde se ealdorman
beswican þone æþeling, and hi toferdon þa butan gefeohte forðan and
rymdon heora feondum.
 1015.17. And Eadric ealdorman aspeon þa feowerti scipa fram ðam
cinge and beah ða to Cnute, and Westsexe bugon and gislodon and horsodon
þone here, and he wæs þær ða oþ midne winter.
 1016.1. Her on þissum geare com Cnut mid his here and Eadric
ealdorman mid him ofer Temese into Myrcum æt Cregelade, and wendon þa to
Wærincwicscire innan ðære middan wintres tide and heregodon and
bærndon and slogon eal þæt hi to comon.
 1016.4. Ða ongan se æþeling Eadmund to gaderigenne fyrde.
 1016.5. Þa seo fyrd gesomnod wæs, ða ne onhagode heom
ðarto buton þæt wære þæt se cyng ðær mid wære and hi
hæfdon þære burhware fultum of Lundene.
 1016.7. Geswicon ða þære fyrdinge, and ferde him ælc man
ham.
 1016.8. Þa æfter ðære tide þa bead man eft fyrde be
fullan wite þæt ælc man ðe fere wære forðgewende, and man sende
to ðam cynge to Lundene and bæd hine þæt he come ongean þa fyrde
mid þam fultume ðe he gegaderian mihte.
 1016.12. Þa hi ealle tosomne comon, þa ne beheold hit nanðinc
þe ma ðe hit oftor ær dyde.
 1016.13. Þa cydde man þam cynge þæt hine man beswican
wolde þa þe him on fultume beon sceoldon.
 1016.14. Forlet ða þa fyrde and cyrde him eft to Lundene.
 1016.16. Ða rad se æþeling Eadmund to Norðhymbron to
Uhtrede eorle, and wende ælc mon þæt hi woldon fyrde somnian ongean
Cnut cyng.
 1016.18. Þa fyrdedon hi into Stæffordscire and into
Scrobsæton and to Legceastre, and hi heregodon on heora healfe and Cnut on
his healfe.
 1016.20. Wende him ut þuruh Buccingahamscire into Bedanfordscire,
and ðanon to Huntadunscire, swa into Hamtunscire andlang fennes to Stanforda,
and þa into Lindcolnescire, þanon ða to Snotingahamscire, and swa to
Norðhymbran to Eoferwic weard.
 1016.23. Ða Uhtred geahsode þis, ða forlet he his hergunge
and efste norðweard and beah ða for nyde and ealle Norðhymbro mid him,
and he gislode, and hine mon ðeahhwæþere ofsloh ðuruh Eadrices ræd
ealdormannes, and þurcytel Nafenan sunu mid him.
 1016.27. And þa æfter ðam gesette se cyng Yric into
Norðhymbron him to eorle ealswa Uhtred wæs, and syððan wende him
suðwerd oþres weges eal be westan and com þa eal se here toforan þam
Eastron to scypon.
 1016.30. And se æþeling Eadmund gewende to Lundene to his
fæder, and ða æfter Eastron wende se cyng Cnut mid eallon his scipon to
Lunden werd.
 1016.33. Þa gelamp hit þæt se cyning Æþelred
forðferde ær þa scypo comon.
 1016.34. He geendode his dagas on Sancte Georgius mæssedæig,
and he geheold his rice mid myclum geswince and earfoðnessum þa hwile ðe
his lif wæs.
 1016.36. And þa æfter his ende ealle ða witan þa on
Lundene wæron and seo burhwaru gecuron Eadmund to cyninge, and he his rice
heardlice werode þa hwile þe his tima wæs.
 1016.39. Þa comon ða scypo to Grenawic to þam gangdagum, and
hi binnon lytlan fæce gewendon to Lundene, and hi ða dulfon ane mycle dic
on suðhealfe and drogon hiora scypo on westhealfe þære bricge and
bedicodon þa syððan þa buruh uton þæt nan man ne mihte ne ing ne
ut, and hi oft rædlice on þa buruh fuhton, ac hi him heardlice
wiðstodon.
 1016.44. Þa wæs Eadmund cyng ær ðam gewend ut and gerad
þa Westsexon, and him beah eal folc to, and raðe æfter þam he gefeaht
wið þone here æt Peonnan wið Gillingaham, and oþer gefeoht he

feoll on ægðre healfe, and ða heras him sylfe toeodan, on þam gefeohte
wæs Eadric ealdorman and ælmær dyrling þam here on fultume ongean
Eadmung kyning.
 1016.51. And þa gegaderede he þryddan siðe fyrde, and ferde
to Lundene eal be norðan Temese and swa ut þuruh Clæighangran, and þa
buruhwaru ahredde and þæne here geflymde to hiora scypon.
 1016.53. And þa ðæs ymbe twa niht gewende se cyning ofer
æt Bregentforda and þa wið þone here gefeaht and hine geflymde, and
þær adranc mycel wæl Englisces folces for hiora agenre gymeleaste, þa
ðe ferdon beforan þære fyrde and woldan fon feng.
 1016.57. And se cyning æfter þam gewende to Westseaxum and his
fyrde samnode.
 1016.58. Þa gewende se here sona to Lundene and ða buruh utan
embsæt and hyre stearclice onfeaht ægðer ge be wætere ge be lande,
ac se ælmihtiga God hi ahredde.
 1016.61. Se here gewende þa æfter þam fram Lundene mid hyra
scypum into Arewan, and ðær up foron and ferdon on Myrcan and slogon and
bærndon swa hwæt swa hi oferforan, swa hira gewuna is, and him metes
tilodon, and hi drifon ægþer ge scipu ge hyra drafa into Medwæge.
 1016.65. Þa gesamnode Eadmund cyng feorðan siðe ealle his
fyrde and ferde ofer Temese æt Brentforda and ferde innon Kent, and se here
him fleah beforan mid hiora horsum into Sceapige, and se cyning ofsloh heora
swa fela swa he offaran mihte, and Eadric ealdorman gewende þa ðone cyning
ongean æt Egelesforda, næs nan mara unræd geræd þonne se wæs.
 1016.71. Se here gewende eft up on Eastsexan and ferde into Myrcum
and fordyde eall þæt he oforferde.
 1016.72. Þa se cyning geahsode þæt se here uppe wæs, þa
gesomnode he fiftan siðe ealle Engla þeode and ferde him æt hindan and
offerde hi on Eastsexum æt þære dune þe man hæt Assandun, and
þar togædere heardlice fengon.
 1016.75. Þa dyde Eadric ealdorman swa swa he ær oftor dyde,
astealde þæne fleam ærest mid Magesæton, and aswac swa his
cynehlaforde and ealre Angelcynnes þeode.
 1016.78. Þær ahte Cnut sige and gefeht him ealle Engla
þeode.

 1016.83. Þa æfter þissum gefeohte gewende Cnut kyninge up

 1052.12. Þa cwædon ealle þæt hi mid him woldon licgan and
lybban.
 1052.13. Ða geaxedon þæt lið þæt on Sandwic læg
embe Godwines fare, setton þa æfter, and he heom ætbærst and him
sylfan gebearh þær þær he þa mihte, and þæt lið wende agen
to Sandwic and swa hamwerd to Lundenbyrig.
 1052.16. Ða þa Godwine geaxode þæt þæt lið þe on
Sandwic læg wæs ham gewend, þa for he eft ongean to Wiht, and þær
abutan be þam særiman swa lange læg þæt hig comon togædere,
Harold eorl his sunu and he, and hi na mycelne hearm ne dydon syððan hig
togædere comon buton þæt heo metsunge namon, ac speonnon heom eall
þæt landfolc to be ðam særiman and eac up on lande, and hig foron
towerd Sandwic, and læson æfre forð mid heom ealle þa butsecarlas
þe heo gemetton, and comon þa to Sandwic mid geotendan here.
 1052.24. Ða Eadwerd cyng þæt geaxode, þa sende he up
æfter maran fultume, ac hi comon swyðe late.
 1052.26. And Godwine sah him æfre towerd Lundenes mid his liðe
þæt he com to Suðgeweorce, and þær onbad sume hwile oð þæt
flod up eode.
 1052.28. On þam fyrste he eac gefadode wið þa burhware,
þæt hi woldon mæst ealle þæt þæt he wolde.
 1052.29. Þa he hæfde ealle his fare gerecenod, þa com se
flod, and hig brudon up ða sona heora ancran and heoldon þurh þa brycge
be ðam syðlande.
 1052.31. And seo landfyrd com ufenon and trymedon hig be þam
strande, and hi hwemdon þa mid þam scypon wið þæs norðlandes,
swylce hig woldon þæs cynges scipa abutan betrymman.
 1052.34. Se cyng hæfde eac mycele landfyrde on his healfe
toeacan his scypmannum, ac hit wæs heom mæst eallon lað þæt hig
sceoldon fohtan wið heora agenes cynnes mannum, forþan þar wæs lyt
elles þe aht mycel myhton buton Englisce men on ægþer healfe, and eac
hig noldon þæt utlendiscum þeodum wære þes eard þurh þæt
þe swiðor gerymed þe hi heom sylfe ælc oðerne forfore.
 1052.39. Geræddon þa þæt man sende wise men betweonan and
setton grið on ægðre healfe, and Godwine for upp and Harold his sunu and
heora lið swa mycel swa heom þa geþuhte.
 1052.42. And wæs þa witenagemot, and man sealde Godwine
clæne his eorldom swa full and swa forð swa he fyrmest ahte, and his sunum
eallswa eall þæt hi ær ahten, and his wife and his dehter swa ful and
swa forð swa hi ær ahton.
 1052.45. And hi gefæstnodon heom þa fulne freondscipe
betweonan and eallum folce gode lage beheton.
 1052.46. And geutlageden þa ealle Frencisce men þe ær unlage
rærdon and undom demdon, and unræd ræddon into ðissum earde buton
swa feala swa hig geræddon þæt þam cynge gelicode mid him to
hæbbenne þe him getreowe wæron and eallum his folce.
 1052.50. And Rodbeard bisceop and Willem bisceop and Ulf bisceop
uneaðe ætburstan mid þam Frenciscum mannum þe heom mid wæron, and
swa ofer sæ becomon.
 1052.52. And Godwine eorl and Harold and seo cwen sæton on heora
are.
 1052.54. Swegen for æror to Hierusalem of Bricge, and wearð
hamweard dead æt Constantinopolim to Michaheles mæsse.
 1052.55. Ðæt wæs on þone Monandæg æfter Sancta
Marian mæsse þæt Godwine mid his scipum to Suðgeweorce becom, and
þæs on merigen on þone Tiwesdæg hi gewurdon sehte, swa hit her
beforan stent.
 1052.58. Godwine þa gesiclode hraðe þæs þe he up com,
and eft gewyrpte, ac he dyde ealles to lytle dædbote of þære Godes are
þe he hæfde of manegum halgum stowum.
 1052.60. On þam ylcan geare com se stranga wind on Thomas
mæsseniht and gehwær mycelne hearm dyde.
 1052.62. Eac man sloh Hris þæs Welscan cynges broþer.
 1053.1. On þysum geare wæs se cyning on Winceastre on Eastran
and Godwine eorl mid him and Harold eorl his sunu and Tostig.
 1053.3. Ða on oðran Easterdæge sæt he mid ðam cynincge
æt gereorde, þa færinga sah he niðer wið þæs fotsetles,
spræce benumen and ealre his mihte, and hine man ða bræd into ðæs
kinges bure, and ðohtan þæt hit ofergan sceolde, ac hit næs na swa,
ac þurhwunode swa unspecende and mihteleas forð oð þone ðunresdæg,
and ða his lif alet, and he lið þær binnan Ealdan mynstre.
 1053.8. And his sunu Harald feng to his eorldome, and let of ðan
þe he ær hæfde, and ælfgar fengc ðærto.
 1053.11. Ðæs ylcan geares gefor Wulfsie bisceop on Licedfelda,
and Leofwine abbud on Cofantreo feng to ðam bisceoprice, and ægelward
abbud on Glæstingabyrig gefor, and Godwine abbud on Wincelcumbe.
 1053.14. Eac Wylsce menn geslogan mycelne dæl Englisces folces
ðæra weardmanna wið Wæstbyrig.
 1053.16. On ðisson geare næs nan arcebisceop on ðissan
lande, butan Stigand bisceop heold þæt bisceoprice on Cantwarabyrig on
Cristes cyrcean and Kynsige on Eoforwic, and Leofwine and Wulfwi foran ofer
sæ and leton hig hadian þær to bisceopum, se Wulfwi feng to ðam
biscoprice þe Ulf hæfde be him libbendum and of adræfdum.
 1054.1. Her for Siward eorl mid mycclum here into Scotlande and
mycel wæl of Scottum gesloh and hig aflymde, and se cing ætbærst.
 1054.2. Eac feoll mycel on his healfe ægðer ge Densce ge
Englisce and eac his agen sunu.
 1054.3. Ðæs ylcan geares man halgode þæt mynster on
Eofeshamme on <foreign>vi Idus Octobris</foreign>.
 1054.5. On ðam ylcan geare ferde Ealdred bisceop suð ofer sæ
into Sexlande, and wearð þær mid mycelre arwurðnesse underfangen.
 1054.6. Þy ylcan geare swealt Osgod Clapa færinga swa swa he
on his reste læt.
 1055.1. On þysum geare forðferde Siward eorl on Eoforwic, and
his lic lið binnan þam mynstre æt Galmanho þe he sylf æt getimbrade
Gode to lofe and eallum his halgum.
 1055.3. Ða ðæræfter binnan lyttlan fyrste wæs
witenagemot on Lundene, and man geutlagode þa ælfgar eorl, Leofrices sunu
eorles, butan ælcan gylte, and he gewende ða to Irlande and begeat him
ðær lið, þæt wæs <foreign>xviii</foreign> scipa butan his agenan.
 1055.7. And wendan ða to Brytlande to Griffine cinge mid þam
werede, and he hine underfeng on his griðe, and hig gegaderadan ða mycle
fyrde mid ðam Yriscan mannan and mid Walkynne.
 1055.10. And Rawulf eorl gaderade mycele fyrde agean to
Herefordport, and hi sohtan hi ðær, ac ær þær wære ænig
spere gescoten, ær fleah ðæt Englisce folc, forðan þe hig wæran
on horsan, and man sloh ðær mycel wæl, abutan feower hund manna
oððe fife, and hig nænne agean.
 1055.14. And hig gewendan ða to ðam porte and ðæt
forbærndan, and þæt mære mynster ðe æþelstan se arwurða
biscop ær let getimbrian, þæt hig beryptan and bereafodan æt
haligdome and æt hreaue and æt eallon ðingan, and þæt folc slogan
and sume onweg læddan.
 1055.18. Ða gaderade man fyrde geond eall Englaland swyðe neah,
and hig comon to Gleaweceastre, and wendan swa unfeorr ut on Wealas and
þær lagon sume hwile, and Harald eorl let dician ða dic abutan þæt
port þa hwile.
 1055.21. Þa on ðam þa spæc man to friðe, and Harald eorl
and ða ðe mid him wæron coman to Bylgeslege, and ðær frið and
freondscipe heom betweonan gefæstnodan, and man geinlagode þa ælfgar
eorl, and man ageaf him eall þæt him wæs ær ofgenumen, and þæt
sciplið gewende to Legeceastre, and ðær abiden heora males þe
ælfgar heom behet.
 1055.26. Se mannslyht wæs on <foreign>ix Kalendas Nouembris</foreign>.
 1055.28. On ðam ylcan geare forðferde Tremerig se Wylsca biscop
sona æfter ðære hergunge, se wæs æþelstanes biscopes gespelia
syððan he unfere wæs.
 1056.1. Her gefor æþelstan se arwurða bisceop on <foreign>iiii Idus
Februarii</foreign>, and his lic lið on Herefordport, and man sette Leofgar to
biscupe, se wæs Haroldes eorles mæssepreost, se werede his kenepas on his
preosthade oð ðæt he wæs biscop.
 1056.4. Se forlet his crisman and his hrode, his gastlican
wæpna, and feng to his spere and to his sweorde æfter his biscuphade, and
swa for to fyrde ongean Griffin þone Wyliscan cing, and hine man ðar ofsloh
and his preostas mid him, and ælfnoð scirgerefan, and manega gode menn
mid heom, and ða oðre ætflugon.
 1056.9. Þis wæs <foreign>viii</foreign> nihton ær middan sumera.
 1056.10. Earfoðlic is to atellanne seo gedrecednes and seo fare
eall and seo fyrdung and þæt geswinc and manna fyll and eac horsa þe
eall Engla here dreah, oð ðæt Leofric eorl com wið and Harald eorl and
Ealdred bisceop, and macedan seht þær betweonan, swa þæt Griffin swor
aðas þæt he wolde beon Eadwarde kinge hold underkingc and unswicigende.
 1056.15. And Ealdred bisceop feng to ðam biscuprice þe Leofgar
hæfde ær <foreign>xi</foreign> wucan and <foreign>iiii</foreign> dagas.
 1056.17. On ðam ylcan geare gefor Cona se casere.
 1056.18. Ðæs geres gefor Odda eorl, and his lic lið on
Perscoran, and he wæs to munece gehadod ær his ende, he gefor on <foreign>ii</foreign>
<foreign>Kalendas Septembres</foreign>.
 1065.1. Her on þissum geare foran to hlafmæssan het Harold
eorl bytlian on Brytlande æt Portascihð, þa þa he hyt gegan hæfde,
and þar mycel god gegaderode, and þohte þone kingc Eadward þar to
habbenne for huntnoþes þingon, and þa hyt eall mæst gegaderod wæs,
þa for Cradoc Griffines sunu to mid eallum þam þe he begytan mihte and
þæt folc mæst eall ofsloh þe þar timbrode and þæt god genam
þe þar gegaderod wæs, and se mannsliht wæs on Sancte Barþolomeus
mæsse dæig.
 1065.9. And þa æfter Michaheles mæssan foran þa þegnas
ealle on Eoferwicscire to Eoferwic, and Tostiges eorles huskarlas þar
ofslogon ealle þa þe hig geaxian mihton and hys gærsuman namon, and
Tostig wæs þa æt Brytfordan mid þam kinge.
 1065.13. And þa wel raðe þaræfter wæs mycel gemot æt
Norðhamtune and swa on Oxenaforda on þon dæig Simonis and Iude, and
wæs Harold eorl þar, and wolde heora seht wyrcan gif he mihte, ac he na
mihte, ac eall hys eorldom hyne anrædlice forsoc and geutlagode and ealle
þa mid hym þe unlage rærdon, forþam þe he rypte God ærost and
ealle þa bestrypte þe he ofer mihte æt life and æt lande.
 1065.19. And hig namon heom þa Morkere to eorle, and Tostig for
þa ofer sæ and hys wif mid him to Baldwines lande, and wintersetl namon
æt Sancte Audomare.
 1065.22. And Eadward kingc com to Westmynstre to þam middan
wintre, and þæt mynster þar let halgian þe he sylf getimbrode Gode to
lofe and Sancte Petre and eallum Godes halgum, and seo circhalgung wæs on
Cildamæssedæig, and he forðferde on Twelftan æfen, and hyne man
bebyrigde on Twelftan Dæig on þam ylcan mynstre swa hyt heræfter
seigð.
 1065.28. And her wearð Harold eac to kynge gehalgod, and he lytle
stillnesse þar on gebad þa hwile þe he rices weold.
 1066.1. On þisum geare com Harold kyng of Eoforwic to
Westmynstre to þam Eastran þe wæron æfter þam middan wintran þe
se kyng forðferde, and wæron þa Eastran on þone dæig <foreign>xvi Kalendas
Mai</foreign>.
 1066.4. Þa wearð geond eall Englaland swylc tacen on heofenum
gesewen swylce nan mann ær ne geseh.
 1066.5. Sume menn cwædon þæt hyt cometa se steorra
wære, þone sume menn hatað þone fexedan steorran, and he æteowde
ærest on þone æfen <foreign>Letania Maiora</foreign>, þæt ys <foreign>viii Kalendas Mai</foreign>,
and swa scean ealle þa <foreign>vii</foreign> niht.
 1066.10. And sona þaræfter com Tostig eorl fram begeondan
sæ into Wiht mid swa myclum liðe swa he begytan mihte, and him man geald
þar æigðer ge feoh ge metsunge, and for þa þanon and hearmas dyde
ægwar be þam særiman þar he to mihte oð þæt he becom to
Sandwic.
 1066.14. Ða cydde man Harolde kynge, þe on Lundene wæs,
þæt Tostig his broðor wæs cumen to Sandwic.
 1066.15. Þa gegadorade he swa mycele scipfyrde and eac landfyrde
swa nan cingc ær her on lande ne gegaderade, forðam þe him wæs to
soðan gesæd þæt Willelm eorll fram Normandige, Eadwardes cingces
mæg, wolde hider cuman and þis land gegan eallswa hit syððan aeode.
 1066.19. Þa Tostig þæt geaxode þæt Harold cing wæs
toward Sandwic, þa for he of Sandwic and nam of þam butsekarlon sume mid
him, sume þances, sume unþances, and gewende þa norð into Humbran and
þær hergode on Lindesege and þær manege gode men ofsloh.
 1066.23. Þa Eadwine eorl and Morkere eorl þæt undergeaton,
þa coman hi þyder and hine of þæm lande adrifon, and he for ða to
Scotlande, and Scotta cynning hine griðede and him to metsunge fylste, and
þær ealne sumor wunode.
 1066.27. Ða com Harold ciningc to Sandwic and þær his
liðes abad, forþam þe hit wæs lang ær hit man gegaderian mihte, and
þa his lið gegaderad wæs, þa for he into Wiht and þær læg
ealne þone sumor and þone hærfest, and man hæfde landfyrde æghwar
be sæ, þeh hit æt þam ende naht ne forstode.
 1066.31. Þa hit wæs to Natiuitas Sancte Marie, þa
wæs manna metsung agan, and hig nan man þar na leng gehealdan ne mihte.
 1066.33. Ða lyfde man mannum ham, and se cyngc rad up, and man
draf þa scypu to Lundene, and manega forwurdon ær hi þyder comon.
 1066.35. Þa ða scypu ham coman, þa com Harold cyning of
Norwegan norð into Tinan on unwaran mid swyðe miclum sciphere and na
lytlan, þæt mihte beon mid ðreom hund scypum oððe ma, and Tostig
eorl him com to mid eallum þam þe he begiten hæfde eallswa hy ær
gesprecen hæfdon and foran þa begen mid eallum ðam liðe andlang Usan
up to Eoferwic ward.
 1066.41. Ða cydde man Harolde cynge be suðan þa he of scipe
cumen wæs, þæt Harold cyng on Norwegan and Tostig eorl wæron
upcumene neh Eoferwic.
 1066.43. Þa for he norðweard dæges and nihtes swa hraðe
swa he his fyrde gegaderian mihte.
 1066.44. Þa ær þam þe se cynning Harold þyder cuman
mihte, þa gegaderode Eadwine eorl and Morkere eorll of heora eorldome swa
mycel werod swa hi begitan mihton and wið þone here gefuhton and mycel
wæl geslogon, and þær wæs þæs Engliscan folces mycel ofslagen
and adrenct and on fleam bedrifen, and Normein ahton wælstowe gewald.
 1066.49. And þis gefeoht wæs on Vigilia Mathei Apreli, and
wæs Wodnesdæg.
 1066.50. And þa æfter þam gefeohte for Harold cyningc of
Norwegan and Tostig eorl into Eoferwic mid swa miclum folce swa heom þa
geþuhte, and hi mon gislade of þære burh and eac to metsunge fylste, and
swa þanon to scipe foran and to fullan friðe gespræcon þæt hig
ealle mid him suð faran woldon and þis land gegan.
 1066.55. Ða amang þissan com Harold Engla cyningc mid ealre his
fyrde on ðone Sunnandæg to Tada and þær his lið fylcade and for
þa on Monandæg þurh ut Eoferwic, and Harold cyningc of Norwegan and
Tostig eorl and heora gefylce wæron afaren of scipe begeondan Eoferwic to
Stanfordbrycge, forþam þe him wæron behaten to gewissan þæt him man
þær of ealre þære scire ongean hy gislas bringan wolde.
 1066.61. Ða com Harold Engla cyning heom ongean on unwaran
begeondan þære brycge, and hi þær togædere fengon and swyðe
heardlice lange on dæg feohtende wæron, and þær wæs Harold cyning
of Norwegan and Tostig eorl ofslagen and ungerim folces mid heom, ægðer ge
Normana ge Englisca, and þa Normen flugon þa Englisa.
 1066.66. Ða wes þer an of Norwegan þe wiðstod þet
Englisce folc, þet hi ne micte þa brigge oferstigen, ne sige gerechen.
 1066.68. Þa seite an Englisce mid anre flane, ac hit nactes ne
widstod, ænd þa com an oþer under þere brigge end hine þurustang en
under þere brunie.
 1066.70. Þa com Harold Engla chinge ofer þere brigge and hys
furde forð mid hine, and þere michel wel geslogon, ge Norweis ge
Flæming, and þes cyninges sunu Hetmundus let Harold faran ham to Norweie
mid alle þa scipe.

 0.1. Brytene igland is ehta hund mila lang and twa hund mila brad,
and her synd on þam iglande fif geþeodu, Ænglisc, Brytwylsc, Scottysc,
Pihttisc and Boclæden.
 0.3. Ærest wæron buend þyses landes Bryttas, þa comen of
Armenia, and gesæton suþonwearde Brytene ærost.
 0.5. Ða gelamp hit þæt Pehtas comon suþon of Scitthian,
mid langum scipum na manegum, and þa comon ærest on Norð Ybernian up,
and þær bædon Scottas þæt hi þær moston wunian.
 0.8. Ac hig noldon heom lyfan, for þon þe hig cwædon
þæt hi ne mihton ealle ætgædere gewunian þær.
 0.9. And þa cwædon þa Scottas, we magon eow hwæþere
ræd gelæron.
 0.10. We witon oþer igland her beeastan, þær ge magon
eardian gyf ge wyllað, and gyf hwa eow wiðstent, we eow fultumiað
þæt ge hit magon gegangan.
 0.14. Ða ferdon þa Pihtas and geferdon þis land
norþanweard, suþonweard hit hæfdon Bryttas, swa we ær cwædon.
 0.15. And þa Pihtas heom abædon wif æt Scottan, on þa
gerad þæt hi gecuron hyre cynecynn aa on þa wifhealfe, þæt hy
heoldon swa lange syþþan.
 0.19. And þa gelamp ymbe geara ryne þæt Scotta sum dæl
gewat of Ybernian on Brytene, and þæs landes sumne dæl geeodon, and
wæs heora heretoga Reoda gehaten, fram þam hy synd genæmnede Dalreodi.
 0.23. Syxtigum wintrum ær þon Crist wære acænned, Gaius
Iulius, Romane Casere, mid hundehtatigum ceolum gesohte Brytene.
 0.25. Ðær he wæs ærest geswænced mid grimmum
gefeohte, and mycelne dæl his heres forlædde.
 0.26. And þa he forlet his here gebidan mid Scottum, and gewat
suð into Galwalum and þær gegaderode syx hund scipa, mid þam he gewat
eft into Brytene.
 0.28. And þa hi ærost togædere geræsde, þa mon ofsloh
þæs kaseres gerefan, se wæs Labienus gehaten.
 0.30. Ða genamon þa Walas and adrifon sumre ea ford ealne mid
scearpum stængum greatum innan þam wætere.
 0.32. Seo ea hatte Tæmese.
 0.32. Ða þæt onfundon þa <foreign>Romani</foreign>, þa noldon hig faran
ofer þone ford.
 0.33. Ða flugon þa Brytwalas to þam wuduwestenum.
 0.34. And se kasere geeode wel monige heahburh mid myclum gewinne,
and eft gewat into Galwalum.

geare his rices Crist wæs acenned.
 2.1. Ða tungelwitegan of eastdæle comon to þam þæt hi
Crist wyrþoden, and þa cild on Betleem ofslagene wæron for ehtnesse fram
Erode.
 3.1. Her swealt Herodes fram him sylfum ofsticod, and Archelaus his
sunu feng to rice.

fram eodon.

wæron ofslægene.

 875.1. Her for se here fram Hreopedune, and Healfdene for mid sumum

 876.1. Her hine bestæl se here into Werham Westseaxna fyrde.

 878.17. And he for ymb ane niht of þam wicum to Æglea, and

 894.1. On þysson geare, þæt wæs ymbe tweolf monað

 894.6. And þa gadrode Ælfred cyning his fyrd and for þæt

 894.10. Þa foron hi syððan æfter þam wealde hloþum and

 894.14. And hæfde se cyning his fyrd on twa tonumen, swa

 894.17. Ne com se here oftor eall ute of þam setum þonne tuwa,

 894.20. Þa hi gefengon mycele herehyðe, and þa woldon ferian

 894.22. Þa forrad seo fyrd hy foran, and him wið feaht æt

flugon ofer Temese butan ælcum forda, þa up be Calne on anne igeað.
 894.26. Þa besæt se fyrd hi ðer utan þa hwile þe hi mete

 894.30. Þa he ða þyderweard wæs, and seo oþru fyrd

 894.33. Þa gaderoden þa ðe on Norðhymbrum bugeað and on

 894.37. Þa se cyning þæt gehyrde, þa wende he hine west

 894.40. Þa foron forð oð hi comon to Lundenbyrig, and þa

 894.42. Wæs þa Hæstan þær cumen, þe ær on Limene

 894.43. Hæfde Hæstan ær geworht þæt weorc æt

 894.45. Þa foron hi to, and geflymdon þone here, and þæt

 894.55. Ac sona swa hi to Beamfleote comon and þæt geweorc

 894.59. Þa se cyning hine west wende myd þære fyrde wið

 894.62. Þa he ða wið þone here þær west abysgod

 894.68. Þa gegaderode Æþered ealdorman and Æþelm

 894.73. Þa hi ða ealle gegaderode wæron, þa offoron hi

 894.76. Þa hi ða þær fela wucena sæton on twa healfe

 894.80. Þa eodon hi ut to þam mannum þe on easthealfe

 894.82. And þær wearð Ordeah þæs cyninges þeng

 894.85. Þa hi ða on Eastsexe comon to hyra geweorce and to

 894.92. Þa ne mihte seo fyrd hi na hindan offaran ær hi

 894.97. And þæt wæs ymb <foreign>xii</foreign> monað þæs þe hi

 895.1. Ond þa sona æfter þam on þyssum gearæ for se

 895.5. Þa foron hi ofer Norðhymbra land on Eastængla, swa

 895.8. And þa se here eft hamweard wende þe Eaxanceaster
beseten hæfde, þa hergoden hi up on Suðseaxum neah Cisceastre, and þa
burhware hy geflymdon, and hyra monig hund ofslogon, and heora scipu sume
genamon.
 895.12. Þa þy ilcan geara on foreweard winter þa Dæniscean
þe on Meresigge sæton tugon heora scipu up on Temese and þa up on

 896.1. Ond þa þy ilcan geare worhte se foresprecena here

 896.6. Þa þæs on herfeste wicode se cyning on neaweste

 896.8. Þa sume dæge rad se cyning up be þære ea, and

 896.12. Þa hi þæt weorc furðum ongunnen hæfdon, and
þærto gewicod hæfde, þa ongeat se here þæt hi ne mihton þa
scipu ut bringan, and eodon þa ofer land, þæt hi gedydon æt Brygce be
Sæfern, and þæt geweorc wrohton.
 896.16. Þa rad seo fyrd æfter þam herge, and þa men on
Lundenbyrig gefetedon þa scipu, and ealle þa þe hi alædan ne mihton hi
tobræcon, and þa þe þær setlwyrðe wæron binnan Lundenbyrig
gebrohton.
 896.19. And þa Dæniscan hæfdon hiora wif befæst innan
Eastengle ær hi ut of þam geweorce foron.
 896.21. Þa sæton hi þone winter æt Brygcge.

 897.39. Ac þæt þæt wæter wæs aebbod fela furlange

 959.16. He wearð wide geond þeodland swyðe geweorðað for

gelome, and Godes lof rærde, wide and side, and wislice rædde, oftost a
symble, for Gode and for weorulde, ealre his þeode.
 959.23. Ane misdæde he dyde þeah to swyðe, þæt he

to fæste, and utlændisce hider in tihte, and deriende leoda bespeon to
þysan earde.

ofslagen, and Kænulf bisceop forðferde.
 1006.5. And ða ofer þone midne sumor com se micla flota to
Sandwic, and dydon ealswa hi ær gewuna wæron, her godon and bærndon
and slogon swa swa hi ferdon.
 1006.8. Ða het se cyng abannan ut ealne þeodscipe of Westseaxum
and of Myrcum, and hi lægon ute þa ealne þone hærfæst on fyrdinge
ongean þone here, ac hit naht ne beheold þe ma ðe hit oftor ær dyde,
ac for eallum þissum se here ferde swa he sylf wolde, and seo fyrding dyde
þære landleode ælcne hearm, þæt him naðær ne dohte ne inhere
ne uthere.
 1006.14. Ða hit winterlæhte þa færde se fyrd ham, and se
here com þa ofer þa Martines mæssan to his fryðstole Wihtlande, and
tylode him þær æghwær þæs þe hi behofedon, and þa to þam
middanwintran eodon him to heora gearwan feorme ut þurh Hamtunscire into
Bearruhscire to Readingon, and hi a dydon hiora ealdan gewuna, ateondon hiora
herebeacna swa swa hi ferdon.
 1006.20. Wendon þa to Wealingæforda, and þæt eall
forswælldon, and wæron him ða ane niht æt Ceolesege, and wendon him
ða andlang Æscesdune to Cwichelmeshlæwe, and þær onbidedon beotra
gylpa, for þan oft man cwæð, gif hi Cwichelmæshlæwe gesohton,
þæt he næfre to sæ gangen ne sceoldon, wendon him ða oþres weges
hamweard.
 1006.25. Ða wæs þær fyrd gesomned æt Cynestan, and hi
ðær togædere fengon, and sona þæt wærod on fleame gebrohton,
and syððan heora herehyðe to sæ feredon.
 1006.28. Ðær mihton geseon Winceasterleode rancne here and
unearhne, þa hi be heora gate to sæ eodon, and mete and madmas <foreign>l</foreign> mila
him fram sæ fetton.
 1006.31. Ða wæs se cyning gewend ofer Temese into
Scrobbesbyrigscire, and nam þær his feorme in þære middewintres
tide.
 1006.33. Ða wearð hit swa mycel ege fram þam here, þæt
nan ne mihte geþencan, and ne asmeagan, hu man hi of earde bringan sceolde,
oþþe þisne eard wið hi gehealdan, for þan þe hi hæfdon ælce
scire on Westseaxum stiðe gemercod mid bryne and mid hergunge.
 1006.37. Agan se cyning þa georne to smeagenne wið his witan
hwæt him eallum rædlicust þuhte, þæt mon þissum earde gebeorgan
meahte, ær hi mid ealle fordon wurde.
 1006.40. Ða gerædde se cyng and his witan eallum þeodscipe
to þearfe, þeah hit him eallum lað wære, þæt mon nyde moste
þæm here gafol geldan.
 1006.42. Ða sende se cyning to þam here, and him cyðan het,
þæt he wolde þæt him grið betweonan beon sceolde, and him mon gaful
and metsunge sylan sceolde, and hi ða ealle þæt underfengon, and hi man
metsode þa geond eall Angelcynn.
 1007.1. Her on þissum geare wæs þæt gafol gelæst
þæm unfriðhere, þæt wæs <foreign>xxxvi</foreign> þusend punda.
 1007.2. On þissum geare wæs Eadric geset to ealdorman geond
Myrcna rice.
 1007.3. Her for Ælfeah bisceop to Rome æfter <foreign>pallium</foreign>.
 1008.1. Her bebead se cyng þæt man sceolde ofer eall Angelcyn
scypu fæstlice wyrcan, þæt is þonne of þrym hund scipum, and <foreign>x</foreign> be
tynum, anne scægð, and of <foreign>viii</foreign> hydum, helm and byrnan.
 1009.1. Her on þissum geare wurdon þa scypo gearwe þe we
ær ymbe spræcon, and hyra wæs swa fela swa næfre ær, þæs
þe us bec secgað, on Angelcynne ne gewurdon on nanes cynges dæge, and hi
man ða ealle togædere ferode to Sandwic, and þær sceoldon licgan, and
þisne eard healdan wið ælcne uthere.
 1009.6. Ac we þa gyt næfdon þa gesælða, ne þone
wurðscipe, þæt seo scypferd nyt wære þissum earde, þe ma þe heo
ofter ær wæs.
 1009.8. Ða gewearð hit on þissum ylcan timan, oððe lytle
ær, þæt Brihtric, Eadrices broþor ealdormannes, forwregde Wulnoð
cild þone Suðseaxcisan to þam cynge, and he þa ut gewende, and him þa
to aspeon þæt he hæfde <foreign>xx</foreign> scipa, and he þa hergode æghwær be
þam suðriman and eac yfel worhton.
 1009.13. Ða cydde man into þære scypfyrde þæt hy man
æaðe befaran mihte, gif man ymbe beon wolde.
 1009.14. Ða genam se Brihtric him to hundeahtatig scypa, and
þohte þæt he him micles wordes wyrcan sceolde, þæt he Wulnoð
cuconne oððe deadne begytan sceolde.
 1009.17. Ac ða hi þiderweard wæron, þa com him swilc wind
ongean, swylce nan man ear ne gemunde, and þa scypo ealle tobeot and
toþærsc, and on lande aweorp, and com se Wulfnoþ sona, and þa scypo
forbærnde.
 1009.21. Ða þis cuð wæs to þam oðrum scypum þær
se cyng wæs hu ða oðre geferdon, wæs þa swilc hit eall rædleas
wære, and ferde se cyning him ham, and þa ealdormenn, and þa heahwitan,
and forlæton þone scypo þus leohtlice, and þæt folc þa þæt
on þæm scypon wæron fercodon þa scypo eft to Lundenne, and læton
ealle þa scypas geswinc þus leohtlice forwurðan, and næs se sige na
betera þe eall Angelcynn to hopode.
 1009.28. Ða ðæs scypfyrd þus geendod wæs, ða com sona
æfter Lafmæssan se ungemetlica unfriðhere to Sandwic, and sona wendon
heora fore to Cantwarebyrig, and þa burh raþe geeodon, gif hi ðe raþor
to him friðæs ne gyrndon.
 1009.32. And ealle Eastcentingas frið wið þone here genamon,
and him gesealdon þreo þusend punda.
 1009.33. And se here þa sona æfter þam wende abuten oð he
com to Wihtlande, and þær æghwær on Suðseaxum, and on Hamtunscire,
and eac on Bearrocscire hergodon and bærndon swa heora gewuna is.
 1009.37. Ða het se cyning abannan ut ealne þeodscipe, þæt
mon ælce healfe wið hy healdan sceolde, ac þeahhwæðere hi ferdon
loca hu hi woldon.
 1009.39. Ða sume siðe hæfde se cyning hi foregan mid ealre
fyrde þa hi to scypon woldon, and eall folc gearu wæs him on to fonne, ac
hit wæs þa þuruh Eadric ealdorman gelæt swa hit gyt æfre wæs.
 1009.42. Ða æfter Sanctus Martinus mæssan þa ferdon hi
æft ongean to Cent, and namon him wintersetl on Tæmesan, and lifdon him
of Eastseaxum and of þam scirum þe þærneaxst wæron on twa healfum
Temese.
 1009.45. And oft hi on þa buruh Lundenne fuhton, ac si Gode lof,
þæt heo gyt gesund stent, and hi þær æfre yfel geferdon.
 1009.47. Ða æfter middanwintra þa namon hi anne upgang up
þuruh Ciltern, and swa to Oxenaforda, and þa burh forbærndan, and namon
hit þa on twa healfe Temese to scype weard.
 1009.50. Þa gehwarnede man hi þæt þær wæs fyrd æt
Lundenne ongean, hi wendon him þa ofer æt Stane, and þus ferdon ealne
þone winter, and þæt lencten wæron him on Cent, and bettan heora
scypo.
 1010.1. Her on þissum geare com se forespecena here ofer Eastron
to Eastænglum, and wendon up æt Gypeswic, and eodon anreces þær hi
geacsedon Ulfcytel mid his fyrde.
 1010.3. Þis wæs on þam dæge <foreign>Prima Ascensio Domini</foreign>.
 1010.4. And þa sona flugon Eastænglæ, þa stod
Grantabricscire fæstlice ingean.
 1010.5. Þær wæs ofslagen Æþelstan þæs cynges
aþum, and Oswig and his sunu, and Wulf, Leofwines sunu, and Eadwig, Æfices
broþor, and feola oþra goda þægna, and folces unrim.
 1010.8. Þone flean astealde ærest Þurcytel Myranheafod, and
þa Denan ahton weallstowe geweald, and þær wurdon gehorsode, and
syþþan ahton Eastengla geweald, and þone eard þry monðas hergodon and
bærndon, ge furþon on þa wilda fennas hi ferdon, and men and yrfe hi
slogon, and bærndon geond þa fennas, and Þeotford forbærndon, and
Grantabricge, and syþþan wendan eft suðweard into Temese, and rydon þa
gehorsedan men ongean þa scipo, and syþþan eft hrædlice wendon
westweard on Oxenafordascire, and þonen to Buccingaham scire, and swa andlang
Usan oð hi comon to Bedanforda, and swa forð oð Temesanford, and a
bærndon swa hi geferdon.
 1010.19. Wendon þa eft to scypon mid heora herehuðe.
 1010.20. And þonne hi to scipon ferdon þonne scolde fyrd ut
æft ongean þæt hi up woldan, þonne ferde seo fyrd ham.
 1010.22. And þonne hi wæron beeastan, þonne heold man fyrde
bewestan, and þonne hi wæron besuðan, þonne wæs ure fyrd
benorðan.
 1010.24. Ðonne bead mon ealle witan to cynge, and man þonne
rædan sceolde hu man þisne eard werian sceolde.
 1010.26. Ac þeah mon hwæt rædde, þæt ne stod furþon
ænne monað.
 1010.27. Æt nextan næs nan heafodman þæt fyrde gaderian
wolde, ac ælc fleah swa he meast mihte, ne furþon nan scir nolde oþre
geleastan æt nextan.
 1010.29. Ða ætforan Sanctus Andreas messandæg þa com se
here to Hamtune, and þæt port sona forbærndon and þærabutan swa
mycel swa hi sylf woldon, and þanon wendon ofer Temese into Westseaxum, and
swa wið Canegan mersces, and þæt eall forbearndon.
 1010.33. Þa hi swa feor gegan heafdon swa hi ða woldon, comon
þa to þam middanwintra to scypon.
 1011.1. Her on þissum geare sende se cyning and his witan to
þæm here and gyrndon fryðes, and him gafol and metsunge beheton wið
þan ðe hy heora hergunge swicon.
 1011.3. Hi hæfdon þa ofergan Eastenglæ <foreign>i</foreign>, and Eastseaxum
<foreign>ii</foreign>, and Middelseaxe <foreign>iii</foreign>, and Oxnaforda <foreign>iiii</foreign>, and Grantabricga <foreign>v</foreign>, and
Heortfordescire <foreign>vi</foreign>, and Buccingahamscire <foreign>vii</foreign>, and Bedanfordscire <foreign>viii</foreign>,
and healfe Huntedunscire <foreign>ix</foreign>, and micel on Hamtunscire <foreign>x</foreign>, and besuðan
Temese ealle Centinges and Suðseaxe and Hæstingas and Suðrige and
Bearrocscire and Hamtunscire and micel on Wiltunscire.
 1011.10. Ealle þa ungesælþa us gelumpon þurh unrædas,
þæt man nolde a timan gafol beodan, ac þonne hi mæst to yfele gedon
hæfdon, þonne nam man gryð and fryð wið hy, and na ðe læs for
eallum þissum gryðe and gafole ferdon æghwyder flocmælum and
hergodon, and ure earme folc rypton and slogon.
 1011.15. And þa on þissum geare betweox <foreign>Natiuitas Sancte
Mariæ</foreign> and Sancte Michaheles mæssan hy ymbesæton Cantwaraburh, and hi
ðærinto comon þuruh hyre wrencas, for þan Ælmær hi becyrde, þe
se arcebisceop Ælfeah ær generode his life, and hi þær genamon
þone arcebisceop Ælfeah, and Ælfweard cynges gerefa, and Leofrune
<foreign>abbatissa</foreign>, and Godwine biscop, and Ælmær abbod hi læton aweg, and hi
ðær genamon inge ealle þa gehadodan men and wæras and wif, þæt
wæs unasecgendlic ænigum men hu micel þæs folces wæs.
 1011.24. And on þære byrig syððan wæron swa lange swa
hi woldon, and ða hi hæfdon þa buruh ealle asmeade, wend on him þa to
scypon, and læddon þone arcebiscop mid him.
 1011.27. Wæs þa ræpling, se þe ær wæs heafod
Angelcynnes and Cristendomes.
 1011.29. Þær man meahte þa geseon ermðe þær man oft
ær geseah blisse, on þære earman byrig þanon us com ærest 
Cristendom and bliss, for Gode and for weorulde.
 1011.33. And hi hæfdon þone arcebisceop mid him swa lange oð
ðone timan þe hi hine gemartredon.
 1012.1. Her on þissum geare com Eadric ealdorman and ealle þa
ildestan witan, gehadode and læwede, Angelcynnes to Lundenbyrig toforan
þam Eastron, wæs Easterdæg þa on þæm <foreign>datarum Idus Aprilis</foreign>, and
hi þær ða swa lange wæron oð þæt gafol eall gelæst wæs
ofer þa Eastron, þæt wæs ehta and feowertig þusend punda.
 1012.6. Ða on ðære Sæternesdæg wearð þa se here
swyðe astyred angen þone bisceop, for ðæm ðe he nolde him nan feoh
behaten, and forbead þæt man nan þing wið him syllan ne moste,
wæron hi eac swyðe druncene, for þæm þær wæs broht win
suðan.
 1012.10. Genamon þa þone bisceop, læddon hine to heora
hustinge on þone Sunnanæfen <foreign>xiii</foreign> <foreign>Kalendas Maias octabas Pasche</foreign>, and
hine/ ðær þa oftorfedon mid banum and mid hryþera neata heafedum, and
sloh hine þa an hiora mid anre eaxe ere on þæt heafod, þæt he mid
þam dynte nyþær astah, and his halige blod on þa eorþan feoll, and
his þa halgan sawle to Godes rice asende.
 1012.16. And mon þone lichamon on mærgen færede to Lundene,
and þa bisceopæs Eadnoð and Ælfun and seo burhwaru hine underfengon
mid ealre arwurðnysse, and hine bebyrigdon on Sancte Paulus mynstre, and
þær God nu sutelað þæs halgan martires mihta.
 1012.20. Ða þæt gafol gelæst wæs and þa friðaþas
asworene, þa toferde se here wide swa he gegaderod wæs.
 1012.22. Ða bugon to þæm cyninge of þæm here fif and
feowertig scype, and him beheton þæt hi woldon þisne eard healdan, and
he hi fedan sceolde and scrydan.
 1013.1. On þæm æfteran geare þe se arcebisceop wæs
gemartred, se cyning gesette Lyfinc bisceop to Cantwarebyrig to þæm
arcestole.
 1013.3. And on þissum ilcan geare toforan þæm monðe
Augustus com Swegen cyning mid his flotan to Sandwic, and wende swyðe hraðe
abutan Eastenglum into Humbra muþan, and swa upweard andlang Trentan oð he
com to Gæignesburh, and þa sona beah Uhtred eorl and ealle norðhymbre to
him, and eall þæt folc on Lindesige, and siþþan þæt folc into
Fifburgum, and raþe ðæs eall here benorðan Wætlingan stræte, and
him man sealde gislas of ælcere scire.
 1013.11. Syþþan he undergeat þæt eall folc him to gebogen
wæs, þa bed he þæt mon sceolde his here mettian and horsian, and he
þa wende syþþan suðweard mid fulre fyrde, and betæhte þa scypu
þa Cnute his suna, and syþþan he com ofer Wætlinga stræte worhton
þæt mæste yfel þæt ænig here don mihte.
 1013.16. Wenda þa to Oxenaforde, and seo buruhwaru sona beah and
gislude, and þanon to Winceastre, and hy þæt ylce dydon.
 1013.18. Wendon þa þanon eastweard to Lundene, and mycel his
folces adrangc on Temese, for þæm þe hi nanre brice ne cæpton.
 1013.20. Þa þe he to þære byrig com þa nolde se
buruhwaru bugan, ac heoldon mid fullon wige ongean, for þan þær wæs
inne se cyning Æþelred and Þurcyl mid him.
 1013.22. Þa wende Swegen cyng þanon to Weallingaforda and swa
ofer Temese westweard to Baþan, and sæt þær mid his fyrde, and com
Æþelmær ealdorman þyder and þa wæstrena ðegenas mid him, and
bugon ealle to Swegene, and gislodon.
 1013.26. And þa he æl þus gefaren hæfde, wende þa
norþweard to his scypum.
 1013.27. And eall þeodscipe hine hæfde þa for fulne cyning.
 1013.28. And seo buruhwaru æfter þæm on Lundenne beah and
gislude, for þon hi ondredon þæt hi fordon wolde.
 1013.30. Bead þa Swegen ful gyld and metsunge to his hære
þone winter, and Þurcyl bead þæt ylce to þæm here þe læg
æt Grenawic, and butan þæm hi gehergodon swa oft swa hi woldon, þa ne
dohte naþær þisse leode ne suðan ne norðan.
 1013.34. Þa wæs se cyning sume hwile mid þam flotan þe on
Temese læg, and seo hlæfdige wende þa ofer sæ to hire broþor
Ricarde, and Ælfsige abbod of Burh mid hire, and se cyning sende Ælfun
bisceop mid þam æþelingum Eadwearde and Ælfrede ofer sæ, þæt
he hi bewitan sceolde.
 1013.39. And se cyning wende þa fram þam flotan to þam
middanwintre to Wihtlande, and wæs þær ða tid, and æfter þære
tide wende ofer þa sæ to Ricarde, and wæs þær mid him oð ðone
byre þe Swegen dead wearð.
 1014.1. Her on þissum geare Swegen geendode his dagas to
Candelmæssan <foreign>iii Nonas Februarii</foreign>.
 1014.2. And þy ilcan geare man hadode Ælfwig bisceop on
Eoforwic to Lundenburuh on Sancta Iuliana mæssedæg.
 1014.4. And se flota þa eall gecuron Cnut to cyninge.
 1014.5. Þa ræddon þa witan ealle, gehadode and læwede,
þæt man æfter þam cyninge Æþelrede sende, and cwædon þæt
him nan hlaford leofra nære þonne hyra gecynda hlaford, gif he hi
rihtlicor healdan wolde þonne he ær dyde.
 1014.8. Þa sende se cyning his sunu Eadweard hider mid his

ascunodon, and ælc þara þinga forgyfon beon sceolde þe him gedon
oððe cwæden wære, wið þam þe hi ealle anrædlice butan
swicdome to him gecyrdon.
 1014.14. And man þa fulne freondscipe gefæstnode mid worde and
mid wedde on ægþre healfe, and æfre ælcne Dæniscne cyning utlah
of Ænglalande gecwædon.
 1014.17. Þa com Æþelred cyning innan þam lænctentid ham
to his agenre þeode, and he glædlice fram him eallum on fangen wæs.
 1014.19. Þa syþþan Swegen dead wæs, sæt Cnut mid his

on Lindesige anes þæt he hine horsian sceoldon, and wið þan ealle
