 1014.23. Ða com se cyning Æþelred mid fulre fyrde þyder
ær/ hi gearwe wæron to Lindesige, and man þa hergode and bærnde and
sloh eall þæt mancynn þæt man geræcan mihte.
 1014.25. And se Cnut gewende him ut mid his flotan, and wearð
þæt earme folc þus beswicen þurh hine, and wende þa suðweard oð
he com to Sandwic, and læt man þær up þa gislas þe his fæder
gesealde wæron, and cearf of heora handa and earan and nosa.
 1014.30. And buton eallum þissum yfelum se cyng het gyldan þam
here þe on Grenewic læg <foreign>xxi</foreign> þusend punda.
 1014.31. And on þissum geare on Sancte Michaeles mæsseæfen
com þæt mycle sæflod geond wide þisne eard, and earn swa feor up swa
næfre ær ne dyde, and adrencte fela tuna, and manncynnes unarimedlic
getel.
 1015.1. On þissum geare wæs þæt mycle gemot on
Oxnaforda.
 1015.2. And þær Eadric ealdorman beswac Siferð and Morcer,
þa yldostan þegenas into Seofonburhgum, bepæhte hi into his bure, and hi
mon þærinne ofsloh ungerysenlice.
 1015.4. And se cyng þa nam ealle heora æhta, and het niman
Siferþæs lafe and gebringan binnan Ealdelmesbyrig.
 1015.6. Þa æfter lytlum fæce færde Eadmund æþeling
to, and genam þæt wif ofer þæs cynges wil, and hæfde him to wife.
 1015.8. Ða toforan <foreign>Natiuitas Sancte Marie</foreign> ferde se æþeling
þanon wæstan norð into Fifburhgum, and gerad sona ealle Siferðæs

 1015.11. And þa on þam ilcan timan com Cnut cyng to Sandwic,
and wende þa sona abutan Centland into Westseaxum oð he com to From
muþan, and hergode þa on Dorsætum and on Wiltunscire and on
Sumersæton.
 1015.15. Þa læg se cyng seoc æt Cosham.
 1015.15. And þa gaderede Eadric ealdorman fyrde, and se
æþeling Eadmund benorðan.
 1015.16. Þa hi togædere comon, þa wolde se ealdorman
beswican þone æþeling, and hi toferdon þa butan gefeohte for þæm,
and rymdon heora feondum.
 1015.19. And Eadric ealdorman aspeon ða feowertig scipa fram
þam cyninge, and beah þa to Cnute, and Wæstseaxe bugon and gislodon and
horsedon þone here, and he wæs þær þa oð midne winter.
 1016.1. Her on þissum geare com Cnut mid his here, and Eadric
ealdorman mid him, ofer Temese into Myrcum, æt Cricgelade, and wendon þa
to Wærincwicscire ingang þære middanwintres tidæ, and hergodon and
bærndon and slogon eall þæt hi to comon.
 1016.5. Ða ongan seo Eadmund æþeling to gadrigenne fyrde,
þa seo fyrd gesomned wæs, þa ne onhagode hy þærto buton þæt
wære þæt se cyng þær mid wære, and hi hæfdon þære
buruhware fultum on Lundene, geswicon þa ðære fyrdinge and ferde ælc
man him ham.
 1016.9. Ða æfter þære tide þa bead man æft fyrde be
fullum wite þæt ælc man þe fere wære forð wende, and man sende
to þæm cyninge to Lundene and bedon hine þæt he come ongean þa
fyrde mid þam fultume þe he gegaderian mihte.
 1016.13. Þa hi ealle tosomne comon, þa ne beheold nan þinc
þe ma ðe hit ofter ær dyde.
 1016.15. Þa cydde man þæm cyninge þæt hine man beswican
wolde, þa ðe him on fultume beon sceoldon, forlet þa þa fyrde, and
cyrde him eft to Lundene.
 1016.17. Ða rad se æþeling Eadmund to Norðhymbron, to
Uhtrede eorle, and wende ælc man þæt hi woldon fyrde somnian ongean
Cnut cyng.
 1016.19. Þa fyrdodon hy into Stæffordscire, and into
Scrobbesbyrig, and to Lægceastre, and hergodon hi on heora healfe, and Cnut
on his.
 1016.21. Wende him ða ut þuruh Buccingahamscire into
Bedanfordscire and þanon to Huntadunscire and swa into Hamtunscire andlang
fennes to Stanforda, and þa into Lincolnescire, þanon þa into
Snotinghamscire, and swa to Norðhymbron to Eoforwic weard.
 1016.26. Ða Uhtred geahsode þis, þa forlet he his hergunge
and efstte norðweard, and beah ða for nyde, and ealle Norðhymbra mid him,
and he gislode, and hine man þeahhwæðere ofsloh, and Þurhcytel, Nafen
sunu, mid him.
 1016.29. And þa æfter þæm se cyng gesette Yric into
Norðhymbron to eorle, ealswa Uhtred wæs, and syððan wende him
suðweard oðres weges, ealswa bewestan.
 1016.32. And com þa eall se here toforam þam Eastron to
scypon.
 1016.33. And se æþeling Eadmund wende to Lundene to his
fæder.
 1016.34. And þa æfter Eastron wende se cyng Cnut mid eallon
his scypon to Lunden weard.
 1016.35. Ða gelamp hit þæt se cyning Æþelred
forðferde ær ða scypo comon, he geendode his dagas on Sancte Georgius
mæssedæg æfter myclum geswince and earfoðnyssum his lifes.
 1016.38. And þa æfter his ende ealle þa witan þe on
Lundene wæron and seo buruhwaru gecuron Eadmunde to cyninge, and he his rice
heardlice wærode þa hwila þe his tima wæs.
 1016.41. Þa comon þa scipo to Grenawic to þam gandagum, and
binnan litlan fæce wendon to Lundene and dulfon þa ane micle dic on
suðhealfe, and drogon hera scipo on westhealfe þære bricge, and
bedicodon þa syððan, and þa buruh utan, þæt nan man ne mihte ne
inn ne ut, and oftrædlice on þa buruh fuhton, ac hi him heardlice
wiðstodon.
 1016.47. Þa wæs Eadmund cyng ær þan gewend ut and geard
þa Westseaxon, and him beah eall þæt folc to.
 1016.49. And raðe æfter þam he gefeaht wið þæne here
æt Peonnan wið Gillingaham, and oþær gefeoht he gefeaht æfter
middansumera æt Scortane, and þær micel wæll feoll on ægðre
healfe, and þa heres him sylfe toeodon on þam gefeohte, and Eadric
ealdorman and Ælmer Dyrling wæron þam here on fultume ongean Eadmunde
cyning.
 1016.54. And þa gegaderade he þriddan siðe fyrde and ferde to
Lundenne, and þa buruhwaru aredde, and þæne here aflymde to scipe, and
þa þæs ymbe twa niht se cynng gewende ofer æt Brægentforda, and
þa wið þone here gefeaht, and hine aflymde, and þær adranc mycel
Ænglisces folces on hyra agenra gymeleaste, þa þe ferdon beforan
þære fyrde and feng woldan fon.
 1016.61. And se kyning æfter þæm gewende to Westseaxan, and
his fyrde samnade.
 1016.62. Þa gewende se here sona to Lundenne, and þa buruh utan
ymbesæton, and hyre stearclice on feaht ægðær ge be wætere ge be
lande, ac se ælmihtiga God hi ahredde.
 1016.65. Se here gewende þa æfter þæm fram Lundene mid
hyra scipum into Arewan, and þær up foran and ferdon on Myrcan, and slogon
and bærndon swa hwæt swa hi oferforan, swa hyra gewuna is, and him metes
tiledan, and hi drifan ægþær ge scipa ge hyra drafa into Medewæge.
 1016.69. Ða samnede Eadmund cyning feorþan siðe ealle Engle
þeode, and ferde ofer Temese æt Brægentforda, and ferde in on Cænt,
and se here him fleah beforan mid heora horsum into Sceapege, and se kyning
ofsloh hyra swa feola swa he offaran mihte.
 1016.74. And Eadric ealdorman gewende þa þone cyning ongean
æt Æglesforda.
 1016.75. Næs nan mare unræd geræd þænne se wæs.
 1016.75. Se here gewende eft up on Eastseaxan, and ferde into
Myrcan, and fordyde eall þæt he oferferde.
 1016.77. Ða se cyning geahsade þæt se here upp wæs, þa
gesamnade he fiftan siðe ealle Engla þeode and ferde him æthindan, and
offerde hi innon Eastseaxan æt þære dune þe man hæt Assandun, and
þær togædere heardlice fengon.
 1016.81. Þa dyde Eadric ealdorman swa swa he ær ofter dyde,
astealde þæne fleam ærast mid Magesætan, and swa aswac his
kynehlaforde and ealle þeodæ Angelcynnes.
 1016.84. Ðær ahte Cnut sige, and gefeaht him wið ealle Engla
þeode.
 1016.85. Þa wearð þær ofslægen Eadnoð biscop, and
Wulfsie abbod, and Ælfric ealdorman, and Godwine ealdorman, and Ulfkytel of
Eastenglan, and Æþelward Ælfwines sunu ealdormannes, and eall seo
duguð of Angelcynnes þeode.
 1016.89. Ða æfter þisum gefeohte wende Cnut cyning up mid
his here to Gleawcestrescire, þær he ofaxade þæt se cyning wæs
Eadmund.
 1016.91. Ða gerædde Eadric ealdorman and þa witan þe
þær gegaderade wæron þæt þa cyningas heom betweonan seht
geworhtan, and coman begen þa cyningas togædre æt Olanige wið
Deorhyrste, and wurdon feolagan and wedbroðra, and þæt gefæstnadan
ægðer mid wedde and eac mid aðan, and þæt gyld gesettan wið
þone here, and hi seoððan tohwurfon.
 1016.96. And feng þa Eamund cyng to Westsexan and Cnut to þam
norðdæle.
 1016.98. Se here gewende þa to scipon mid þam þe hi gefangen
hæfdon, and Lundenwaru gryðede wið þone here and heom fryð bohtan,
and hi gebrohtan heora scypa on Lundene, and hæfdon þær wintersetl.
 1016.101. Ða to Sancte Andreas mæssan forðferde Eadmund
cyng, and is bebyrged mid his ealdan fæder Eadgare on Glæstingabyri.
 1017.1. Her on þisan geare feng Cnut cyng to eall Englalandes
rice, and todælde hit on feower, him seolfan Westsexan, and Þurkylle
Eastenglan, and Eadrice Myrcean, and Eiric Norðhymbran.
 1017.4. On þisum geare wæs eac Eadric ealdorman ofslægen,

 1017.7. And Cnut cining aflymde ut Eadwi æþeling and Eadwi

 1017.8. And þa toforan <foreign>Kalendas Augusti</foreign> het se cyng feccean him

 1018.4. And se here þa ferde sum to Denmarcon, and <foreign>xl</foreign> scypa

 1023.11. Ða on þam þryddan dæge com Imma seo hlæfdie

forð þæt se casere hæfde of Baldawine eall þæt he wolde.
 1050.10. Þær com eac Swegen eorl, þe for ær of þisan
lande to Denmarcon, and þær forworhte hine wið Denum.
 1050.12. He com hider mid hiwunge, cwæð þæt he wolde eft
bugan to þam cynge, and Beorn eorl him gehet þæt he him on fylste beon
wolde.
 1050.14. Þa syððan þæs caseres seht wæs and
Baldwines, foron fela scypa ham, and se kyng belaf bæftan æt Sandwic mid
feawum scypum.
 1050.16. And Godwine eorl eac for mid <foreign>xlii</foreign> scypum fram Sandwic to
Peuenesea, and Beorn eorl him for mid.
 1050.18. Þa cyðde man þam cynge þæt Osgod lage on Ulpe
mid <foreign>xxxix</foreign> scypon, and se cyng þa sende æfter þam scypum þe he
ofsendan mihte, þe ær ham wendon.
 1050.20. And Osgod sette his wif on Brygce and wendon eft ongean
mid <foreign>vi</foreign> scypum, and þa oðre foron on Suðsexe to Eadulfesnæsse, and
þær hearm dydon, and wendon eft to scypon, and heom com þa strang wind
to, swa þæt hi wæron ealle forfarene buton feower þa man ofsloh
begeondan sæ.
 1050.25. On þam þe Godwine eorl and Beorn lagon on Peuenesea,
þa com Swein eorl and bæd Beorn eorl mid facne, þe wæs his eames
sunu, þæt he his gefera wære to þam cynge to Sandwic, and his wisa
wið hine gebette.
 1050.29. He wende þa for þære sibbe mid þreom geferum mid
him, and he hine lædde þa toward Bosanham, þær his scypu lagon, and
hine man þa geband, and to scypa lædde.
 1050.32. Wende þa þanon mid him to Dertamuðan, and hine
þær het slean, and deope bedelfan, hine man funde eft and ferede hine to
Wincestre, and byrigde wið Cnut cyng his eam.
 1050.35. Lytle ær þan þa men of Hæstingaceastre and
þærabutan gewunnon his twa scypa mid heora scypan, and þa men ealle
ofslogon, and þa scypa brohton to Sandwic to þan cynge, ehta scypu he
hæfde ær he Beorn beswice, syððan hine forleton ealle buton twam.
 1050.39. On þam ilcan geare comon upp on Wylisce Axa of Yrlande
<foreign>xxxvi</foreign> scypa, and þærabutan hearmas dydon mid Gryfines fultume þæs
Wæliscan cynges.
 1050.42. Man gegaderade þa folc togenes, þær wæs eac
Ealdred biscop mid, ac hi hæfdon to lytelne fultum, and hi comon unwær on
heom, on ealne ærnemergen, and fela godra manna þær ofslogon, and þa
oþre ætburston forð mid þam biscope.
 1050.45. Þis wæs gedon on <foreign>iiii Kalendas Augusti</foreign>.
 1050.46. Ðæs geres forðferde on Oxnafordscire Oswi abbod on
Þornege, and Wulfnoð abbod on Westmynstre.
 1050.47. And Ulf preost wæs geset þam bisceoprice to hyrde
þe Eadnoð hæfde, and he wæs syððan of adryfon, for þan þe he
ne gefremede naht biscoplices þæron, swa þæt us sceamað hit nu mare
to tellanne.
 1050.51. And Sigward biscop gefor, se ligeð on Abbandune.
 1050.51. And her man halgode þæt micele mynster æt Remys.
 1050.52. Þær wæs se papa Leo and se casere, and mycelne
sinoð þær hæfdon embe Godes þeowdom, þine sinoð foresæt
Sanctus Leo papa.
 1050.54. Hit is earfoð to witane þara biscopa þe þærto
comon, and huru abbuda, and heonon of lande wæron twegen gesende of Sancte
Agustine and of Rammesege.
 1051.1. On þisan geare gefor Eadsie arcebiscop on Cantwarebyri,
and se cyng sealde Rotbearde þan Freoncyscan þe ær wæs biscop on
Lundene þæt arcerice, and Spearhafoc abbod of Abbandune feng to þan
bisceoprice on Lundene, and hit wæs eft of him genumen ær he gehadod
wære.
 1051.5. And Hereman biscop and Ealdred biscop foron to Rome.
 1052.1.1. Her forðferde Ælfric arcebiscop on Eoferwic, swiðe
arwyrðe wer and wis.
 1052.1.2. And on þan ylcan geare alede Eadward cyng þæt
heregyld þæt Æþelred cyng ær astealde, þæt wæs on þam
nigon and þrittigoðan geare þæs þe he hit ongunnon hæfde,
þæt gyld gedrehte ealle Engla þeode on swa langum fyrste swa hit bufan
her awriten is, þæt wæs æfre ætforan oðrum gyldum þe man
myslice geald, and men mid menigfealdlice drehte.
 1052.1.8. On þam ylcan geare com Eustatius up æt Doferan, se
hæfde Eadwardes cynges sweostor to wife.
 1052.1.9. Þa ferdon his men dyslice æfter inne, and sumne man
ofslogon of þam porte, and oðer man of þam porte heora geferan, swa
þæt þær lagon <foreign>vii</foreign> his geferana, and micel hearm þær gedon
wæs on ægðre healfe mid horse and eac mid wæpnum oð þæt folc
gegaderede.
 1052.1.14. And hi þa ætflugon þæt hi comon to þam cynge
to Gleawcestre, and he heom gryð sealde.
 1052.1.15. Þa undernam Godwine eorl swyðe þæt on his
eorldome sceolde swilc geweorðan, ongan þa gadrian folc ofer eall his
eorldom, and Swein eorl his sunu ofer his, and Harold his oðer sunu ofer his
eorldom, and hi gegaderedan ealle on Gleawcesterscire æt Langatreo mycel
fyrd and unarimedlic, ealle gearwe to wige ongean þone cyng, buton man ageafe
Eustatsius and his men heom to hand sceofe, and eac þa Frencyscan þe on
þam castelle wæron.
 1052.1.23. Þis wæs gedon <foreign>vii</foreign> nihton ær þære lateran
Sancta Maria mæssan.
 1052.1.24. Þa wæs Eadward cyng on Gleawcestre sittende.
 1052.1.25. Sende þa æfter Leofrice eorl, and norð æfter
Siwarde eorle, and bæd heora gencges, and hi him þa to comon ærest mid
medemum fultume, ac siððan hy wiston hu hit þær besuðan wæs, þa
sendon hi norð ofer ealne heora eorldom and leton beodan mycele fyrde heora
hlaforde to helpe, and Raulf eac ofer his eorldom, and comon ða ealle to
Gleawceastre þam cynge to helpe, þeah hit læt wære.
 1052.1.31. Wurdan þa ealle swa anræde mid þam cynge þæt
hy woldon Godwines fyrde gesecan gif se cyng þæt wolde.
 1052.1.33. Þa leton hy sume þæt þæt mycel unræd
wære þæt hy togedere comon, for þam þær wæs mæst þæt
rotoste þæt wæs on Ænglalande on þam twam gefylcum, and leton
þæt hi urum feondum rymdon to lande, and betwyx us sylfum to mycclum
forwyrde.
 1052.1.37. Geræddon þa þæt man sealde gislas betweonan,
and setton stefna ut to Lundene, and man bead þa folce þider ut ofer ealne
þisne norðende, on Siwardes eorldome, and on Leofrices, and eac elles
gehwær, and sceolde Godwine eorl and his suna þær cuman to
wiðermale.
 1052.1.42. Þa comon hy to Suðgeweorce, and micel mænegeo mid
heom of Westsæxum, ac his wered wanode æfre þe lang þe swiðor.
 1052.1.44. And man borhfæste þam kyninge ealle þa
þægnas þe wæron Haroldes eorles his suna, and man utlagode þa
Swægn eorl his oðerne sunu.
 1052.1.46. Þa ne onhagode him to cumenne to wiðermale ongean
þone cyng and agean þone here þe him mid wæs.
 1052.1.48. For þa on niht awæg.
 1052.1.48. And se cyng hæfde þæs on morgen witena gemot,
and cwæð hine utlage, and eall here, hine and ealle his suna, and he wende
suð to þornege, and his wif and Swegen his suna and Tostig and his wif,
Baldwines mage æt Brycge, and Gerð his suna, and Harold eorl and Leofwine
foran to Brycgstowe on þæt scip þe Swegen eorl hæfde him silfum ær
gegearcod and gemetsod.
 1052.1.54. And se cining sende Ealdred biscop of Lundene mid genge,
and sceoldon hine ofridan ær he to scipe come, ac hi ne mihton, oððe hi
noldon.
 1052.1.56. And he wende þa ut of Afene muðan, and feng swa
stið weder þæt he uneaðe awæig com, and him þær micel
forferde.
 1052.1.58. Wende þa forð to Irlande, ða him weder com, and
Godwine and þa þe mid him wæron wendan of Ðornege to Brycge to
Baldwines lande on anum scipe mid swa miclum gærsuman swa hi mihton
þæron mæst gelogian to ælcum mannum.
 1052.1.62. Þæt wolde ðyncan wundorlic ælcum men þe on
Englalande wæs, gif ænig man ær þam sæde þæt hit swa
gewurþan sceolde, for ðam þe he wæs ær to þam swyðe up ahafen
swylce he weolde þæs cynges and ealles Englalandes, and his sunan wæron
eorlas, and þæs cynges dyrlingas, and his dohtor þæm cynge beweddod
and beæwnod, þa man gebrohte to Hwærwellan and hy þære abedissan
betæhton.
 1052.1.69. Ða sone com Willelm eorl fram geondan sæ mid
mycclum werode Frencisra manna, and se cyning hine underfeng, and swa feola his
geferan swa him to onhagode, and let hine eft ongean.
 1052.1.72. Þæs ilcan geres man sealde Wyllelme preoste
þæt biscoprice on Lundene þe wæs ær Spærhafoce geseald.
 1052.2.1. Her forþferde Ælfgyfu seo hlefdige, Æðelredes
laf cynges, and Cnutes cynges, on <foreign>ii Nonas Marias</foreign>.
 1052.2.2. On þam ilcan gere hergode Griffin se Wylisca cing on
Herefordscire þæt he com swyþe neah to Leomynstre, and men gadorodon
ongean ægðer ge landes men ge Frencisce men of ðam castele, and man
þær ofsloh swyþe feola Engliscra godra manna, and eac of þam
Frenciscum, þæt wæs þæs ylcan dæges on ðreottene geara þe
man ær Eadwine ofsloh mid his geferum.
 1052.2.8. And sona com Harold eorl of Irlande mid his scipum to
Sæfern muðan neh Sumersæton gemære and Dafenascire, and þær
mycel gehergode, and þæt landfolc him ongean gaderode ægþær ge of
Sumorsæton ge of Dafenascire, and he hyg aflimde, and þær ofsloh ma
þonne <foreign>xxx</foreign> godra ðegna, buton oðre folce, and sona æfter ðam for
abuton Penwiðsteort.
 1052.2.14. And þa læt Eadward cyng scypian XL snacca, þa
lagon æt Sandwic, þa sceoldon cepan Godwines eorles ðe on Brycge wæs
þone winter, and he ðeah com hider to lande ærest swa hy hit nystan, and
on þam þe he her on lande wæs he gespeon ealle Centingas, and ealle þa
butsekarlas of Hæstingum and þær æghwar abuton be þære
særiman, and ealne Eastsexan and Suðerege, and mycel elles toeacan þam.
 1052.2.21. Þa cwædon ealle þæt hi woldon mid him libban
and licgean.
 1052.2.22. Þa geaxedon þæt lið þæt on Sandwic læg
embe Godwines fare, setton þa æfter, and he heom ætbærst, and
þæt lið wende ongean to Sandwic, and swa hamweard to Lundenbyrig.
 1052.2.25. Þa þa Godwine geaxede þæt þæt lið þe
on Sandwic læig wæs ham gewend, þa for he æft ongean to Wiht, and
þærabutan be þam særiman, swa lange þæt hi comon togædere,
Harold eorl his suna and he, and hi noldon no mycelne hearm don syððon,
buton þæt hyg metsunge namon, ac speonnan heom þa eall þæt landfolc
to be þam særiman, and eac upp on lande, and hy foran toweard Sandwic, and
læson æfre forð mid heom ealle þa butsecarlas þe hy gemetton, and
coman þa to Sandwic mid geotendan here.
 1052.2.33. Þa Eadward þæt geaxode þa sende he upp æfter
maran fulltume, ac hy comon swiðe læte, and Godwine sæh him æfre
toward Lundenne mid his liðe þæt he com to Suðweorce, and þær
abad sume hwile oð þæt þæt flod upp eode.
 1052.2.37. On þam fyrste, and æc ær, he gefadode wiþ ða
burhwaru þæt hi mæst ealle woldon ðæt he wolde.
 1052.2.39. Þa þa he hæfde ealle his fare gereconod, þa com
þæt flod, and hy brudon sona upp heora ancras, and heoldan þurh þa
brycge aa bi þæm suþlande, and seo landfyrde coman ofenan, and trymedon
hy be þæm strande , and hi hwemdan ða mid þam scipum swylce hy woldon
ðes cynges scypu abuton betrymman.
 1052.2.44. Se cyning hæfde eac micle landfyrde on his halfe,
toeacan his scipmannum, ac hit wes mæst eallan lað to feohtanne wið
heora agenes cynnes mannum, for ðam þær wæs lytel elles þe aht
mycel myhton butan Englisce on ægðre healfe, and eac hi noldon þæt
utlendiscum mannum wære þes eard þurh þæt ðe swiðor gerymed
þe hi him sylfe ælc oþerne forfore.
 1052.2.50. Geræddan þa þæt man sende wyse men betweonan
and setton grið on ægðre halfe, and Godwine for upp, and Harold, and
heora lið swa micel swa heom þa geþuhte, and wæs þa witene gemot,
and man sealde Godwine clæne his eorldom, swa full and swa forð swa he
fyrmest ahte, and his sunum eallum eall þæt hy ær ahton, and his wife
and his dohtor swa full and swa forð swa hi ahton, and hi fæstnedon þa
fulne freondscipe heom betweonan, and allum folce fulle lagu beheton, and
geutlagedon ealle þa Frenciscean þe ær unlagon rærdon, and undom
demdon, and unræd ræddan into ðissum earde, buton swa fela swa hi
geræddon þæt þam cynge gelicode mid him to habbenne, þe him
getreowe wæron and eallum his folce.
 1052.2.62. And Rodbeard arcebiscop and Willelm biscop and Ulf
biscop uneaðe ætburstan mid þam Frenciscean mannum þe him mid
wæron, and swa ofer sæ comon.
 1053.1. Her wæs se micla wind on Þomes mæsseniht, and eac
eall þa midewinter wæs mycel wind.
 1053.2. And man rædde þæt man sloh Ris þæs Wyliscean
cynges broþer for ðy he hearmas dyde, and man brohte his heafod to
Glewcestre on Twelftan æfen.
 1053.5. And þæs ylcan geres foran to Alra Halgena mæssan
forðferde Wulfsyg biscop æt Licetfelda, and Godwine abbod on Wincelcumbe,
and Ægelward abbod on Glestingabyrig, ealle binnan anum monþe.
 1053.8. And Leofwine feng to þam biscoprice æt Licedfelde, and
Aldret biscop feng to þam abbodrice on Wincelcumbe, and Ægelnað feng to
þam abbodrice on Glestincgabyrig.
 1053.11. And þæs ylcan geres forðferde Ælfric, Oddan
broðer, on Deorhyrste, and his lichama resteð on Perscore.
 1053.12. And þæs ylcan geres forðferde Godwine eolr, and him
geyfelode þær he mid þam cynge sæt on Wincestre, and Harold his sunu
feng to þam eorldome þe his fæder ær hæfde, and Ælfgar eorl
feng to þam eorldome þe Harold ær hæfde.
 1054.1. Her ferde Siward eolr mid miclum here on Scotland,
ægðer ge mid scyphere and mid landfyrde, and feaht wið Scottas, and
aflymde þone kyng Macbeoðen, and ofsloh eall þæt þær betst wæs
on þam lande, and lædde þonan micele herehuðe swilce nan man ær ne
begeat, ac his sunu Osbarn, and his sweostor suna  Sihward, and of his
huscarlum and eac þæs cynges wurdon þær ofslægene on þone dæg
<foreign>Septem Dormientium</foreign>.
 1054.8. Ðæs ilcan geres for Aldred biscop to Colne ofer sæ
þæs kynges ærende, and wearð þær underfangen mid mycclan
weorðscipe fram þan casere, and þær he wunode wel neh an ger, and him
geaf ægðer þeneste ge se biscop on Colone and se casere.
 1054.12. And he lofode Leofwine biscope to halgianne þæt
mynster æt Eofeshamme on <foreign>vi Idus Octobris</foreign>.
 1054.13. And on þisan geare swalt Osgod færinga on his bedde.
 1054.14. And her forðferde Sanctus Leo papa, and Victor wæs to
papa gecoren on his stede.
 1055.1. On þisan gere forðferde Syhward eorl on Eoferwic, and
he ligeð æt Galmaho on þam mynstre þe he sylf let timbrian and halgian
on Godes and Olafes naman.
 1055.3. And Tosti feng to þan eorldome þe he hæfde.
 1055.4. And Kynsie arcebiscop fette his <foreign>pallium</foreign> æt Victore
papan.
 1055.5. And þæræfter sona man utlagode Ælfgar eorl,
Leofrices sunu eorles, forneh butan gylte, ac he gewende to Hirlande and
Brytlande, and begeat him þær micel genge, and ferde swa to Hereforda, ac
him com þær togenes Raulf eorl mid mycclan here, and mid lytlan gewinne hi
on fleam gebrohte, and micel folc on þan fleame ofsloh, and gewendon þa
into Herefordporte and forhergode þæt, and forbærnde þæt mære
mynster þe Æþelstan biscop getimbrode, and ofsloh þa preostas innan
þam mynstre, and manege þærtoeacan, and namon þærinne ealle þa
maðmas, and mid heom aweglæddon.
 1055.15. And þa þa hi hæfdon mæst to yfele gedon man
gerædde þone ræd þæt man Ælfgar eorl geinnlagode, and ageaf him
his eorldom and ealle þæt him of genumen wæs.
 1055.18. Ðeos hergung wæs geworden on <foreign>nonas Kalendas
Nouembris</foreign>.
 1055.19. On þam ilcan geare forðferde Tremerin se Wylisca
biscop sona æfter þære hergunge, and he wæs Æþelstanes biscop
gespelia siððan he unfere wæs.
 1056.1. Her forlet Ægelric bisceop his bisceoprice æt Dunholm
and ferde to Burh to Sancte Petres mynstre, and his broðor Ægelwine feng
ðærto, and eac her forðferde Æðelstan biscop on <foreign>iiii Idus
Februarii</foreign>, and his lic lið on Herforda, and man sette Lefegar to biscop, se
wæs Haroldes eorles mæssepreost, and on his preosthade he hæfde his
kenepas oð þæt he biscop wæs.
 1056.6. Se forlet his crisman and his rode and his gastlican
wæpnu, and feng to his spere and to his swurde, and swa for to ferde ongean
Griffin þone Wyliscan cining, and he wearð þær ofslagen, and his
preostes mid him, and Ælfnoð scirgerefa, and manega oðre gode men.
 1056.11. Þis wæs ehtan nihte ær middansumere, and Ealdred
bisceop feng to ðam biscoprice þe Leofegar hæfde <foreign>xi</foreign> wucan and <foreign>iiii</foreign>
dagas.
 1056.13. Ðæs geares forðferde Odda eorl, and he lið on
Perscora, se wæs to muneca gehadod ær his ende, god man and clæne and
swiðe æðele, and he gewat on <foreign>ii Kalendas Septembris</foreign>.
 1056.16. And Cona se casere forðferde.
 1057.1. Her com Eadward æþeling to Englalande, se wæs
Eadwerdes broðor sunu kynges, Eadmund cing, Irensid wæs geclypod for his
snellscipe.
 1057.5. Þisne æþeling Cnut cyng hæfde forsend on
Ungerland to beswicane, ac he þær geþeh to godan men, swa him God uðe,
and him wel gebyrede, swa þæt he begeat þæs caseres maga to wife, and
bi þære fægerne bearnteam gestrynde, seo wæs Agathes gehaten.
 1057.12. Ne wiston we for hwylcan intingan þæt gedon
wærð, þæt he ne moste his mæges Eadweardes cynges geseon.
 1057.15. Wala, þæt wæs hreowlic sið and hearmlic eallre
þissere þeode, þæt he swa raðe his lif geendade, þæs þe he to
Englalande com, for ungesælhðe þissere earman þeode.
 1057.20. On þan ilcan gere forðferde Leofric eorl on <foreign>ii
Kalendas Octobris</foreign>, se wæs swiðe wis for Gode and eac for worulde,
þæt fremode eallre þisre ðeode.
 1057.22. He lið æt Cofentreo, and his sunu Ælfgar feng to
his rice.
 1057.23. And on þam geare forðferde Raulf eorl on <foreign>xii Kalendas
Ianuarii</foreign>, and lið on Burh.
 1057.24. Eac gefor Heca biscop on Suðsexum, and Ægelric wæs
on setl ahafen.
 1057.25. And her Victor papa forðferde, and Stefanus wæs to
papa gecoren.
 1058.1. Her man ytte ut Ælfgar eorl, ac he com sona inn ongean
mid strece þurh Gryffines fultum.
 1058.2. And her com scyphere of Norwegan.
 1058.3. Hit is langsum to atellanne eall hu hit gefaren wæs.
 1058.4. On þam ilcan gere Ealdred biscop halgode þæt mynster
on Gleawcestre þe he sylf geforðode, Gode to lofe and Sancte Petre, and swa
ferde to Hierusalem mid swilcan weorðscipe swa nan oðer ne dyde ætforan
him, and hine sylfne þær Gode betæhte, and wurðlic lac eac geoffrode
to ures Drihtenes byrgene, þæt wæs an gylden calic on fif marcon,
swiðe wundorlices geworces.
 1058.10. On þam ilcan gere forðferde Stefanus papa, and
Benedictus wæs to papan geset, se sende <foreign>pallium</foreign> Stigande biscope.
 1058.12. And Ægelric wæs to biscope gehadod to Suðsexum,
and Sihward abbod to biscoppe to Hrofecestre.
 1059.1. Her on þisan gere wæs Nicolaus gecoren to papan, se
wæs biscop ær æt Florentia þære burh, and Benedictus wæs ut
adryfen þe þær wæs ær papa.
 1059.3. And on þisan gere wæs se stypel gehalgad æt Burh on
<foreign>xvi Kalendas Nouembris</foreign>.
 1060.1. On þisan gere wæs micel eorðdyne on <foreign>Translatione
Sancti Martini</foreign>.
 1060.2. And Heinric se cyng forðferde on Francrice.
 1060.2. And Kynsie arcebiscop on Eoferwic gewat on <foreign>xi Kalendas
Ianuarii</foreign>, and he ligeð on Burh, and Ealdred biscop feng to þam rice, and
Waltere feng to þam biscoprice on Herefordscire, and Duduc biscop eac

 1061.1. Her for Ealdred biscop to Rome æfter his <foreign>pallium</foreign>, and
he hine underfeng æt þam papan Nicolae, and se eorl Tostig and his wif eac
foron to Rome, and se bisceop and se eorl gebidan mycele earfoðnysse þa hi
hamward foran.
 1061.4. And her forðferde Godwine biscop æt Sancte Martine,
and Wulfric abbod æt Sancte Agustine <foreign>iiii x Kalendas Aprilis</foreign>.
 1061.6. And Nicolaus papa forðferde, and Alexander wæs to
papan gecoron, se wæs biscop æt Lucan.
 1063.1. On þissum geare for Harold eorl æfter middanwintre of
Gleaweceastre to Rudelan, þe Griffines wæs, and þone ham forbærnde,
and his scipa and alle þa gewæda þe þærto gebyrede, and hine on
fleame gebrohte, and þa to þam gongdagan for Harold mid scipum of
Brycgstowe abutan Brytland, and þæt folc griþede and gisledon, and
Tostig for mid landferde ongean, and þæt land geeodon.
 1063.7. Ac her on ðissan ilcan geare on herfeste wearþ Griffin
kync ofslangen on <foreign>Nonas Agusti</foreign> fram his agenum mannum, þurh þæt gewinn
þe he won wiþ Harold eorl, se wæs kyning ofer eall Wealcyn, and man
brohte his eafod to Harolde eorle, and Harold hit þam kynge brohte, and his
scipes heafod, and þa bone þermid, and se kyng Eadward betæhte þæt
land his twam gebroþran Bleþgente and Rigwatlan, and hig aþas sworon and
gislas saldan þæm cynge and þæm eorle þæt heo him on allum
þingum unswicende beon woldon, and eighwar him gearwe on wætere and on
lande, and swylc of þam lande gelæstan swylc man dyde tofor an ær
oþrum kynge.
 1065.1. Her on þisum geare foran to Hlafmæssan het Harold eorl
bytlian on Brytlande æt Portaschið þa þa he hit gegan hæfde, and
þær mycel god to gegaderode, and þohte þone cyng Eadward þær to
habbane for huntoðes þingon.
 1065.4. Ac þa hit eall wæs gearo þa for Cradoc to, Gryffines
sunu, mid eallon þam genge þe he begeotan mihte, and þæt folc eall
mæst ofsloh þe þær timbrode, and þæt god þe þær gegearcod
wæs namon.
 1065.8. Ne wisten we hwa þone unræd ærest gerædde.
 1065.8. Þis wæs gedon on Sancte Bartholomeus mæssedæg.
 1065.9. And sona æfter þisan gegaderedon þa þegenas hi
ealle on Eoforwicscire and on Norðhymbralande togædere, and geutlagedan
heora eorl Tosti, and ofslogon his hiredmen, ealle þe hig mihten to cumen,
ægþær ge Englisce ge Denisce, and naman ealle his wæpna on Eaforwic,
and gold and seolfer and ealle his sceattas þe hig mihton ahwær þær
geacsian, and sendon æfter Morkere, Ælfgares sunu eorles, and gecuron
hine heom to eorle, and he for suð mid ealre þære scire, and mid
Snotinghamscire, and Deorbyscire, and Lincolnascire, oð he com to Hamtune,
and his broþor Eadwine him com togeanes mid þam mannum þe on his eorldome
weron, and eac fela Brettas comon mid him.
 1065.21. Þer com Harold eorl heom togeanes and hig lægdon
ærende on hine to þam cyninge Eadwarde, and eac ærendracan mid him
sendon, and bædon þæt hi moston habban Morkere heom to eorle, and se
cyning þæs geuðæ, and sende æfter Haralde heom to to Hamtune on
Sancte Symones and Iuda mæsseæfen, and kyðde heom þæt ilce, and
heom þæt a hand sealde, and he nywade þær Cnutes lage.
 1065.27. And þa Ryðrenan dydan mycelne hearm abutan Hamtune
þa hwile þe he for heora ærende, ægþær þæt hi of slogon
menn and bærndon hus and corn and namon eall þæt orf þe hig mihton to
cuman, þæt wæs feola þusend, and fela hund manna hi naman, and
læddan norð mid heom, swa þæt seo scir and þa oðra scira þæ
ðærn eah sindon wurdon fela wintra ðe wyrsan.
 1065.34. And Tostig eorl and his wif, and ealle þa ðe woldon
þæt he wolde, faran suð ofer sæ mid him to Baldwine eorle, and he hi
ealle underfengc, and hig wæron ealne þone winter þær.
 1065.37. And Eadward cyng com to Westmynstre to þam middanwintre,
and þet mynster þær let halgian þe he silf getimbrode, Gode to lofe
and Sancte Petre and eallum Godes halgum, and seo cyrichalgung wæs on Cilda
mæssædeg.
 1065.40. And he forðferde on Twelftan æfen, and hine man
bebyrigde on Twelftan dæg on þam illcan minstre, swa hit her æfter
sægð.
 1065.43. And her wearð Harold eorl eac to cynge gehalgod, and he
lytle stilnesse þæron gebad þa hwile þe he rices weold.
 1066.1. On þissum geare com Harold cyng of Eoforwic to
Westmynstre to þam Eastran þe wæron æfter þam middanwintre þe se
cyng forðferde, and wæron þa Eastran on þone dæg <foreign>xvi Kalendas
Maias</foreign>.
 1066.4. Þa wearð geond eall Englaland swylc tacen on heofenum
gesewen swylce nan man ær ne geseah.
 1066.5. Sume men cwedon þæt hit cometa se steorra wære,
þone sume men hatað þone fæxedon steorran, and he æteowde ærest
on þone æfen <foreign>Letania Maior viii Kalendas Maias</foreign>, and swa scan ealle þa
seofon niht.
 1066.9. And sona þeræfter com Tostig eorl in fram begeonde
sæ into Wiht mid swa miclum liðe swa he begitan mihte, and him man geald
þær ægþær ge feoh ge metsunge.
 1066.12. And Harold cyng, his broþor, gegædrade swa micelne
sciphere and eac landhere swa nan cyng her on lande ær ne dyde, for þam
þe him wæs gecyðd þæt Wyllelm bastard wolde hider and ðis land
gewinnen, ealls wa hit syððan aeode.
 1066.15. And þa wile com Tostig eorl into Humbran mid sixtigum
scipum, and Eadwine eorl com mid lanferde and adraf hine ut, and þa
butsacarlas hine forsocan, and he for to Scotlande mid xii snaccum, and hine
gemette þær Harold cyng of Norwegon mid þreom hund scypum, and Tostig
him to beah and his man wearð, and hi foron þa begen into Humbran, oð
þæt hi comon to Eoforwic, and heom þær wið fuhton Eadwine eorl and
Morkere eorl, his broðor, ac þa Normen ahton sige.
 1066.24. Man cyðde þa Harolde, Engla cynge, þæt þis
wæs þus gefaren, and þis gefeoht wæs on <foreign>Uigilia Sancti Mathei</foreign>.
 1066.25. Ða com Harold ure cyng on unwær on þa Normenn and
hytte hi begeondan Eoforwic æt Steinford Brygge mid micclan here Englisces
folces, and þær wearð on dæg swiðe stranglic gefeoht on ba halfe.
 1066.29. Þar wearð ofslægen Harold Harfagera, and Tosti
eorl, and þa Normen þe þær to lafe wæron wurdon on fleame, and þa
Engliscan hi hindan hetelice slogon, oð þæt hig sume to scype coman,
sume adruncen, and sume eac forbærnde, and swa mislice forfarene þæt
þær wæs lyt to lafe, and Engle ahton wælstowe geweald.
 1066.34. Se kyng þa geaf gryð Olafe, þæs Norna cynges
suna, and heora biscoppe, and þan eorle of Orcanege, and eallon þan þe on
þam scypum to lafe wæron, and hi foron þa upp to uran kyninge, and
sworon aðas þæt hi æfre woldon fryð and freondscype into þisan
lande haldan, and se cyng hi let ham faran mid <foreign>xxiiii</foreign> scypum.
 1066.39. Þas twa folcgefeoht wæron gefremmede binnan fif
nihtan.
 1066.40. Ða com Wyllelm eorl of Normandige into Pefnesea on
Sancte Michæles mæsseæfen, and sona þæs hi fere wæron, worhton
castel æt Hæstingaport.
 1066.43. Þis wearð þa Harolde cynge gecydd, and he gaderade
þa mycelne here, and com him togenes æt þære haran apuldran, and
Wyllelm him com ongean on unwær, ær þis folc gefylced wære.
 1066.46. Ac se kyng þeah him swiðe heardlice wið feaht mid
þam mannum þe him gelæstan woldon, and þær wearð micel wæl
geslægen on ægðre healfe.
 1066.48. Ðær wearð ofslægen Harold kyng, and Leofwine
eorl his broðor, and Gyrð eorl his broðor, and fela godra manna, and þa
Frencyscan ahton wælstowe geweald, eallswa heom God uðe for folces
synnon.
 1066.51. Aldred arcebiscop and seo burhwaru on Lundene woldon
habban þa Eadgar cild to kynge, eallswa him wel gecynde wæs, and Eadwine
and Morkere him beheton þæt hi mid him feohtan woldon, ac swa hit æfre
forðlicor beon sceolde swa wearð hit fram dæge to dæge lætre and
wyrre eallswa hit æt þam ende eall geferde.
 1066.57. Þis gefeoht wæs gedon on þone dæg Calesti pape.
 1066.57. And Wyllelm eorl for eft ongean to Hæstingan, and
geanbidode þær hwæðer man him to bugan wolde, ac þa he ongeat
þæt man him to cuman nolde, he for upp mid eallon his here þe him to
lafe wæs, and him syððan fram ofer sæ com, and hergade ealne þone
ende þe he oferferde, oð þæt he com to Beorhhamstede, and þær him
com ongean Ealdred arcebiscop, and Eadgar cild, and Eadwine eorl, and Morkere
eorl, and ealle þa betstan men of Lundene, and bugon þa for neode þa
mæst wæs to hearme gedon, and þæt wæs micel unræd þæt man
æror swa ne dyde, þa hit God betan nolde for urum synnum, and gysledan and
sworon him aðas, and he heom behet þæt he wolde heom hold hlaford beon,
and þeah onmang þisan hi hergedan eall þæt hi oferforon.
 1066.70. Ða on midwintres dæg hine halgode to kynge Ealdred
arcebiscop on Westmynstre, and he sealde him on hand mid Christes bec and eac
swor, ær þan þe he wolde þa corona him on heafode settan, þæt he
wolde þisne þeodscype swa wel haldan swa ænig kyngc ætforan him betst
dyde, gif hi him holde beon woldon.
 1066.75. Swaþeah leide gyld on mannum swiðe stið, and for
þa on þam lengtene ofer sæ to Normandige, and nam mid him Stigand
arcebiscop, and Ægelnað abbod on Glæstingabiri, and Eadgar cild, and
Eadwine eorl, and Morkere eorl, and Wælþeof eorl, and manege oðre gode
men of Englalande, and Oda biscop and Wyllelm eorl belifen her æfter and
worhton castelas wide geond þas þeode, and earm folc swencte, and a
syððan hit yflade swiðe.
 1066.82. Wurðe god se ende þonne God wylle.
 1067.1. Her com se kyng eft ongean to Englalande on Sancte Nicolaes
mæssedæge.
 1067.2. And þæs dæges forbarn Cristes cyrce on
Cantwarebyri.
 1067.3. And Wulfwi biscop forðferde, and is bebyrged æt his

 1067.4. And Eadric cild and þa Bryttas wurdon unsehte and wunnon
heom wið þa castelmenn on Hereforda, and fela hearmas heom dydon.
 1067.6. And her se kyng sette micel gyld on earm folc, and
þeahhwæðre let æfre herigan eall þæt hi oferforon, and þa he
ferde to Defenascire and besæt þa burh Exancester <foreign>xviii</foreign> dagas, and
þær wearð micel his heres forfaren, ac he heom wel behet, and yfele
gelæste, and hig him þa burh ageafon, for þan þa þegen as heom
geswicon hæfdon.
 1067.11. And þæs sumeres Eadgar cild for ut mid his modor
Agatha, and his twam sweostran, Margareta and Christina, and Mærlaswegen,
and fela godra manna mid heom, and comon to Scotlande on Malcholomes cyninges
gryð, and he hi ealle underfeng.
 1067.15. Ða begann se cyngc Malcholom gyrnan his sweostor him to
wife, Margaretan, ac he and his men ealle lange wiðcwædon, and eac heo
sylf wiðsoc, and cwæð þæt heo hine ne nanne habban wolde, gyf hire
seo uplice arfæstnys geunnan wolde, þæt heo on mægðhade mihtigan
Drihtne mid lichomlicre heortan on þisan life sceortan on clænre
forhæfednysse cweman mihte.
 1067.24. Se kyng befealh georne hire breðer oð þæt he
cwæð ia wið, and eac he elles ne dorste, for þan þe hi on his anwald
becumene wæron.
 1067.26. Hit wearð þa swa geworden swa God foresceawode on
ær, and elles hit beon ne mihte, eallswa he sylf on his godspelle sæið
þæt furðon an spearwa on gryn ne mæg befeallan forutan his
foresceawunge.
 1067.29. Se forewitola Scyppend wiste on ær hwæt he of hyre
gedon habban wolde, for þan þe heo sceolde on þan lande Godes lof
geeacnian/ and þone kyng gerihtan of þam dweliandan pæðe and gebegean
hine to beteran wege and his leode samod, and alegcean þa unþeawas þe seo
þeod ær beeode, eallswa heo syððan dyde.
 1067.35. Se kyng hi þa underfeng, þeah hit hire unþances
wære, and him gelicade hire þeawas, and þancode Gode þe him swylce
gemæccean mihtiglice forgeaf, and wislice hine beþohte, swa he full witter
wæs, and awende hine sylfne to Gode, and ælce unsiuernysse oferhogode.
 1067.39. Be þam se apostol Paulus, ealra þeoda lareow,
cwæð, <foreign>Saluabitur uir infidelis per mulierem fidelem, sic et mulier
infidelis per uirum fidelem et reliqua</foreign>, þæt is on uran geþeode, Ful oft
se ungeleaffulla wer bið gehalgad and gehæled þurh þæt rihtwise
wif, and swa gelice þæt wif þurh geleaffulne wer.
 1067.44. Ðeos foresprecene cwen seoððan on þam lande manege
nytwyrðe dæda gefremede Gode to lofe, and eac on þa kynewisan wel
geþeh, eallswa hire gecynde wæs.
 1067.47. Of geleaffullan and æðelan cynne heo wæs
asprungon, hire fæder wæs Eadward æþeling, Eadmundes sunu kynges,
Eadmund Æþelreding, Æþelred Eadgaring, Eadgar Eadreding, and swa
forð on þæt cynecynn, and hire modorcynn gæð to Heinrice casere,
þe hæfde anwald ofer Rome.
 1067.51. And her ferde Gyða ut, Haroldes modor, and manegra godra
manna wif mid hyre, into Bradan Reolice, and þær wunode sume hwile, and
swa for þanon ofer sæ to Sancte Audomare.
 1067.54. On þisan Eastron com se kyng to Wincestre, and þa
wæron Eastra on <foreign>x Kalendas Aprilis</foreign>, and sona æfter þam com Mathild
seo hlæfdie hider to lande, and Ealdred arcebiscop hig gehalgode to cwene on
Westmynstre on Hwitan Sunnandæg.
 1067.58. Þa kyðde man þan kyninge þæt þæt folc
benorðan hæfdon heom gegaderad togædere, and woldan him ongean standan,
gif he come.
 1067.60. He for þa to Snotingaham, and worhte þær castel,
and for swa to Eoferwic, and þær worhte twegen castelas, and on Lincolna
and gehwar on þan ende, and Gospatric eorl and þa betstan men foron into
Scotlande.
 1067.64. And amang þisan com an Haroldes suna of Yrlande mid
scyphere into Afenan muðan unwær, and hergode sona ofer eall þone ende,
foron þa to Brygcstowe, and þa burh abrecan woldon, ac seo burhwaru heom he
ardlice wið feaht, and þa hi ne mihton of þære burh naht gewinnan, hi
foron þa to scypan mid þan þe hi gehergod hæfdon, and swa hi foron on
Sumersæton, and þær upp eodon, and Eadnoð stallere heom wið ge
feaht, and wearð þær ofslægen, and manege gode menn on ægðre
healfe, and þanon aweig foron þe þær to lafe wæron.
 1068.1. Her on þissum geare Willelm cyngc geaf Rodbearde eorle
þone ealdordom ofer Norðhymbraland, ac þa landes menn hine beforon innan

 1068.4. And sona þæræfter Eadgar æðeling com mid

 1068.6. And Wyllelm kyng com suðan on unwær on heom mid

 1068.11. Æfter þisum coman Haroldes sunas of Yrlande to þam

 1068.17. Her forðferde Aldred arcebiscop on Eoferwic, and is
þær bebyrged æt his biscopstole, and he gewat on þone dæg Proti
<foreign>et</foreign> Iacinthi, and he heold þone arcestol mid mycclan weorðmynte <foreign>x</foreign> gear
buton <foreign>xv </foreign> wucan wanan.
 1068.21. Sona þæræfter coman of Denmarcon þreo Swegenes
suna kyninges, mid cc scypum and xl, and Esbeorn eorl, and Þurkyl eorl, into
Humbran/, and heom com þær togenes Eadgar cild and Waldþeof eorl, and
Mærleswegen, and Gospatric eorl mid Norðhymbrum, and ealle þa

burh forbærned, and eac þæt halie mynster Sanctus Petrus eall forhergod
and forbærned.
 1068.33. Þa se kyng þis geaxode, þa for he norðward mid
ealre his fyrde þe he gegaderian mihte, and þa scire mid ealle forhergode
and aweste, and þæt lið læig ealne winter innan Humbre, þær se
kyng heom to cuman ne mihte.
 1068.37. And se kyng wæs þone midwintres dæig on Eoferwic,
and swa ealne þone winter on þam lande, and com to Wincestre on þa ilcan
Eastron.
 1068.39. And Ægelric biscop wæs forwreged, þe wæs on
Burh, and hine man lædde to Westmynstre, and utlagode his broðor
Ægelwine biscop.
 1071.1. Her se eorl Wælþeof gryðode wið þone cyngc.
 1071.1. And þæs on lengten se kyngc let hergian ealle þa
mynstra þe on Englalande wæron.
 1071.3. And þæs geres wæs micel hunger.
 1071.3. And man hergade þæt mynster æt Burh, þæt
wæron þa menn þe se biscop Ægelric ær amansumade, for þon þe
hi namon þær eall þæt he ahte.
 1071.6. And þæs ilcan sumeres com þæt lið into Temese,
and lagon þær twa niht, and heoldon syððan to Denmar con.
 1071.7. And Baldawine eorl forðferde, and Arnulf his sunu feng to
þan rice, and Francena kyning and Wyllelm eorl sceoldon beon his geheald, ac
þær com Rodbeart, and ofsloh Arnulf his mæig, and þone eorl 
Wyllelm, and þone kyngc aflymde, and ofsloh his manna fela þusenda.
 1072.1. Her Eadwine eorl and Morkere eorl hlupon ut, and mislice
ferdon on wuda and on feldon oð þæt Eadwine wearð ofslægen fram his
agenum mannum, and Morkere mid scype gewende to Helig, and þær com
Ægelwine biscop, and Sigwarð Barn, and fela hund manna mid heom.
 1072.5. Ac þa se kyngc Wyllelm þis geahsade, þa bead he ut
scypfyrde and landfyrde, and þæt land eall utan embsette, and brygce
worhte, and scypfyrde on þa sæhealfe, and hi ealle þa eodon þan
kyninge on hand, þæt wæs Ægelwine biscop and Morkere eorl and ealle
þa þe mid heom wæron, buton Herewerde anum and ealle þa þe mid him
ætfleon mihton, and he hi ahtlice ut alædde.
 1072.11. And se kyng nam heora scypa and wæpna and manega
sceattas, and þa menn ealle he toc, and dyde of heom þæt he wolde, and
Ægelwine biscop he sende to Abbandune, and he þær forðferde.
 1073.1. Her Wyllelm kyng lædde scypferde and landfyrde to
Scotlande, and þæt land on þa sæhealfe mid scypum ymblæig, and him
sylf mid his landfyrde ferde inn ofer þæt wæð, and he þær naht
ne funde þæs þe heom þe betere wære, and Malcolm cyngc com and
gryðode wið Wyllelm cyngc, and wæs his man, and him gyslas salde, and he
syððan ham gewende mid ealre his fyrde.
 1073.7. And se biscop Ægelric forðferde, he wæs to biscoppe
gehadod to Eoferwic, ac hit wæs mid unrihte him of genumen, and geaf him
þæt biscoprice æt Dunholme, and he hit hæfde þa hwile þe he
wolde, and forlet hit syððan, and ferde to Burh to Sancte Petres mynstre,
and þær drohtnode <foreign>xii</foreign> gear.
 1073.12. Þa æfter þam þe Wyllelm gewann Englaland, he let
hine nyman of Burh, and sende hine to Westmynstre, and he þær forðferde
on <foreign>Idus Octobris</foreign>, and is þær bebyrged innan Sancte Nicolaes portice.
 1074.1. On þisan gere Willelm cyngc lædde Englisce fyrde and
Frencisce ofer sæ, and gewann þæt land Mans, and hit Englisce menn
swiðe amærdon, wingeardas hi fordydon, and burga forbærndan, and
þæt land swiðe amyrdon, and eall þæt land gebegdan þan kyninge to
handan, and hig seoððan ham gewendan.
 1075.1. On þissum gere Wyllelm cyngc for ofer sæ to
Normandige.
 1075.2. And Eadgar cild com of Fleminga lande into Scotlande on
Sancte Grimbaldes mæssedæg, and se kyngc Malcholom and his sweostor
Margareta hine underfengon mid mycclan weorðscype.
 1075.5. On þære ilcan tide sende se kyng of Francrice,
Filippus, gewrit to him, and bead him þæt he to him come, and he wolde
geofan him þone castel æt Mustræl, þæt he mihte syððan
dæghwamlice his unwinan unþancas don.
 1075.9. Hwæt þa se cyngc Malcolm and his sweoster Margareta
geafon him myccla geofa and manega gærsama and eallon his mannan, on scynnan
mid pælle betogen, and on merðerne pyleceon, and graschynnene, and hearm
ascynnene, and on pællon, and on gyldenan faton, and on seolfrenan, and hine
and ealle his scyperan mid mycclan weorðscipe of his gryðe alædde.
 1075.15. Ac on þære fare heom yfele gelamp, þa hi ut on
sæ wæron, þæt heom on becom swiðe hreoh weder, and seo wode sæ
and se stranga wind hi on þæt land awearp þæt ealle heora scypa
toburston, and hi sylfe earforðlice to lande coman, and heora gærsama
forneh eall losade, and his men eac wurdon sume gelæhtæ of Frencyscan
mannan, ac he sylf and his ferestan menn ferdon eft ongean to Scotlande, sume
hreowlice on fotan gangende, and sume earmlice ridende.
 1075.22. Ða gerædde se kyngc Malcholom him þæt he sende
to Wyllelme cynge ofer sæ, and bæde his gryðes, and he eac swa dyde,
and se cyngc him þæs getiðade, and æfter him sende.
 1075.25. And se kyngc eft Malcolm and his sweostor him and eallon
his mannan unarimede gærsama geafon, and swiðe weorðlice hine eft of
heora gryðe sendon.
 1075.28. And se scirgerefa of Eoferwic com him togeanes æt
Dunholme, and ferde ealne weig mid him, and let him findan mete and foddor
æt ælcan castelle þær hi to comon, oð þæt hig ofer sæ to
þam kynige coman.
 1075.31. And se kyngc Wyllelm mid micclan weorðscype þa hine
underfengc, and he wæs þær þa on his hirede, and toc swilce gerihta
swa he him gelagade.
 1076.1. On þissan geare Wyllelm cyngc geaf Raulfe eorle Wyllelmes
dohtor, Osbarnes sunu, and se ylca Raulf wæs Bryttisc on his modor healfe,
and Rawulf his fæder wæs Englisc, and wæs geboren on Norðfolce, and
se kyngc geaf for þi his suna þær þone eorldom, and Suðfolc eac.
 1076.5. He þa lædde þæt wif to Norðwic, þær wæs
þæt brydealo, þæt wæs manegra manna bealo.
 1076.9. Ðær wæs Rogcer eorl, and Walþeof eorl, and
biscopas, and abbodas, and ræddon þær þæt hi woldon heora
kynehlaford of his cynerice adrifan, and þis wæs þam kyninge sona to
Normandie gecyðed.
 1076.12. Rawulf eorl and Rogcer eorl wæron hofdingas æt
þisan unræde, and hi speonon heom to þa Bryttas, and sendan eac to
Denemarcon æfter scyphere, and Rogcer ferde west to his eorldome, and
gaderade his folc þan cyngce to unþearfe, he þohte, ac hit wearð heom
seolfan to mycclan hearme.
 1076.17. Rawulf eac wolde mid his eorldome forðgan, ac þa
castelmenn þe wæron on Englalande, and eac þæt land folc, heom
togenes comon, and hi ealle geletton þæt hi naht ne dydon, ac wæs
fægen þæt he to scypum æt fleah.
 1076.21. And his wif belaf æfter in þam castele, and hine swa
lange heold oð þæt man hire gryð salde, and heo þa ut ferde of
Englalande, and ealle hire menn þe hire mid woldon.
 1076.24. And se kyngc syððan com to Englalande and gefeng
Rogcer eorl his mæg, and sette on prisun.
 1076.25. And Walþeof eorl ferde ofer sæ, and wreide hine
sylfne, and bæd forgyfenysse, and bead gærsuman.
 1076.27. Ac se kyngc let lihtlice of oð þæt he com to
Englalande, and hine let syððan tacan.
 1076.28. And sona æfter þisan coman of Denemarcon twa hund
scypa, þæron on wæron heafdesmenn Cnut, Swegnes sunu cynges, and Hacon
eorl, and ne dorston nan gefeoht healdan wið Willelme cynge, ac ferdon to
Eoforwic, and bræcon Sancte Petres mynster, and tocon þærinne mycele
æhta, and foron swa aweg, ac ealle þa forferdon þe æt þam ræde
wæron, þæt wæs Hacones sunu eorles, and manege oðre mid him.
 1076.35. And Eadgyð seo hlæfdie forðferde, seo wæs
Eadwardes cynges geresta, seofon niht ær Christesmæssan on Wincestre, and
se cyngc hig let bryngan to Westmynstre mid mycclan weorðscype, and leide heo
wið Eadwarde cynge hire hlaforde.
 1076.39. Se kyngc wæs þa þone midwinter on Westmynstre,
þær mon fordemde ealle þa Bryttas þe wæron æt þam brydlope
æt Norðwic, sume hi wurdon geblende, and sume wrecen of lande, and sume
getawod to scande.
 1076.45. Þus wurdon þæs kyninges swican genyðerade.
 1077.1. On þisan geare forðferde Swegen kyngc on Denemarcon,
and Harold his sunu feng to his cynerice.
 1077.2. Her Wyllelm cyngc geaf þæt abbodrice æt Westmynstre
Fiþele abbode, and se wæs ær munuc æt Bernege.
 1077.4. And her wæs Walþeof eorl beheafdod on Wincestre on
Sancte Petronella mæssedæg, and his lic wearð gelæd to Crulande, and
he þær is bebyrged.
 1077.7. And Wyllelm cyngc for ofer sæ, and lædde fyrde to
Brytlande, and besæt þone castel æt Dol, ac þa  Bryttas hine heoldon
oð þæt se cyngc com of Francrice, and Wyllelm cyngc þa þanon for,
and þær forleas ægðer menn and hors and unarimede gærsaman.
 1078.1. Her se mona aþystrode þreom nihton ær
Candelmæssan.
 1078.2. And Ægelwig se woruldsnotra abbod on Eofeshamme
forðferde on Sancta Iuliana mæssedæg, and Waltere wæs to abbod geset
on his stede, and Hereman biscop forðferde, se wæs biscop on Bearrucscire
and on Wiltunscire and on Dorsætan.
 1078.5. And her Malcholom kyngc gewann Mælslæhtan modor and
ealle his betstan menn and ealne his gærsuman and his orf.
 1078.8. And he sylf uneaðe ætbærst.
 1078.9. And her wæs se dria sumor, and wilde fyr com on manega
scira, and forbærnde fela tuna, and eac manega burga forburnon.
 1079.1. Her Rodbert, þæs cynges sunu Willelm, hleop fram his
fæder to his eame Rotbryhte on Flandron, for þan þe his fæder ne
wolde him lætan waldan his eorldomes on Normandige þe he sylf and eac se
kyng Filippus mid his geþafunge him gegyfen hæfdon, and þa þe betst
wæron on þam lande hæfdon aðas him gesworon, and hine to hlaforde
genumen.
 1079.6. Her Rotbert feht wið his fæder, and hine on þa hand
gewundade, and his hors wearð under ofscoten, and se þe him oðer to
brohte wearð þærrihte mid anan arblaste ofscoten, þæt wæs Tokig,
Wiggodes sunu, and fela þær wurdon ofslægen, and eac gefangene, and
Robert eft gewende to Fleminga lande.
 1079.11. Ne wylle we þeh her na mare scaðe awritan þe he his
fæder ge.
 1080.1. Her werþ Anagus ofsleien fram Scotta eere and þer
werþ micel weell ofsleigen mid him.
 1080.2. Þer wes codes riþt gesochen on him for þet he wes all
forswoorn.

 0.1. Brittene igland is ehta hund mila lang. & twa hund brad.
& her sind on þis iglande fif geþeode. Englisc. & Brittisc. &
Wilsc. & Scyttisc. & Pyhtisc. & Boc Leden.
 0.3. Erest weron bugend þises landes Brittes. þa coman of
Armenia. & gesætan suðewearde Bryttene ærost.
 0.5. Þa gelamp hit þæt Pyhtas coman suþan of Scithian. mid
langum scipum na manegum. & þa coman ærost on norþ Ybernian up.
& þær bædon Scottas þæt hi ðer moston wunian.
 0.8. Ac hi noldan heom lyfan. forðan hi cwædon þæt hi ne
mihton ealle ætgædere gewunian þær. & þa cwædon þa
Scottas. we eow magon þeah hwaðere ræd gelæron.
 0.11. We witan oþer egland her be easton. þer ge magon eardian
gif ge willað. & gif hwa eow wiðstent. we eow fultumiað. þæt ge
hit magon gegangan.
 0.13. Ða ferdon þa Pihtas. & geferdon þis land
norþanweard. & suþanweard hit hefdon Brittas. swa we ær cwedon.
 0.15. And þa Pyhtas heom abædon wif æt Scottum. on þa
gerad þæt hi gecuron heora kyne cinn aa on þa wif healfa. þæt hi
heoldon swa lange syððan.
 0.17. & þa gelamp hit imbe geara rina. þæt Scotta sum
dæl gewat of Ybernian on Brittene. & þes landes sum dæl geeodon.
& wes heora heratoga Reoda gehaten. from þam heo sind genemnode Dæl
Reodi.
 0.21. Sixtigum wintrum ær þam þe Crist were acenned. Gaius
Iulius Romana Kasere mid hundehtatigum scipum gesohte Brytene.
 0.23. Þer he wes ærost geswenced mid grimmum gefeohte. &
micelne dæl his heres forlædde.
 0.24. & þa he forlet his here abidan mid Scottum. & gewat
into Galwalum. & þer gegadorode six hund scipa. mid þam he gewat eft in
to Brytene.
 0.26. & þa hi ærost togedore geræsdon. þa man ofsloh
ðes Caseres gerefan. se wes Labienus gehaten.
 0.28. Ða genamon þa Walas. & adrifon sumre ea ford ealne
mid scearpum pilum greatum innan þam wetere. sy ea hatte Temese.
 0.30. Þa þæt onfundon ða Romani. þa noldon hi faron ofer
þone ford.
 0.31. Þa flugon þa Bryt Walas to þam wudufæstenum. &
se Kasere geeode wel manega hehburh mid mycelum gewinne. & eft gewat into
Galwalum.

Lundone þe wæs Wina gehaten. & seo Myrcene biscop, Ieruman wæs
gehaten. & Tuda biscop.
 656.32. & þær wæs Wilfrid preost þe siððon wæs
biscop. & þær wæron ælle his ðegnas þe wæron on his
kynerice.
 656.35. Ða seo mynstre wæs gehalgod on Sancte Petres nama
& Sancte Paules & Sancte Andres þa stod seo kyning up toforen ealle
his ðægna. & cwæd luddor stefne. ðancod wurð hit þon hæge
ælmihti God þis wurðscipe þæt her is gedon.
 656.38. & ic wile wurðigen þis dæi Crist & Sancte
Peter. & ic wille þæt ge ealle getiðe mine worde.
 656.40. Ic Wulfere gife to dæi Sancte Petre & þone abbode
Saxulf & þa munecas of þe mynstre þas landes & þas wateres
& meres & fennes & weres & ealle þa landes þa þær
abuton liggeð ða of mine kynerice sindon freolice. swa ðet nan man na
haue þær nan onsting buton seo abbot & se muneces.
 656.45. Ðas is se gife: fram Medeshamstede to Norðburh, &
to ðet stede þet man cleopeð Folies. & swa æl se feon riht to
Esendic. & fra Esendic to þæt steode þe man cleopeð Feðermude.
& swa þæt rihte weie <foreign>x</foreign> mile lang to Cuggedic. & swa to
Raggewilh.
 656.48. & fra Raggewilh <foreign>v</foreign> mile to þe rihte æ þe gað
to Ælm & to Wisebece. & swa abutan <foreign>iii</foreign> mile to þrokonholt. &
fra þrokonholt riht þurh al ðe fen to Fereuorde þæt is <foreign>xx</foreign> mile
lang. & swa to Grætecros.
 656.51. & fra Grætecros þurh an scyr wæter Bradan æ
hatte. & þeonon <foreign>vi</foreign> mile to Paccelade. & swa forð þurh ælle
þa meres & feonnes þa liggen toward Huntendune porte.
 656.54. & þas meres & laces. Scælfremere &
Witlesmere & ælle þa oþre þæt þar abutan liggan mid land
& mid huses þa sindon on æsthalfe Scælfremere. & þeonen
ælle þa feonnon to Medeshamstede.
 656.57. & fra Medeshamstede al to Welmes forde. & fra
Welmes forde to Cliue. and þeonen to Æstune. & fra Æstune to
Stanford. & fra Stanford swa swa þæt wæter renneð to seo
forensprecone Norðburh.
 656.60. Ðis sindon þa landes & ða feonnes þe seo kyning
gef into Sancte Petres mynstre.
 656.62. Ða cwæð seo kyning. Hit is litel þeos gife. ac ic
wille þæt hi hit hælden swa kynelice & swa freolice. þæt
þær ne benumen of na geld na gaule. buton to þa munecan ane.
 656.64. Ðus ic wille freon þis mynstre þet hit ne be
underþed buton Rome ane. & hider ic wille þæt we secan Sancte Petre.
ealle þa þa to Rome na magen faren.
 656.68. Betwix þas worde þa geornde seo abbode þet he scolde
him tyþian þet he æt him geornde. & seo kining hit him tydde.
 656.69. Ic haue here godefrihte muneces þa wolden drohtien here
lif on ankersetle gif hi wisten hwere. oc her is an igland þæt man
cleopeð Ancarig. & wile þes geornen þæt we moten þær wircen
an mynstre Sancte Marie to loue. þet hi moten þær wunen þa ða here
lif wilen læden mid sibbe & mid reste.
 656.75. Ða andswerode seo kyning & þus cwæð. Saxulf la
leof. ne þet an þæt ðu geornest oc ealle þa þing þæt ic wat
þet ðu geornest on ure Drihtnes halfe. swa ic lufe & tyðe.
 656.77. And ic bidde þe broðer æðelred. & mine swustre
Cyneburh & Cynesuuith. for iure sawle alesednesse, þet ge beon witnesse.
& þæt geo hit write mid iure fingre.
 656.80. And ic bidde ealle þa ða æfter me cumen, beon hi
mine sunes. beon hi mine breðre, ouþer kyningas þa æfter me cumen.
þæt ure gyfe mote standen. swa swa hi willen beon delnimende on þa ece
lif. & swa swa hi wilen ætbeorstan þet ece wite.
 656.84. Swa hwa swa ure gife ouþer oðre godene manne gyfe
wansiaþ. wansie him seo heofenlice iateward on heofonrice. & swa hwa swa
hit eceð. ece him seo heofenlice iateward on heofenrice.
 656.88. Ðas sindon þa witnes þe þær wæron, & þa
þæt gewriten mid here fingre on Cristesmele. & ietten mid here tunge.
 656.89. Ðet wæs first seo kyning Wulfere þe þæt

Cristesmel. & þus cwæð.

 656.99. And we þes kyningas swustre Cyneburh & Cynesuith we

 656.101. And ic Kantwarabyrig ærcebiscop Deusdedit hit tyðe.

 656.103. Ðet wæron be nam. Ithamar biscop of Rofecestre. and

 656.115. Swa beo hit. seiþ alle. Amen.
 656.116. Þa þis þing wæs gedon. þa seonde seo kyning to
Rome to seo papa Uitalianus þe þa was. & geornde þæt he scolde

 656.118. & seo papa seonde þa his writ þus cwæðend. Ic
Uitalianus papa geate þe Wulhfere cyning & Deusdedit ærcebiscop &
Saxulf abbod ealle þe þing þe ge geornon. & ic forbede þet ne
kyning. ne nan man ne haue nan onsting buton þon abbod ane. ne he ne hersumie
nan man buton þone papa on Rome & se ærcebiscop on Cantwarbyrig.
 656.124. Gif hwa þis tobrekeþ æniþing. Sancte Petre mid
his sweord him adylige.
 656.125. Gif hwa hit hælt. Sancte Petre mid heofne keie undo him

 656.126. Ðus wæs seo mynstre Medeshamstede agunnen. þæt

 656.128. Siððon com an oþre ærcebiscop to Cantwarbyrig.

þe selue mynstre wæs coren to abbot.

þæt he scolde þæt geten mid his writ & mid his bletsunge.
 675.10. And seo papa seonde þa his gewrite to Englalande þus
cweðende. Ic Agatho papa of Rome grete wel seo wurðfulle æðelred
Myrcene kyning & se ærcebiscop Theodorum of Cantwarbyrig. & seo
Myrcene biscop Saxulf seo ær wæs abbot. & alle þa abbotes þa
sindon on Englalande Godes gretinge & minre bletsunge.
 675.16. Ic haue geheord seo kyninges æðelredes geornunge &
þes ærcebiscopes Theodorus. & þes biscopes Saxulfes. & þes
abbotes Cuthbaldes. & ic hit wille þæt hit on ælle wise beo. swaswa
ge hit sprecon hauen.
 675.19. And ic bebeode of Godes half & Sancte Petres. &
ealra halgan. & ealre hadode heafde. þet ne kyning ne biscop ne eorl. ne
nan man ne haue nan onsting. ne gafle ne geold ne feording ne nanes cinnes
ðeudom ne nime man of þæt abbotrice of Medeshamstede.
 675.23. Ic beode æc þæt þe scyrbiscop ne seo swa
dyrstlece þæt he ne hading ne haleging ne do on þis abbotrice buton seo
abbot hit him bidde. ne biscopwite ne sinað ne nanes kinnes þing na haue
þær nan onsting.
 675.27. & ic wille þæt seo abbot beo gehealden for legat
of Rome ofer eal þæt iglande. & hwilc abbot þe beþ þær coren
of þe munecan þæt he beo gebletsad of þan ærcebiscop of
Cantwarbyrig.
 675.30. Ic wille & tyðe þæt whilc man swa haued behaten
to faren to Rome, and he ne muge hit forðian. ouðer for untrumnisse,
ouðer for lauerdes neode. ouðer for haueleste. ouðer for hwilces cinnes
oðer neod he ne muge þær cumon. beo he of Englelande ouðer of hwilc
oðer igland beo he. cume to þæt mynstre on Medeshamstede. & haue
þæt ilce forgiuenesse of Criste & Sancte Peter. & of þonne abbot
& of þone muneca þæt he scolde hauen gif he to Rome fore.
 675.37. Nu bidde ic þe broðer Theodorus þæt þu lete
bedon geond æl Englelande þet seo sinað wurðe gegaderod. & þis
write wurðe geredd & gehealdon.
 675.40. Alswa ic beode þe Saxulf biscop þæt swa swa þu hit
geornest. þæt seo mynstre beo freo. swa ic forbeode þe & ealle þe
biscopas þe æfter ðe cumon of Criste & of ealle his halgan þæt
ge nan onsting ne hauen of þæt mynstre buton swa micel swa þone abbot
wile.
 675.44. Nu wille ic hit segge mid worde þæt hwa swa halt þis
write & þis bode. þa wurðe he efre wuniende mid God ælmihti on
heuenrice. & hwa swa hit tobreceð. þa wurðe he amansumed &
aniðrod mid Iudas & mid ealle deofle on helle buton he cume to dedbote.
AMEN.
 675.49. Ðas writ seonde seo papa Agatho & an hundred &
fif & twenti biscopes bi Wilfrid ærcebiscop of Eoferwic to Englalande.
 675.51. Þis wæs gedon æfter ure Drihtnes acennednesse <foreign>dc
lxxx</foreign> þes kininges <foreign>vi</foreign> gear æðelredes.
 675.53. Ða heot seo kining þone ærcebiscop Theodorus
þæt he scolde setton ealle gewitenemot æt þone stede þæt man
cleopeð Heatfelde.
 675.55. Ða hi wæron þær gegaderod. þa leot he rædon
þa gewrite þe seo papa þider seonde. & ealle hit getton &
fulfeostnodon.
 675.58. Ða seide se kyning, Ealle þa þing þe min broðer
Peada. & min broðer Wulfere. & mine swuster Kineburh & Kynesuith
geafon & getton Sancte Peter & þone abbot þa wile ic þæt
stande. & ic wile on min dæi hit æcon for here sawle. & for minre
sawle.
 675.62. Nu gife ic Sancte Peter todæi into his minstre
Medeshamstede þas landes. & eal þæt þær to liggeð. þet is
Bredune. Hrepingas. Cedenac. Swineshæfed. Heanbyrig. Lodeshac. Scuffanhalch.
Costesford. Stretford. Wættelleburne. Lufgeard. Æþelhuniglond.
Barþanig.
 675.66. Ðas landes ic gife Sancte Peter ealswa freolice swa ic
seolf hit ahte. & swa þæt nan min æftergengles þær nan þing
of ne nime.
 675.68. Gif hwa hit doð. þes papa curs of Rome & ealre
biscope curs he habbe. & here ealre þe her be gewitnesse. & þis ic
festnie mid Cristes tacne.
 675.70. Ic Theodorus ærcebiscop of Cantwarbyrig am witnesse of
þas gewrite of Medeshamstede. & ic festnie mid min gewrite. & ic
amansumie ealle þa þær aniþing ofbreke. & ic bletsie ealle þa
þe hit healden.
 675.73. Ic Wilfrid ærcebiscop of Æferwic ic eam witnesse of
þas gewrite. & ic gæte þæs ilce curs.
 675.75. Ic Saxulf þe wæs first abbot & nu eam biscop ic
gife hi min curs & ealle min æftergengle þe þis tobreket.
 675.77. Ic Ostriðe æðelredes cwen hit tyðe.
 675.77. Ic Adrianus legat hit iete.
 675.78. Ic Putta biscop of Rofecestre ic hit write.
 675.79. Ic Waldhere biscop of Lundene hit festnie.
 675.79. Ic Cuðbald abbot hit geate swa þet hwa swa hit breket.
ealre biscope cursunge & eal Cristene foces he hafe. Amen.

beheonan sæ wæs. & his gefægene wæron.
 878.16. & he for ymb ane niht of þam wicum to Æglea. &
þæs ymb ane niht to eðandune. & þær gefeaht wið ealne here
& hine geflymde. & him æfter rad oð þet geweorc. & þær
sæt <foreign>xiiii</foreign> niht.
 878.19. & þa sealde se here him gislas. and mycele aðas.
þet hi of his rice woldon. & him eac geheton þet heora cyng fulwihte
onfon wolde. & hi þæt gelæston.
 878.21. & þæs ymb <foreign>iii</foreign> wucan com se cyng Godrum.
þrittigum sum. þara manna þe in þam here weorðuste wæron æt
Alre. & þæt is wið æðelinga ige.
 878.24. & his se cyng onfeng þær æt fulwihte. & his

he hine mycclum & his geferan mid feo weorðode.

 959.3. On his dagum hit godode georne; & God him geuðe,

 959.7. He arerde Godes lof wide, & Godes lage lufode, &

 959.11. & God him eac fylste, þæt ciningas & eorlas
georne him to bugon, & wurden underþeodde to þam þe he wolde, &
butan gefeohte eal he gewilde, þet he sylf wolde.
 959.16. He wearð wide, geond þeodland, swiðe geweorðad,

 959.23. Ane misdæda he dyde þeah to swiðe, þæt he

 963.18. Syððon com se biscop Aðelwold to þære mynstre

 963.33. & swa ic hit freo þet nan biscop ne haue þær

 1009.31. & ealle East Centingas wið þone here frið
genamon. & him gesealdon <foreign>iii</foreign> þusend punda.
 1009.32. & se here þa sona æfter þam gewende abuton oð
þet hi comon to Wihtlande. & þær æghwer on Suðseaxum. & on
Hamtunscire. & eac on Bearrucscire hergodon & bærndon swa heora
gewuna wæs.
 1009.35. Þa het se cyng abannan ut ealne þeodscipe þet mann
on ælce healfe wið hi gehealden sceolde. ac þeah hweðere hi ferdon loc
hu hi woldon.
 1009.38. Þa sum siðe heafde se cyng hi forebegan mid ealre
fyrde. þa hi to scipan woldon. & eall folc gearu wæs heom on to fonne.
ac hit wæs ða þurh Eadric ealdorman gelet swa hit þa æfre wæs.
 1009.41. Ða æfter sanctus Martinus mæssan. þa ferdon hi
eft ongean to Cent. & namon him wintersettl on Temesan. & lifedon of
East Seaxum. & of ðam scirum þe þær nyxt wæron on twam healfe
Temese. & oft hi on þa burh Lundene gefuhton.
 1009.45. Ac si Gode lof. þet heo gyt gesund stent. & hi
þær æfre yfel geferdon.
 1009.46. Ða æfter middan wintra hi namon þa ænne upgang
ut þurh Ciltern. & swa to Oxneforda. & þa burh forbærndon. &
namon hit þa on twa healfe Temese to scipanweard.
 1009.49. Þa gewarnode man hi þæt þær wæs fyrd æt
Lundene ongean. hi gewendon þa ofer æt Stane. & þus ferdon ealne
þone winter, & ðone lencten wæron him on Cent. and bettan heora
scipa.
 1010.1. Her on ðissum geare com se foresprecenda here ofer
Eastron to East Englum. & wendon up æt Gipeswic. & eodon anreces
þær hi geaxodon Ulfcytel mid his fyrde.
 1010.3. Ðis wæs on þam dæg <foreign>prima ascensio Domini</foreign>.
 1010.4. & þa sona flugon East Engla. þa stod

 1010.8. Þone fleam ærest astealde þurcytel Myran heafod.
& þa Dæniscan ahton wælstowe geweald. & þær wurdon
gehorsode.
 1010.10. & syððon ahton East Engle geweald. & þone
eard <foreign>iii</foreign> monþas hergodon & bærndon.
 1010.11. Gefurðon on þa wildan fennas hi ferdon. & menn

forbærndon. & Grantabrycge.
 1010.14. & syððon wendon eft suðweard into Temese. &
ridon þa gehorsedan menn ongean þa scipo.
 1010.15. & syððon hrædlice wendon westweard on
Oxnafordscire. & þanon to Bucinghamscire. & swa andlang Usan. oð hi
comon to Bedanforda & swa forð oð Temesanford. & a bærndon swa
hi geferdon.
 1010.19. Wendon þa eft to scipon mid heora herehuðe. &
þone hi to scipon streddon. þonne sceolde fyrd ut eft ongean þæt hi up
woldon.
 1010.21. Þonne ferde seo fyrd ham.
 1010.21. & þonne hi wæron be easton. þonne heold man
fyrde be westan. & þonne hi wæron be suðan. þonne wæs ure fyrd
be norðan.
 1010.23. Ðonne bead man ealle witan to cynge. & man þonne
rædan scolde hu man þisne eard werian sceolde. Ac þeah man hwæt
þonne rædde. þæt ne stod furðon ænne monað.
 1010.26. Æt nyxtan næs nan heafodman þæt fyrde gaderian
wolde. ac ælc fleah swa he mæst myhte. Ne furðon nan scir nolde oðre
gelæstan æt nyxtan.
 1010.29. Þa ætforan sanctus Andreas mæssan. ða com se
here to Hamtune. & þone port sona forbærndon. & þær namon
abuton swa mycel swa hi woldon sylfe. & þanon wendon ofer Temese into
West Seaxum. & swa wið Caningan mærsces. & þæt eall
forbærndon.
 1010.33. Þa hi swa feor gegan hæfdon swa hi þa woldon. þa
comon hi to ðam middanwintra to scipon.
 1011.1. Her on þissum geare sende se cyng & his witan to

wið þam þe hi heora hergunga geswicon.

 1011.10. Ealle þas ungesælða us gelumpon þurh unrædes.
þæt mann nolde him to timan gafol bedan. ac þonne hi mæst to yfele

 1011.12. & naðelæs for eallum þisum griðe &

 1011.15. & On þissum geare betwix Natiuitate sancte Marie

 1011.18. & hi þær þa genaman þone arcebiscop
Ælfeah. & Ælfword þæt cynges gerefan. & Leofwine abbod.
& Godwine biscop. & Ælmær abbod hi lætan aweg.
 1011.20. & hi þær genaman inne ealle þa gehadode menn.
& weras. & wif. þæt wæs unasecgendlic ænigum menn hu mycel
þæs folces wæs.
 1011.22. & on þære byrig siððon wæron swa lange swa
hi woldon. & þa hi hæfdon þa burh ealle asmeade. wendon him þa to
scipon. & læddon þone arcebiscop mid him;
 1011.26. Wæs ða ræpling, se þe ær wæs Angelcynnes
heafod & Christendomes.
 1011.28. Þær man mihte þa geseon earmðe þær man ær
geseah blisse on þære ærman byrig, þanon us com ærest Christendom
& blisse for Gode & for worulde.
 1011.32. & hi heafdon þone arcebiscop mid him swalange oð
þone timan þe hi hine gemartyredon.
 1012.1. Her on þissum geare com Eadric ealdorman. & ealle

 1012.5. Þa on þone Sæternesdæg wearð swiðe gestired

& forbead þæt man nan þing wið him syllan ne moste.
 1012.8. Wæron hi eac swyðe druncene. forþam þær wæs

 1012.10. Genamon þa þone biscop. leaddon hine to heora hustinga

 1012.12. & sloh hine þa an heora mid anre æxe yre on þet

eorðan feoll. & his þa haligan sawle to Godes rice asende.
 1012.15. & þa biscopas Eadnoð & Ælfhun. & seo

 1012.19. Ða þet gafol gelest wæs. & þa frið aðas

 1012.21. Ða bugon to þam cyninge of þam here <foreign>xlv</foreign> scipa.

 1013.1. On þam æftran geare þe se arcebiscop wæs

 1013.3. & on þam ilcan geare toforan þam monðe Augustus

 1013.6. & þa sona abeah Uhtred eorl. & eall Norðhymbra

 1013.10. Syððan he undergeat þet eall folc him to gebogen

 1013.12. & he þa gewende syððan suðweard mid fulre

 1013.13. & syððan he com ofer Wæclingastræte, hi

 1013.15. Wende þa to Oxnaforda. & seo burhwaru sona abeah

 1013.17. Wendon þa þanon eastward to Lundene. & mycel his

 1013.18. Ða he to þære byrig com. þa nolde seo burhwaru

 1013.21. Þa wende Swegen cyning þanon to Wealingaforda. &

 1013.23. & com Æþelmer ealdorman þider. & þa

 1013.25. Þa he eall þus gefaren heafde. wende þa norðweard

 1013.26. & eall þeodscipe hine heafde for fullne cyning.
 1013.27. & seo burhwaru æfter þam on Lundene beah &

 1013.29. Bead þa Swegen full gild & metsunga to his here

 1013.32. Ða ne duhte naðor þisse þeoda ne suðan. ne

 1013.32. Þa wæs se cyng sume hwile mid þam flotan þe on

 1013.35. & se cyng sende Ælfun biscop mid þam
æþelinge Eadwarde. & Ælfrede ofer se. þæt he hi bewitan
sceolde.
 1013.37. & se cyng gewende þa fram þam flotan to ðam
middan wintra to Wihtlande. & wæs þær þa tid.
 1013.38. & æfter þære tide gewende þa ofer sæ to

wearð.
 1013.41. & ða hwile þe seo læfdige mid hire broþer

 1013.43. Fand þær ærm stede. ærm abbot & ærme

 1014.3. Ða geræddan þa witan ealle ge hadode ge læwede

 1014.12. & man þa fullne freondscipe gefæstnode mid worde

 1014.15. Ða com æðelred cyning innan þam lenctene ham to

 1014.17. & þa syððon Swegen dead wæs. sætt Cnut mid

 1014.20. Ða com se cyning æðelred mid fulre fyrde þider

 1015.1. On þissum geare wæs þæt mycele gemot on

 1016.1. Her on þissum geare com Cnut cyning mid his here <foreign>clx</foreign>

 1016.5. Ða ongan se æðeling Eadmund to gadrienne fyrde.

 1016.12. Ða hi ealle tosomne comon. þa ne beheold hit naht þe

 1016.14. Þa cydde mann þam cyninge þæt hine mann beswicon

 1016.31. & se æþeling Ædmund wende to Lundene to his

 1016.35. Ða gelamp hit þet se cyng æðelred forðferde

 1016.45. & oft rædlice on ða burh fuhton. ac hi heom

 1016.46. Þa wæs Eadmund cyng ær þam gewend ut. &

 1016.47. & raðe æfter þam he gefeaht wið þone here

 1016.49. & þær mycel wæll feoll on ægðre healfe.

 1016.51. & Eadric ealdorman & Ælmær Deorlingc

 1016.52. & þa gegaderode he <foreign>iii</foreign> siðe fyrde & ferde to

 1016.54. & þa wæs ymbe twa niht þæt se cyning gewende

 1016.56. & þær adranc mycel Ænglisces folces on heora

fon.
 1016.58. & se cyning wende æfter þam to West Seaxan. &

 1016.59. Ða gewende se here sona to Lundene. & þa burh
utone besæton. & hire stranglice wiðfeaht ge be wætere ge be lande.
ac se ælmihtiga God hi ahredde.

þær & his menn. & to Dofran gewende.
 1048.21. Ða he wæs sume mila oððe mare beheonan Dofran.
þa dyde he on his byrnan. & his geferan ealle. & foran to Dofran.
 1048.23. Þa hi þider comon. þa woldon hi innian hi þær
heom sylfan gelicode.
 1048.25. Þa com an his manna. & wolde wician æt anes
bundan huse his unðances. & gewundode þone husbundon. & se husbunda
ofsloh þone oðerne.
 1048.27. Ða wearð Eustatius uppon his horse. & his gefeoran
uppon heora & ferdon to þam husbundon. & ofslogon hine binnan his
agenan heorðæ.
 1048.29. & wendon him þa up to þære burgeweard. &
ofslogon ægðer ge wiðinnan ge wiðutan. ma þanne <foreign>xx</foreign> manna. &
þa burhmen ofslogon <foreign>xix</foreign> menn on oðre healfe. & gewundoden þæt hi
nystan hu fela.
 1048.33. & Eustatius ætbærst mid feawum mannum. &
gewende ongean to þam cynge. & cydde be dæle hu hi gefaren hæfdon.
 1048.35. & wearð se cyng swiþe gram wið þa burhware.
& ofsænde se cyng Godwine eorl. & bæd hine faran into Cent mid
unfriða to Dofran. forþan Eustatius hæfde gecydd þam cynge þet hit
sceolde beon mare gylt þære burhwaru þonne his.
 1048.38. Ac hit næs na swa. & se eorl nolde na
geðwærian þære infare. forþan him wæs lað to amyrrene his
agenne folgað.
 1048.41. Ða sende se cyng æfter eallon his witan. & bead
heom cuman to Gleaweceastre neh þære æftre sancte Maria mæssan.
 1048.43. Þa hæfdon þa welisce menn gewroht ænne castel on
Herefordscire on Swegenes eorles folgoðe. & wrohten ælc þæra
harme. & bismere þæs cynges mannan þær abutan þe hi mihton.
 1048.46. Ða com Godwine eorl & Swegen eorl & Harold eorl
togædere æt Byferesstane. & manig mann mid heom. to ðon þæt hi
woldon faran to heora cynehlaforde. & to þam witan eallon þe mid him
gegaderode wæron. þæt hi þæs cynges ræd hæfdon & his
fultum. & ealra witena. hu hi mihton þæs cynges bismer awrecan &
ealles þeodscipes.
 1048.51. Ða wæron þa wælisce men ætforan mid þam
cynge. & forwregdon ða eorlas. þet hi ne moston cuman on his eagon
gesihðe. Forðan hi sædon þæt hi woldon cuman þider for þes
cynges swicdome.
 1048.54. Wæs þær cuman Siward eorl & Leofric eorl.
& mycel folc mid heom norþan to þam cynge. & wæs þam eorle
Godwine & his sunan gecydd þæt se cyng & þa menn þe mid him
wæron. woldon rædon on hi. & hi trymedon hi fæstlice ongean.
þæh him lað wære þæt hi ongean heora cynehlaford standan
sceoldan.
 1048.59. Ða gerædden þa witan on ægðer halfe þæt
man ða ælces yfeles geswac. & geaf se cyng Godes grið & his
fulne freondscipe on ægðre healfe.
 1048.63. Ða gerædde se cyning & his witan þæt man
sceolde oðre syðan habban ealra gewitena gemot on Lundene to hærfestes
emnihte.
 1048.65. & het se cyning bannan ut here. ægðer ge
besuðan Temese ge benorðan eall þæt æfre betst wæs.
 1048.66. Ða cwæð man Swegen eorl utlah. & stefnode man
Godwine eorle & Harolde eorle to þon gemote swa raðe swa hi hit gefaran
mihton.
 1048.68. Þa hi þider utcomon. þa stefnede heom man to gemote.
þa gyrnde he griðes & gisla. þet he moste unswican into gemote cuman.
& ut of gemote.
 1048.71. Ða gyrnde se cyng ealra þæra þegna þe þa
eorlas ær hæfdon. & hi letan hi ealle him to handa.
 1048.73. Þa sende se cyng eft to heom. & bead heom þæt
hi comon mid <foreign>xii</foreign> mannum into þæs cynges ræde.
 1048.74. Þa geornde se eorl eft griðes & gisla. þæt he
moste hine betellan æt ælc þæra þinga þe him man on lede.
 1048.76. Þa wyrnde him mann ðera gisla. & sceawede him mann
<foreign>v</foreign> nihta grið ut of lande tofarenne.
 1048.78. & gewende þa Godwine eorl & Swegen eorl to
Bosenham & scufon ut heora scipu. & gewendon heom begeondan sæ.

 1048.81. & Harold eorl gewende west to Yrlande. & wæs
þær ealne þone winter on þes cynges griðe.
 1048.82. & sona þæs þe þis wæs. þa forlet se cyng
þa hlæfdian. seo wæs gehalgod him to cwene. & let niman of hire
eall þæt heo ahte. on lande. & on golde. & on seolfre & on
eallon þingon. & betæhte hy his swyster to Hwerwillon.
 1048.87. & Sparhafoc abbod wearð ða adrifen ut of þam
biscoprice on Lundene. & wes Willelm þæs cynges preost gehadod
þærto.
 1048.89. & man sette þa Oddan to eorle ofer Defenascire.

 1052.1. Her on ðisum geare forðferde Ælfgiue Ymma Eadwardes
cynges modor & Hardacnutes cynges.
 1052.2. & on þam sylfan geare gerædde se cyng & his

eorl & Oddan eorl to heafodmannum þærto.
 1052.5. Ða gewende Godwine eorl ut fram Brycge mid his scypum to
Yseran. and let ut ane dæge ær midsumeres mæsseæfene þæt he
com to Næsse. þe is besuðan Rumenea.
 1052.8. Þa com hit to witenne þam eorlum ut to Sandwic. &
hi þa gewendon ut æfter þam oðrum scipum. & bead man landfyrde ut
ongean þa scipu.
 1052.10. Þa amang þison þa wearð Godwine eorl gewarnod.
& gewende him þa into Pefenesea. & wearð þæt wæder swiðe
strang. þæt þa eorlas ne mihton gewitan hwet Godwine eorl gefaren

 1052.13. & gewende þa Godwine eorl ut agean þæt he com
eft to Brycge. & ða oðra scipu gewenden heom eft ongean to Sandwic.
 1052.15. & gerædde man þa þæt þa scipu gewendan eft

hasæton to þam scipum. ða lengde hit man swa lange þæt seo scipfyrd
eall belaf. & gewendon ealle heom ham.
 1052.19. Ða geaxode Godwine eorl þet. & teah þa up his
segl & his lið. & gewendon heom þa west on an to Wiht. & eodon
þær up. & hergodon swa lange þær þæt þæt folc geald

 1052.22. & gewendon heom þa westweard oð þet hi comon to
Portlande. & eodon þær up & dydon to hearme swa hwet swa hi don
mihton.
 1052.26. Þa wes Harold gewend ut of Yrlande mid nigon scipon.
& com þa up æt Portlocan. & wes þær mycel folc gegaderod
ongean. ac he ne wandode na him metes to tylienne.
 1052.28. Eode up. & ofsloh þær mycelne ende þes folces.
& nam him on orfe. & on mannum. & on æhtum. swa him gewearð.
 1052.30. & gewende him þa eastweard to his feder. &
gewendon heom þa begen eastweard þæt hi comon to Wiht. & namon
þær þæt him ær wiðæftan wæs.
 1052.33. & gewendon heom þa þanon to Pefenesea. &
begeat forð mid him swa fela scipu. swa þær fera wæron. & swa
forð þæt he com to Næsse. & begeat ealle þa scipu. þe
wæron on Rumenea. & on Hyþe & on Folcesstane.
 1052.36. & gewendon þa east to Dofran. & eodon þær

 1052.38. & ferdon swa to Sandwic. & dydon hand þæt
sylfa. & heom man geaf æghwer gislas. & metsunga. þær þær
hi gyrndon.
 1052.40. & gewendon heom þa to Norðmuðan. & swa to
Lundeneweard.
 1052.41. & sume þa scipu gewendon binnon Scepige. & dydon

& forbearndon þæt eall. & wæron heom to Lundeneweard æfter

 1052.44. Þa hi to Lundene comon. þa læg se cyng & þa

 1052.46. Þa sendon þa eorlas to þam cynge. & gerndon to

unrihte ofgenumen wæs.
 1052.48. Ða wiðlæg se cyng sume hwile þeah. swa lange oð

cyng. & ongean his folc. swa þæt se eorl sylf earfoðlice gestylde
þæt folc.
 1052.51. Þa ferde Stigand biscop to mid Godes fultume. & þa
wise menn ægðær ge binnan burh ge buton. & geræddon þæt man
tremede gislas on ægðer healfe. & man swa dyde.
 1052.54. Ða geaxode Rotberd arcebiscop & þa Frencisce menn

sume norð to Rodbertes castele.
 1052.57. & Rodberd arcebiscop & Vlf biscop gewendon ut

 1052.58. & gewendon heom on an to Ealdulfesnæse. &

 1052.63. Ða cwæð mann mycel gemot wiðutan Lundene. &

 1052.65. Þær bær Godwine eorl up his mal. & betealde

þet he wæs unscyldig þæs þe him geled wæs. & on Harold his

 1052.68. & se cyng forgeaf þam eorle & his bearnum his

hlæfdian eall þæt heo ær ahte.
 1052.72. & cweð man utlaga Rotberd arcebiscop fullice, &

betweonan Godwine eorle & þam cynge.
 1052.74. & Stigand biscop feng to þam arcebiscoprice on

 1052.78. & se abbot Leofric godede þa þæt mynstre swa

 1066.1. On þissum geare man halgode þet mynster æt

 1066.15. & man cydde Harolde cyng hu hit wæs þær gedon

 1066.28. God are his saule.

 1066.35. Þa wearð gildene burh to wrecce burh.
 1066.35. Ða cusen þa munecas to abbot Brand prouost. forðan

 1066.39. Þa þe cyng Willelm geherde þæt secgen. þa

 1066.41. Þa eodon gode men heom betwenen & sahtloden heom
