 1067.1. Her for se cyng ofer sæ. & hæfde mid him gislas
& sceattas.
 1067.2. & com þæs oðres geares on sancte Nicolaes
mæssedæg. & þæs dæges forbearn Cristes cyrce on
Cantwarabyrig.
 1067.3. & he geaf ælces mannes land þa he ongean com.
 1067.4. & þæs sumeres for Eadgar cild ut. & Mærle
swegen. & fela manna mid heom. & foran to Scotlande. & se cyng
Melcolm hi ealle underfeng. & genam þes cildes swuster to wife
Margaretan.
 1068.2. Her on þissum geare Willelm cyng geaf Rodberde eorle
þone eorldom on Norðhymbraland.
 1068.2. Ða comon þa landesmenn togeanes him. & hine
ofslogon. & <foreign>ix</foreign> hund manna mid him.
 1068.4. And Eadgar æðeling com þa mid eallum Norðhymbram
to Eoferwic. & þa portmen wið hine griðedon.
 1068.5. & se cyng Willelm com suðan mid eallan his fyrde.
& þa burh forhergode. & fela hund manna ofsloh. & se æðeling
for eft to Scotlande.
 1069.1. Her man wrægde þone biscop Ægelric on Burh. &
sende hine to Westmynstre. & utlagode his broðer Ægelwine biscop.
 1069.3. Þa betwyx þam twam sancta Marian mæssan. comon
easton of Dænmarcun mid <foreign>ccc</foreign> scipum. þæt wæron Swægnes sunan
cynges. & his broðer Osbearn eorl.
 1069.5. & þa ferde se eorl Walðeaf ut. & com he &
Eadgar æðeling. & fela hund manna mid heom. & gemetton þet lið
innan Humbran.
 1069.7. & ferdon to Eoferwic. & upp eodan & þa
castelas gewunnan. & ofslogon fela hund manna. & to scipe læddon
sceattas fela. & þa heafodmen hæfdon on beandon. & lagon betwyx
Vsan & Trentan ealne þone winter.
 1069.11. & se cyng Willelm for into þære scire. & hi
eall fordyde.
 1069.12. & on þisum ilcan geare forðferde Brand abbod of
Burh. on <foreign>v kalendæ Decembris</foreign>.
 1070.1. Her se eorl Walþeof griðede wið þone cyng. &
þæs on lengten se cyng let hergian ealle þa mynstra þe on Englalande
wæron.
 1070.3. Þa on þam ilcan geare com Swegn cyng of Denmarcan into
Humbran. & þæt landfolc comen him ongean & griðedon wið hine
wændon þæt he sceolde þet land ofergan.
 1070.6. Þa comen into Elig Cristien þa Densce biscop &
Osbearn eorl & þa Densca huscarles mid heom.
 1070.7. & þet Englisce folc of eall þa feonlandes comen to
heom. wendon þæt hi sceoldon winnon eall þæt land.
 1070.9. Þa herdon þa munecas of Burh sægen þæt heora
agene menn wolden hergon þone mynstre, þæt wæs Hereward & his
genge.
 1070.11. Þæt wæs forðan þet hi herdon sæcgen þet
se cyng heafde gifen þæt abbotrice an Frencisce abbot Turolde wæs
gehaten. & þæt he wæs swiðe styrne man. & wæs cumen þa
into Stanforde mid ealle hise Frencisce menn.
 1070.14. Þa wæs þære an cyrceweard Yware wæs gehaten.
nam þa be nihte eall þet he mihte. þet wæron Cristes bec &
mæsse hakeles & cantelcapas & reafes & swilce litles hwat. swa
hwat swa he mihte.
 1070.17. & ferde sona ær dæg to þone abbot Turolde
& sægde him þæt he sohte his griðe. & cydde him hu þa
utlages sceolden cumen to Burh. þæt he dyde eall be þære munece
ræde.
 1070.20. Þa sona on morgen comen ealle þa utlaga mid fela
scipe, & woldon into þam mynstre. & þa munecas wiðstoden þæt
hi na mihton incumen.
 1070.22. Þa lægdon hi fyr on. & forbærndon ealle þa
munece huses & eall þa tun buton ane huse.
 1070.24. Þa comen hi þurh fyre in æt Bolhiðe geate. &
þa munecas comen heom togeanes. beaden heom grið, ac hi na rohten na
þing.
 1070.26. Geodon into þe mynstre. clumben upp to þe halge rode.
namen þa þe kynehelm of ure Drihtnes heafod eall of smeate golde. namen
þa þet fotspure þe wæs undernæðen his fote. þæt wæs eall
of read golde.
 1070.29. Clumben upp to þe stepel. brohton dune þæt hæcce
þe þær wæs behid. hit wæs eall of gold & of seolfre. hi namen
þære twa gildene scrines & <foreign>ix</foreign> seolferne.
 1070.32. & hi namen fiftene mycele roden. ge of golde ge of
seolfre.
 1070.33. Hi namen þære swa mycele gold & seolfre & swa
manega gersumas on sceat & on scrud & on bokes swa nan man ne mæi
oðer tællen. sægdon þæt hi hit dyden for ðes mynstres
holdscipe.
 1070.36. Syððon geden heom to scipe. ferden heom to Elig,
betæhtan þær þa ealla þa gærsume;
 1070.37. Þa Denescæ menn wændon þæt hi sceoldon
ofercumen þa Frencisca men. þa todrefodon ealle þa munekes. beleaf
þær nan butan an munec he wæs gehaten Leofwine lange. he læi seoc in
þa secræman in.
 1070.41. Ða com Turold abbot & æhte siþe twenti
Frencisce men mid him & ealle fullwepnode.
 1070.42. Þa he þider com þa fand he forbærnd wiðinnan
& wiðutan. eall butan þa cyrece ane.
 1070.44. Þa wæron þa utlagas ealle on flote. wistan þæt
he scolde þider cumen.
 1070.45. Þis wæs don þæs dæges <foreign>iiii Nonæ Iunii</foreign>.
 1070.45. Þa twegen kyngas Willelm & Swægn wurðon
sæhtlod. þa ferdon þa Dænesca menn ut of Elig mid ealle þa
forenspræcena gærsume & læddon mid heom.
 1070.48. Þa hi comen on middewarde þe sæ. þa com an mycel
storm & todræfede ealle þa scipe þær þa gersumes wæron inne.
sume ferdon to Norwæge. sume to Yrlande. sume to Dænmarce.
 1070.51. & eall þæt þider com þæt wæs þone
hæcce & sume scrine & sume roden & fela of þa oðre
gærsume. & brohten hit to an cynges tun hatte. & dyden hit eall þa
in þone cyrce.
 1070.54. Ða syððon þurh heora gemelest & þurh heora
druncenhed on an niht forbærnde þa cyrce. & eall þet þær
innæ wæs.
 1070.56. Ðus wæs se mynstre of Burch forbærnd &
forhærgod.
 1070.57. Ælmihtig God hit gemiltse þurh his mycele
mildhertnesse.
 1070.58. And þus se abbot Turolde com to Burh. & þa munecas
comen þa ongean. & dydan Cristes þeudom in þære cyrce. þæt
ær hæfde standen fulle seofeniht forutan ælces cynnes riht.
 1070.61. Ða herde Ægelric biscop þet gesecgon. þa
amansumede he ealle þa men þa þæt yfel dæde hæfden don.
 1070.62. Ða wæs mycel hunger þæs geares.
 1070.63. & þa þæs sumeres com þet lið norðan of
Humbran into Tæmese. & lagon þær twa niht. & heoldan syððon
to Dænmercan.
 1070.65. And Baldewine eorl forðferde. & his sunu Arnulf feng
to rice.
 1070.66. & Willelm eorl sceolde ben his geheald. & Franca
cyng eac. & com þa Rodbriht eorl & ofsloh his mæg Arnulf. &
þone eorl. & þone cyng aflymda. and his menn ofsloh fela þusenda.
 1071.1. Her Ædwine eorl & Morkere eorl uthlupon &
mislice ferdon on wudu & on felda.
 1071.2. Ða gewende Morkere eorl to Elig on scipe. And Eadwine
eorl wearð ofslagen arhlice fram his agenum mannum.
 1071.4. & com se biscop Egelwine. & Siward Bearn. &
fela hund manna mid heom into Elig.
 1071.6. & þa þe se cyng Willelm þæt geaxode. þa bead
he ut scipfyrde & landfyrde. & þet land abutan sæt. & brycge
gewrohte. & inn for. & seo scipfyrde on þa sæhealfe.
 1071.8. & þa utlagan þa ealle on hand eodan. þæt
wæs Egelwine biscop. & Morkere eorl. & ealle þa þe mid heom
wæron buton Herewarde ane.
 1071.10. & ealle þa þe mid him woldon. & he hi ahtlice
utlædde.
 1071.11. & se cyng genam scipa & wæpna & sceattas
manega. & þa men he ateah swa swa he wolde. & þone biscop Egelwine
he sende to Abbandune. & he þær forðferde sona þæs wintres.
 1072.1. Her Willelm cyng lædde scipfyrde & landfyrde to
Scotlande. & þæt land on þa sæhealfe mid scipum ymbelæg. &
his landfyrde æt þam Gewæde innlædde. & he þær naht ne
funde þæs þe him þe bet wære.
 1072.4. & se cyng Melcolm com & griðede wið þone cyng
Willelm & gislas sealde. & his man wæs.
 1072.6. & se cyng ham gewende mid ealre his fyrde.
 1072.6. & se biscop Egelric forðferde. he wæs to biscop
hadod to Eoferwic. ac hit wæs mid unrihte him ofgenumon.
 1072.8. & man geaf him þæt biscoprice on Dunholme. &
he heafde hit þa hwile þe he wolde. & forlet hit syððan. &
ferde to Burch to sancte Petres mynstre. & þær drohtnode <foreign>xii</foreign> gear.
 1072.11. Ða æfter þam þe Willelm cyng gewan Englalande.
þa nam he hine of Burch & sende hine to Westmynstre.
 1072.13. & he forðferde on <foreign>IDus Octobris</foreign>. & he is
bebyrged þær innan þam mynstre. innon sanctus Nicolaus portice.
 1073.1. On þisum geare Willelm cyng lædde Engliscne here &
Frencisce ofer sæ. & gewan þæt land Mans.
 1073.2. & hit Englisce men swyðe amyrdon. wingearðas hi
fordydon. & burga forbærndon. & swiðe þet land amyrdon. &
hit eall abegdon Willelme to handa.
 1073.5. & hi syððon ham gewendon to Englalande.
 1074.1. On þisum geare for Willelm cyng ofer sæ to Normandig.
& Eadgar cild com of Scotland to Normandige.
 1074.2. & se cyng hine geinlagode. & ealle his men. &
he wæs on þes cynges hyrede. & nam swilce gerihta swa se cyng him
geuðe.
 1075.1. On þisum geare Willelm cyng geaf Raulfe eorle Willelmes
dohtor Osbearnes sunu. & se ylca Raulf wæs Bryttisc on his moderhealfe.
& his fæder wæs Englisc Raulf hatte. & wæs geboren on
Norðfolc.
 1075.4. Þa geaf se cyng his sunu þone eorldom on Norðfolc.
& Suðfolc. þa lædde he þæt wif to Norðwic.
 1075.7. Þær wes þæt bryd eala mannum to beala.
 1075.9. Ðær wæs Roger eorl. & Walþeof eorl. &
biscopas & abbotes. & ræddon þær swa þæt hi woldon þone
cyng gesettan ut of Englelandes cynedome.
 1075.11. & hit wearð sona gecydd þam cynge to Normandige hu
hit wæs geræd. þæt wæs Roger eorl. & Raulf eorl. þe
wæron yldast to ðam unreode. & hi speonan þa Bryttas heom to. &
sendon east to Denmearcan æfter sciphere heom to fultume.
 1075.15. & Roger ferde west to his eorldome. & gegaderode
his folc to þæs cynges unþearfe. ac he wearð gelet.
 1075.17. & Raulf eac on his eorldome wolde forðgan mid his
folce. ac þa castelmen þe wæron on Englalande & eac þæt
landfolc him togeanes comen. & gemacodon þæt he naht ne dyde. ac for
to scipe æt Norðwic.
 1075.20. & his wif wæs innan þam castele. & hine heold
swa lange þæt man hire grið sealde. & heo ut ferde þa of
Englalande. & ealle hire men þe hire mid woldon.
 1075.23. & se cyng siððan com to Englalande. & genam
Roger eorl his mæg. & gefestnode hine. & Walþeof eorl he genam
eac.
 1075.26. & sona æfter þam comon eastan of Denmearcan <foreign>cc</foreign>
scipa. & þær on wæron twægen heafodmenn. Cnut Swægnes sunu.
& Hacun eorl. & hi ne dorstan nan gefeoht healdan wið Willelm cynge.
ac heoldon ofer sæ to Flandran.
 1075.30. & Eadgið seo hlæfdig forðferde on Winceastre
<foreign>vii</foreign> nihton ær Cristes mæssan. & se cyng hi let bryngan to
Westmynstre mid mycclan wurðscipe. & lægde hi wið Eadward kyng hire
hlaforde.
 1075.34. & se wæs on Westmynstre þone midewinter. &
man fordyde þær ealle þa Bryttas þe wæron æt þam brydealoð
æt Norðwic.
 1075.36. Sume hy wurdon ablænde & sume of land adrifene. swa
wurdon Willelmes swican geniðrade.
 1076.1. On þisum geare forðferde Swægn cyng on Dænmercan.
& Harold his sunu feng to þe kynerice.
 1076.3. & se cyng geaf Westmynster Vithele abbode se wæs
ær abbod on Bærnege. & Walþeof eorl wes beheafdod on Winceastre.
& his lic wearð gelead to Crulande.
 1076.6. & se cyng for ofer sæ. & lædde his fyrde to

 1076.7. & þa Bryttas hine heoldon þæt se cyng com of

ge hors. & feola his gersuma.
 1077.1. Her on þisum geare wurdon sæhte Franca cyng &
Willelm Englalandes cyng. ac hit heold litle hwile.
 1077.3. & ðes geares forbarn Lundenburh anre nihte ær
Assumptio sancte Mariæ swa swyðe swa heo næfre ær næs syðþan
heo gestabeled wæs.
 1077.6. And on þisum geare forðfyrde Ægelwig abbod on
Euesham on þam dæge <foreign>xiv kalendæ Marcii</foreign>. And Hereman biscop eac
forðferde on þam dæge <foreign>x kalendæ Marcii</foreign>.
 1079.1. On þisum geare com Melcolm cyng of Scotlande into
Englelande betwyx þam twam Mariam mæssan mid mycclum fyrde. &
gehergode Norðhymbraland oð hit com to Tine. & ofsloh feala hund manna.
& ham lædde manige sceattas. & gersuma. & menn on heftninge.
 1079.6. And þi ilcan geare se cyng Willelm gefeaht togeanes his
sunu Rotbearde wiðutan Normandige be anum castele Gerborneð hatte. & se
cyng Willelm wearð þær gewundod. & his hors ofslagen þe he on
sæt. & eac his sunu Willelm wearð þær gewundod. & fela manna
ofslagene.
 1080.1. On þisum geare wæs se biscop Walchere ofslagen on
Dunholme æt anum gemote. & an hund manna mid him Frencisce &
Flemisce. & he sylf wæs on Hloðeringa geboren. þis dydon
Norðhymbran on Maies monðe.
 1081.1. ON þisum geare se cyng lædde fyrde into Wealan. &
þær gefreode fela hund manna.
 1082.1. Her nam se cyng Odan biscop. & her wæs mycel
hungor.
 1083.1. On þisum geare aras seo ungehwærnes on
Glæstingabyrig betwyx þam abbode þurstane. & his munecan.
 1083.2. Ærest hit com of þæs abbotes unwisdome. þæt he
misbead his munecan on fela þingan.
 1083.4. & ða munecas hit mændon lufelice to him. &
beadon hine þæt he sceolde healdan hi rihtlice. & lufian hi. & hi
woldon him beon holde. & gehyrsume.
 1083.6. Ac se abbot nolde þæs naht. ac dyde heom yfele. &
beheot heom wyrs.
 1083.8. Anes dæges þe abbot eode into capitulan. &
spræc uppon þa munecas. & wolde hi mistukian.
 1083.9. & sende æfter læwede mannum. & hi comon into
capitulan on uppon þa munecas full gewepnede. & þa wæron þa
munecas swiðe aferede of heom. nyston hwet heom to donne wære.
 1083.12. Ac to scuton. sume urnon into cyrcean. & belucan þa
duran into heom. & hi ferdon æfter heom into þam mynstre. & woldon
hit utdragan. þaða hig ne dorsten na utgan.
 1083.15. Ac reowlic þing þær gelamp on dæg. þæt þa
Frencisce men bræcen þone chor & torfedon towærd þam weofode
þær ða munecas wæron. & sume of ðam cnihtan ferdon uppon þone
uppflore. & scotedon adunweard mid arewan toweard þam haligdome. swa
þæt on þære rode þe stod bufon þam weofode sticodon on mænige
arewan.
 1083.20. & þa wreccan munecas lagon onbuton þam weofode.
& sume crupon under. & gyrne cleopedon to Gode his miltse biddende.
þa þa hi ne mihton nane miltse æt mannum begytan.
 1083.23. Hwæt magon we secgean. buton þæt hi scotedon
swiðe. & þa oðre ða dura bræcon þær adune & eodon inn.
 1083.25. & ofslogon sume þa munecas to deaðe. &
mænige gewundedon þærinne. swa þæt ðet blod com of ðam weofode
uppon þam gradan. & of ðam gradan on þa flore.
 1083.28. Þreo þær wæron ofslagene to deaðe. &
eahteteone gewundade.
 1083.30. & on þæs ilcan geares forðferde Mahtild
Willelmes cynges cwen. on þone dæg æfter ealra halgena mæssedæg.
 1083.32. And on þes ylcan geares æfter midewintre se cyng let
beodan mycel gyld & hefelic ofer eall Englaland. þæt wæs æt
ælcere hyde twa & hund seofenti peanega.
 1084.1. Her on ðisum geare forðferde Wulfuuold abbod on
Ceortesege. on þam dæge <foreign>xiii kalendæ Mai</foreign>.
 1085.1. On þisum geare menn cwydodon & to soðan sædan.
þæt Cnut cyng of Denmearcan Swægnes sune cynges fundade hiderward.
& wolde gewinnan þis land mid Rodbeardes eorles fultume of Flandran.
forðan þe Cnut heafde Rodbeardes dohter.
 1085.5. Ða Willelm Englalandes cyng þe þa wæs sittende on
Normandige. forðig he ahte ægðer ge Englaland ge Normandige. þis
geaxode. he ferde into Englalande mid swa mycclan here ridendra manna. &
gangendra of Francrice and of Brytlande. swa næfre ær þis land ne
gesohte. swa þæt menn wundredon hu þis land mihte eall þone here
afedan.
 1085.10. Ac se cyng let toscyfton þone here geond eall þis land
to his mannon. & hi fæddon þone here ælc be his landefne.
 1085.12. & men heafdon mycel geswinc þæs geares. & se
cyng lett awestan þæt land abutan þa sæ. þet gif his feond comen
upp. þæt hi næfdon na on hwam hi fengon swa rædlice.
 1085.15. Ac þa se cyng geaxode to soðan þæt his feond
gelætte wæron. & ne mihten na geforðian heora fare. þa lett he
sum þone here faren to heora agene lande. & sum he heold on þisum lande
ofer winter.
 1085.19. Ða to þam midewintre wæs se cyng on Gleaweceastre
mid his witan. & heold þær his hired <foreign>v</foreign> dagas. & syððan þe
arcebiscop & gehadode men hæfden sinoð þreo dagas.
 1085.20. Ðær wæs Mauricius gecoren to biscop on Lundene.
& Willelm to Norðfolce & Rodbeard to Ceasterscire. hi wæron ealle
þæs cynges clerecas.
 1085.23. Æfter þisum hæfde se cyng mycel geþeaht. &
swiðe deope spæce wið his witan ymbe þis land hu hit wære gesett.
oððe mid hwylcon mannon.
 1085.26. Sende þa ofer eall Englaland into ælcere scire his
men. & lett agan ut hu fela hundred hyda wæron innon þære scire.
oððe hwet se cyng him sylf hæfde landes. & orfes innan þam lande.
oððe hwilce gerihtæ he ahte to habbanne to <foreign>xii</foreign> monþum of ðære
scire.
 1085.30. Eac he lett gewritan hu mycel landes his arcebiscops
hæfdon. & his leodbiscops. & his abbods. & his eorlas. &
þeah ic hit lengre telle. hwæt oððe hu mycel ælc mann hæfde þe
landsittende wæs innan Englalande. on lande. oððe on orfe. & hu
mycel feos hit wære wurð.
 1085.35. Swa swyðe nearwelice he hit lett utaspyrian. þæt
næs an ælpig hide. ne an gyrde landes. ne furðon, hit is sceame to
tellanne. ac hit ne þuhte him nan sceame to donne. an oxe. ne an cu. ne an
swin. næs belyfon. þæt næs gesæt on his gewrite.
 1085.39. & ealle þa gewrita wæron gebroht to him
syððan.
 1085.41. Her se cyng bær his corona & heold his hired on
Winceastre to þam Eastran. & swa he ferde þæt he wæs to þam
Pentecosten æt Wæstminstre. & dubbade his sunu Henric to ridere
þær.
 1085.44. Syððan he ferde abutan swa þæt he com to
Lammæssan to Searebyrig. & þær him comon to his witan. and ealle
þa landsittende men. þe ahtes wæron ofer eall Engleland. wæron
þæs mannes men þe hi wæron.
 1085.48. & ealle hi bugon to him. & weron his menn. &
him holdaðas sworon þæt hi woldon ongean ealle oðre men him holde
beon.
 1085.50. Ðanon he ferde into Wiht. forþig he wolde faran into
Normandige & swa dyde syððan.
 1085.51. And þeah he dyde ærest æfter his gewunan. begeat
swiðe mycelne sceatt of his mannan þær he mihte ænige teale tohabban
oððe mid rihte oððe elles.
 1085.54. Ferde þa syððan into Normandige. & Eadgar
Æþeling Ædwardes mæg cynges beah þa fram him forþig he næfde
na mycelne wurðscipe of him. ac se ælmihtiga God him gife wurðscipe on
þam toweardan.
 1085.57. & Cristina þæs æðelinges swuster beah into
mynstre to Rumesege. & underfeng halig rest.
 1085.60. & þæs ilcan geares wæs swiðe hefelic gear.
& swiðe swincfull & sorhfull gear innan Englelande on orfcwealme.
& corn. & wæstmas wæron ætstandene.
 1085.62. & swa mycel ungelimp on wæderunge. swa man naht
æðelice geþencean ne mæg. swa stor þunring. & lægt wes. swa
þæt hit acwealde manige men. & aa hit wyrsode mid mannan swiðor
& swiðor.
 1085.65. GEbete hit God elmihtiga. þonne his willa sy.
 1086.1. Æfter ure Drihtnes Hælendes Cristes gebyrtide. an
þusend wintra & seofan & hundeahtatig wintra. on þam an &
twentigan geare þæs þe Willelm weolde & stihte Engleland swa him God
uðe. gewearð swiðe hefelic and swiðe woldberendlic gear on þissum
lande.
 1086.5. Swylc coðe com on mannum. þæt fullneah æfre þe
oðer man wearð on þam wyrrestan yfele. þet is on ðam drife. &
þet swa stranglice. þæt mænige menn swulton on ðam yfele.
 1086.8. Syððan com þurh þa mycclan ungewiderunge þe comon
swa we beforan tealdon. swyðe mycel hungor ofer eall Engleland. þæt
manig hundred manna earmlice deaðe swulton þurh þone hungor.
 1086.11. Eala hu earmlice & hu reowlic tid wæs ða.
 1086.12. Ða ða wreccæ men lægen fordrifene fullneah to
deaðe. & syððan com se scearpa hungor & adyde hi mid ealle.
 1086.15. Hwam ne mæg earmian swylcere tide?
 1086.15. Oððe hwa is swa heardheort þæt ne mæg wepan
swylces ungelimpes?
 1086.16. Ac swylce þing gewurðaþ for folces synna þæt hi
nellað lufian God & rihtwisnesse.
 1086.18. Swa swa hit wæs þa on ðam dagum. þæt litel
rihtwisnesse wæs on þisum lande mid ænige menn. buton mid munecan ane
þær þær hi wæll ferdon.
 1086.20. Se cyng & þa heafod men lufedon swiðe &
oferswiðe gitsunge. on golde. & on seolfre. & ne rohtan hu synlice
hit wære begytan buton hit come to heom.
 1086.23. Se cyng sealde his land swa deore to male. swa heo deorost
mihte.
 1086.24. Ðonne com sum oðer & bead mare þonne þe oðer
ær sealde. & se cyng hit lett þam menn þe him mare bead.
 1086.26. Ðonne com se þridde. & bead geat mare. & se
cyng hit let þam men to handa þe him eallra meast bead. & ne rohte na
hu swiðe synlice þa gerefan hit begeatan of earme mannon. ne hu manige
unlaga hi dydon.
 1086.29. Ac swa man swyðor spæc embe rihte lage. swa mann dyde
mare unlaga.
 1086.30. Hy arerdon unrihte tollas. & manige oðre unriht hi
dydan. þe sindon earfeþe to areccenne.
 1086.33. Eac on ðam ilcan geare ætforan hærfeste forbarn
þæt halige mynster sancte Paule þe biscopstol on Lundene. &
mænige oðre mynstres. & þæt mæste dæl & þæt
rotteste ealle þære burh.
 1086.35. Swylce eac on ðam ilcan timan forbarn fullneah ælc
heafodport on eallon Englalande.
 1086.37. Eala reowlic & wependlic tid wæs þæs geares.
þe swa manig ungelimp wæs forðbringende.
 1086.39. Eac on þam ilcan geare toforan Assumptio sancte Marie
for Willelm cyng of Normandige into France mid fyrde. & hergode uppan his
agenne hlaford Philippe þam cynge.
 1086.41. & sloh of his mannon mycelne dæl. & forbearnde
þa burh Maðante. & ealle þa halige mynstres þe wæron innon
þære burh. & twegen halige menn þe hyrsumedon Gode on ancersettle
wuniende. þær wæron forbearnde.
 1086.46. Ðissum þus gedone. se cyng Willelm cearde ongean to
Normandige.
 1086.47. Reowlic þing he dyde. & reowlicor him gelamp.
 1086.48. Hu reowlicor?
 1086.48. Him geyfelade. & þæt him stranglice eglade.
 1086.49. Hwæt mæg ic teollan?
 1086.49. Se scearpa deað þe ne forlet ne rice menn. ne heane.
seo hine genam.
 1086.50. He swealt on Normandige on þone nextan dæg æfter
natiuitas sancte Marie. & man bebyrgede hine on Caþum æt sancte
Stephanes mynstre. ærer he hit arærde. & syððan mænifealdlice
gegodade.
 1086.54. Eala hu leas & hu unwrest is þysses middaneardes
wela.
 1086.55. Se þe wæs ærur rice cyng. & maniges landes
hlaford. he næfde þa ealles landes buton seofon fot mæl. & se þe
wæs hwilon gescrid mid golde. & mid gimmum. he læg þa oferwrogen
mid moldan.
 1086.59. He læfde æfter him þreo sunan. Rodbeard het se
yldesta. se wæs eorl on Normandige æfter him. se oðer het Willelm. þe
bær æfter him on Engleland þone kinehelm. Se þridda het Heanric.
þam se fæder becwæð gersuman unateallendlice.
 1086.63. Gif hwa gewilnigeð to gewitane hu gedon mann he wæs.
oððe hwilcne wurðscipe he hæfde. oððe hu fela lande he wære
hlaford. ðonne wille we be him awritan swa swa we hine ageaton. ðe him on
locodan. & oðre hwile on his hirede wunedon.
 1086.68. Se cyng Willelm þe we embe specað wæs swiðe
wisman. & swiðe rice. & wurðfulre and strengere þonne ænig his
foregenga wære.
 1086.70. He wæs milde þam godum mannum þe God lufedon. &
ofer eall gemett stearc þam mannum þe wiðcwædon his willan.
 1086.72. On ðam ilcan steode þe God him geuðe þæt he
moste Engleland gegan. he arerde mære mynster. & munecas þær
gesætte. & hit wæll gegodade.
 1086.74. On his dagan wæs þæt mære mynster on
Cantwarbyrig getymbrad. & eac swiðe manig oðer ofer eall Englaland.
 1086.76. Eac þis land wæs swiðe afylled mid munecan. &
þa leofodan heora lif æfter sanctus Benedictus regule.
 1086.78. & se Cristendom wæs swilc on his dæge þæt
ælc man hwæt his hade to belumpe. folgade se þe wolde.
 1086.80. Eac he wæs swyðe wurðful. þriwa he bær his
cynehelm ælce geare. swa oft swa he wæs on Englelande.
 1086.81. On Eastron he hine bær on Winceastre. on Pentecosten on
Westmynstre. on midewintre on Gleaweceastre.
 1086.83. & þænne wæron mid him ealle þa rice men ofer
eall Englaland. arcebiscopas. & leodbiscopas. abbodas & eorlas.
þegnas & cnihtas.
 1086.85. Swilce he wæs eac swyðe stearc man & ræðe.
swa þæt man ne dorste nan þing ongean his willan don.
 1086.87. He hæfde eorlas on his bendum. þe dydan ongean his
willan.
 1086.88. Biscopas he sætte of heora biscoprice. & abbodas of
heora abbodrice. & þægnas on cweartern. & æt nextan he ne
sparode his agenne broðor. Odo het.
 1086.90. He wæs swiðe rice biscop on Normandige. on Baius
wæs his biscopstol. & wæs manna fyrmest to eacan þam cynge.
 1086.92. & he hæfde eorldom on Englelande. & þonne se
cyng wæs on Normandige. þonne wæs he mægest on þisum lande.
 1086.94. & hine he sætte on cweartern.
 1086.95. Betwyx oðrum þingum nis na to forgytane þæt gode
frið þe he macode on þisan lande. swa þæt an man þe him sylf aht
wære. mihte faran ofer his rice mid his bosum full goldes ungederad. &
nan man ne dorste slean oðerne man. næfde he næfre swa mycel yfel gedon
wið þone oðerne.
 1086.99. & Gif hwilc carl man hæmde wið Wimman hire
unðances. sona he forleas þa limu þe he mid pleagode.
 1086.102. He rixade ofer Englæland. & hit mid his geapscipe
swa þurhsmeade. þæt næs an hid landes innan Englælande. þæt
he nyste hwa heo hæfde. oððe hwæs heo wurð wæs. & syððan
on his gewrit gesætt.
 1086.105. Brytland him wæs on gewealde. & he þær inne
casteles gewrohte. & þet Manncynn mid ealle gewealde.
 1086.107. Swilce eac Scotland he him underþædde. for his
mycele strengþe.
 1086.108. Normandige þæt land wæs his gecynde.
 1086.108. & ofer þone eorldom þe Mans is gehaten he
rixade.
 1086.109. & Gif he moste þa gyt twa gear libban. he hæfde
Yrlande mid his werscipe gewunnon. & wiðutan ælcon wæpnon.
 1086.111. Witodlice on his timan hæfdon men mycel geswinc. &
swiðe manige teonan.
 1086.114. Castelas he let wyrcean & earme men swiðe
swencean.
 1086.116. Se cyng wæs swa swiðe stearc & benam of his
underþeoddan man manig marc goldes & ma hundred punda seolfres.
 1086.119. Ðet he nam be wihte & mid mycelan unrihte of his
landleode for littelre neode.
 1086.121. He wæs on gitsunge befeallan & grædinæsse he
lufode mid ealle.
 1086.123. He sætte mycel deorfrið & he lægde laga
þærwið, þæt swa hwa swa sloge heort oððe hinde, þæt hine
man sceolde blendian.
 1086.126. He forbead þa heortas swylce eac þa baras, swa
swiðe he lufode þa headeor swilce he wære heora fæder.
 1086.129. Eac he sætte be þam haran þæt hi mosten freo
faran.
 1086.130. His rice men hit mændon & þa earme men hit
beceorodan.
 1086.131. Ac he wæs swa stið þæt he ne rohte heora
eallra nið, ac hi moston mid ealle þes cynges wille folgian, gif hi woldon
libban oððe land habban, land oððe eahta oððe wel his sehta.
 1086.135. Wala wa, þæt ænig man sceolde modigan swa hine
sylf upp ahebban & ofer ealle men tellan.
 1086.137. Se ælmihtiga God cyþæ his saule mildheortnisse
& do him his synna forgifenesse.
 1086.139. Ðas þing we habbað be him gewritene. ægðer ge
gode ge yfele. þæt þa godan men niman æfter þeora godnesse. &
for leon mid ealle yfelnesse. & gan on ðone weg. þe us lett to heofonan
rice.
 1086.143. Fela þinga we magon writan þe on ðam ilcan geare
gewordene wæron.
 1086.144. Swa hit wæs on Denmearcan. þæt þa Dænescan
þe wæs ærur geteald eallra folca getreowast. wurdon awende to þære
meste untriwðe. & to þam mæsten swicdome þe æfre mihte
gewurðan.
 1086.147. Hi gecuron & abugan to Cnute cynge. & him aðas
sworon. & syððan hine earhlice ofslogon innan anre cyrcean.
 1086.149. Eac wearð on Ispanie þæt þa hæðenan men
foran & hergodan uppon þam Cristenan mannan. & mycel abegdan to heora
anwealde.
 1086.151. Ac se Cristena cyng, Anphos wæs gehaten, he sende ofer
eall into ælcan lande. & gyrnde fultumes. & him com to fultum of
ælcen lande þe Cristen wæs, & ferdon & ofslogon & aweg
adrifan eall þet hæðena folc. & gewunnon heora land ongean. þurh
Godes fultum.
 1086.156. Eac on þisan ilcan lande on þam ilcan geare.
forðferdon manega rice men. Stigand biscop of Ciceastre. & se abbod of
sancte Augustine. & se abbod of Baðon. & þe of Perscoran. &
ða heora eallra hlaford Willelm Englælandes cyng. þe we ær beforan
embe spæcon.
 1086.160. Æfter his deaðe his sune. Willelm hæt eallswa
þe fæder. feng to þam rice & wearð gebletsod to cynge fram
Landfrance arcebiscop on Westmynstre. þreom dagum ær Michaeles
mæssedæg. & ealle þa men on Englalande him to abugon. & him
aðas sworon.
 1086.164. Ðisum þus gedone. se cyng ferde to Winceastre. &
sceawode þæt madmehus. & þa gersuman þe his fæder ær
gegaderode.
 1086.166. Þa wæron unasecgendlice ænie men hu mycel
þær wæs gegaderod. on golde & on seolfre. & on faton. & on
pællan. & on gimman. & on manige oðre deorwurðe þingon. þe
earfoðe sindon to ateallene.
 1086.169. Se cyng dyde þa swa his fæder him bebead ær he
dead wære. dælde þa gersuman for his fæder saule. to ælcen
mynstre þe wes innan Englelande to suman mynstre <foreign>x</foreign> marc goldes. to suman
<foreign>vi</foreign> & to ælcen cyrcean uppe land <foreign>lx</foreign> pænega. & into ælcere
scire man seonde hundred punda feos. to dælanne earme mannan for his saule.
 1086.174. & ær he forðferde he bead þæt man sceolde
unlesan ealle þa menn þe on hæftnunge wæron under his anwealde.
 1086.176. & se cyng wæs on ðam midewintre on Lundene.
 1087.1. On þisum geare wæs þis land swiðe astirad. &
mid mycele swicdome afylled. swa þæt þa riceste Frencisce men þe weron
innan þisan lande. wolden swican heora hlaforde þam cynge. & woldon
habban his broðer to cynge Rodbeard þe wæs eorl on Normandige.
 1087.5. On þisum ræde wæs ærest Oda biscop. &
Gosfrið biscop. & Willelm biscop on Dunholme.
 1087.6. Swa wæll dyde se cyng be þam biscop. þæt eall
Englaland færde æfter his ræde. & swa swa he wolde. & he
þohte to donne be him eall swa Iudas Scarioth dyde be ure Drihtene.
 1087.9. & Rogere eorl wæs eac æt þam unræde. &
swiðe mycel folc mid heom ealle Frencisce men. & þæs unræd
wærð geræd innan þam lengtene.
 1087.11. Sona swa hit com to þam Eastron. þa ferdon hi &
hergodon & bærndon & aweston þæs cynges feorme hames. &
eallra þæra manna land hi fordydon þe wæron innan þæs cynges
holdscipe.
 1087.14. & heora ælc ferde to his castele. & þone
mannoden & metsoden swa hig betst mihton.
 1087.16. Gosfrið biscop & Rodbeard a Mundbræg ferdon to
Bricgstowe & hergodon & brohton to þam castele þa hergunge. &
syððon foron ut of ðam castele & hergodon Baðon. & eall
þæt land þær abutan. & eall Beorclea hyrnesse hi awæston.
 1087.19. & ða men þe yldest wæron of Hereforde. &
eall þeo scir forð mid. & þa men of Scrobscyre mid mycele folce of
Brytlande comon & hergodon & bærndon on Wiðreceastrescire forð
þæt hi comon to þam porte sylfan. & woldon þa ðæne port
bærnen. & þæt mynster reafian. & þæs cynges castel
gewinnan heom to handa.
 1087.24. Ðas þing geseonde se arwurða biscop Wlstan. wearð
swiðe gedrefed on his mode. forðig him wæs betæht þe castel to
healdene.
 1087.26. Þeah hweðer his hired men ferdon ut mid feawe mannan
of þam castele. & þurh Godes mildheortnisse & þurh þæs
biscopas geearnunga ofslogon & gelæhton fif hundred manna. & þa
oðre ealle aflymdon.
 1087.29. Se biscop of Dunholme dyde to hearme þæt he mihte
ofer eall be norðan.
 1087.30. Roger het an of heom. se hleop into þam castele æt
Norðwic. & dyde git eallra wærst ofer eall þæt land.
 1087.32. Hugo eac an þe hit ne gebette nan þing. ne innan
Lægreceastrescire. ne innan Norðhamtune.
 1087.34. Ðe biscop Odo þe þas þyng of awocan ferde into
Cent to his eorldome. & fordyde hit swyðe. & þæs cynges land.
& þæs arcebiscopas mid ealle aweston. & brohte eall þæt god
into his castele on Hrofeceastre.
 1087.37. Ða þe cyng undergeat ealle þas þing. & hwilcne
swicdom hi dydon toweard his. þa wearð he on his mode swiðe gedrefed.
 1087.39. Sende þa æfter Englisce mannan. & heom
foresæde his neode. & gyrnde heora fultumes.
 1087.40. & behet heom þa betsta laga þa æfre ær
wæs on þisan lande. & ælc unriht geold he forbead. & geatte
mannan heora wudas. and slætinge. ac hit ne stod nane hwile.
 1087.42. Ac Englisce men swa þeah fengon to þam cynge heora
hlaforde on fultume.
 1087.43. Ferdon þa toweard Hrofeceastre. & woldon þone
biscop Odan begytan. þohtan gif hi hæfdon hine þe wæs ærur heafod
to ðam unræde. þæt hi mihton þe bet begytan ealla þa oðre.
 1087.47. Hi comon þa to þam castele to Tonebricge. þa
wæron innan þam castele Oda biscopas cnihtas. & oðre manige þe
hine healdon woldan ongean þone cyng.
 1087.50. Ac þa Englisce men ferdon. & tobræcon þone
castel. & þa men þe þærinne wæron. griðodon wið þone
cyng.
 1087.51. Se cyng mid his here ferde toweard Hrofeceastre. &
wendon þæt se biscop wære þærinne. ac hit wearð þam cynge
cuð þet se biscop wæs afaren to ðam castele a Pefenesea.
 1087.54. & se cyng mid his here ferde æfter. & besætt
þone castel abutan. mid swiðe mycele here fulle six wucan.
 1087.57. Betwyx þissum se eorl of Normandige Rodbeard þes
cynges broðer gaderode swiðe mycel folc. & þohte to gewinnane
Engleland mid þæra manna fultume þe wæron innan þisan lande ongean
þone cyng. & he sende of his mannan to þisum lande. & wolde cuman
himsylf æfter.
 1087.61. Ac þa Englisce men þe wærdedon þære sæ.
gelæhton of þam mannon. & slogon. & adrengton ma þonne ænig
man wiste to tellanne.
 1087.64. Syððan heom ateorede mete wiðinnan þam castele.
ða gyrndon hi griðas. & agefan hine þam cynge.
 1087.65. & se biscop swor þæt he wolde ut of Englelande
faran. & na mare cuman on ðisan lande butan se cyng him æfter sende.
& þæt he wolde agifan þone castel on Hrofeceastre.
 1087.68. Ealswa se biscop ferde & sceolde agifan þone castel.
& se cyng sende his men mid him.
 1087.70. Ða arisan þa men þe wæron innan þam castele.
& namon þone biscop & þes cynges men. & dydon hi on
hæftnunge.
 1087.72. Innan þam castele wæron swiðe gode cnihtas.
Eustatius þe iunga. & Rogeres eorles þreo sunan. & ealle þa
betstboren men. þe wæron innan þisan lande. oððe on Normandige.
 1087.75. Ða se cyng undergeat þas þing. þa ferde he
æfter mid þam here þe he ðær hæfde. & sende ofer eall
Englalande. & bead þæt ælc man þe wære unniðing sceolde
cuman to him, Frencisce & Englisce. of porte & of uppelande.
 1087.78. Him com þa mycel folc to. & he for to Hrofeceastre.
& besætt þone castel. oððet hi griðedon þæ þær inne
wæron. & þone castel ageafon.
 1087.81. Se biscop Odo mid þam mannum þe innan þam castele
wæron ofer sæ ferdon. & se biscop swa forlet þone wurðscipe þe
he on þis land hæfde.
 1087.83. Se cyng syððan sende here to Dunholme. & let
besittan þone castel. & se biscop griðode and ageaf þone castel.
& forlet his biscoprice. & ferde to Normandige.
 1087.86. Eac manige Frencisce men forleton heora land. & ferdon
ofer sæ. & se cyng geaf heora land þam mannum þe him holde
wæron.
 1089.1. On þisum geare se arwurða muneca feder & frouer
Landfranc arcebiscop gewat of þissum life. ac we hopiað þæt he ferde
to þæt heofanlice rice.
 1089.3. Swilce eac gewarð ofer eall Engleland mycel
eorðstyrunge. on þone dæg <foreign>iii IDus Augustus</foreign>.
 1089.4. & wæs swiðe lætsum gear on corne. & on
ælces cynnes wæstmum. swa þæt manig men ræpon heora corn onbutan
Martines mæssan. & gyt lator.
 1090.1. <foreign>INDICTIONE XIII</foreign>.
 1090.1. Ðissum þus gedon. eall swa wæ ær abufan sædan
be þam cynge. & be his broðer. & be his mannon. Se cyng wæs
smægende hu he mihte wrecon his broðer Rodbeard swiðost swencean. &
Normandige of him gewinnan.
 1090.5. Ðeah þurh his geapscipe. oððe þurh gærsuma he
begeat þone castel æt sancte Waleri. & þa hæfenan.
 1090.6. & swa he begeat þone æt Albemare. & þarinne
he sette his cnihtas. & hi dydon hearmes uppon þam lande on hergunge
& on bærnete.
 1090.9. Æfter þisum he begeat ma castelas innan þam lande.
& þær inne his rideras gelogode.
 1090.11. Se eorl of Normandige Rodbeard syððan he undergeat
þæt his gesworene men him trucedon. & agefon hera castelas him to
hearme. þa sende he to his hlaforde Philippe Francena cynge. & he com to
Normandige mid mycelan here.
 1090.14. & se cyng & se eorl mid ormætre fyrde
besæton þone castel abuton. þær þæs cynges men of Engleland inne
wæron.
 1090.16. Se cyng Willelm of Englalande sende to Philippe Francena
cynge. & he for his lufan oððe for his mycele gersuma forlet swa his
man þone eorl Rodbeard & his land. & ferde ongean to France & let
heom swa weorðan.
 1090.20. & betwyx þisum þingum þis land wæs swiðe
fordon. on unlagagelde. & on oðre manige ungelimpe.
 1091.1. On þisum geare se cyng Willelm heold his hired to Cristes
messan on Wæstmynstre. & þær æfter to Candelmæssan he ferde
for his broðær unþearfe ut of Englalande into Normandige.
 1091.4. On mang þam þe he þær wæs. heora sehte
togædere eode. on þæt gerad þæt se eorl him to handan let Uescam.
& þone eorldom æt Ou. & Kiæresburh. And þær to eacan þes
cynges men sacleas beon moston. on þam castelan. þe hi ær þes eorles
unþances begiten hæfdon.
 1091.8. & Se cyng him ongean þa Manige behet, þe ær
heora fæder gewann. & þa fram þam eorle gebogen wæs, gebygle to
donne. & eall þæt his fæder þær begeondan hæfde. butan
þam þe he þam cynge þa geunnen hæfde.
 1091.12. & þæt ealle þa þe on Englelande for þam
eorle æror heora land forluron. hit on þisum sehte habban sceoldan. &
se eorl on Englelande eall swa mycel swa on heora forewarde wæs.
 1091.15. And gif se eorl forðferde butan sunu be rihtre æwe.
wære se cyng yrfenuma of eallon Normandig. Be þisre sylfan forewarde gif
se cyng swulte. wære se eorl yrfenuma ealles Englalandes.
 1091.18. Ðas forewarde gesworan <foreign>xii</foreign> þa betste of þes cynges
healfe. and <foreign>xii</foreign> of þes eorles. þeah hit syððan litle hwile stode.
 1091.21. On mang þisum sæhte wearð Eadgar æþeling
belandod. of þam þe se eorl him æror þær to handa gelæten
hæfde. & ut of Normandig for to þam cynge his aðume to Scotlande.
& to his swustor.
 1091.25. On mang þam þe se cyng Willelm ut of Englelande
wæs. ferde se cyng Melcolm of Scotlande hider into Englum. & his mycelne
dæl oferhergode. oð þæt þa gode mæn þe þis land bewiston.
him fyrde ongean sændon. & hine gecyrdon.
 1091.28. Ða þa se cyng Willelm into Normandige þis gehyrde.
þa gearcode he his fare. & to Englelande com. & his broðer se eorl
Rodbeard mid him.
 1091.31. & sona fyrde het ut abeodan. ægðer scipfyrde
& landfyrde. ac seo scipfyrde ær he to Scotlande cuman mihte.
ælmæst earmlice forfor. feowan dagon toforan sancte Michæles
mæssan.
 1091.34. And se cyng & his broðer mid þære landfyrde
ferdon. ac þa ða se cyng Melcolm gehyrde þæt hine man mid fyrde secean
wolde. he for mid his fyrde ut of Scotlande into Loðene on Englaland &
þær abad.
 1091.37. Ða þa se cyng Willelm mid his fyrde genealehte. þa
ferdon betwux Rodbeard eorl & Eadgar æðeling & þæra cinga
sehte swa gemacedon. þæt se cyng Melcolm to uran cynge com. & his man
wearð to eall swilcre gehyrsumnisse swa he ær his fæder dyde. &
þæt mid aðe gefestnode.
 1091.42. & se cyng Willelm him behet on lande & on ealle
þinge þæs þe he under his fæder ær hæfde.
 1091.45. On þisum sehte wearð eac Eadgar eþeling wið þone
cyng gesæhtlad. & þa cyngas þa mid mycclum sehte tohwurfon. ac
þæt litle hwile stod.
 1091.47. And se eorl Rodbeard her oð Cristes mæsse forneah mid
þam cynge wunode. & litel soðes þær on mang. of heora forewarde
onfand. & twam dagon ær þære tide on Wiht scipode. & into
Normandig for. & Eadgar æðeling mid him.
 1092.1. On þisum geare se cyng Willelm mid mycelre fyrde ferde
norð to Cardeol. & þa burh geæðstaþelede. & þone castel
arerde. & Dolfin utadraf þe æror þær þes landes weold. &
þone castel mid his mannan gesette.
 1092.4. & syððan hider suð gewænde. & mycele
mænige Eyrlisces folces mid wifa & mid orfe þyder sænde. þær
to wunigenne þæt land to tilianne.
 1093.1. On þisum geare to þam længtene warð se cyng
Willelm on Gleaweceastre to þam swiðe geseclod. þæt he wæs ofer
eall dead gekyd.
 1093.3. & on his broke he Gode fela behæsa behet. his agen
lif on riht to lædene. & Godes cyrcean griðian & friðian. &
næfre ma eft wið feo gesyllan. & ealle rihte lage on his þeode to
habbene.
 1093.6. And þæt arcebiscoprice on Cantwarbyrig þe ær on
his agenre hand stod. Anselme betæhte. se wæs ær abbod on Bæc.
& Rodbeard his cancelere þæt biscoprice on Lincolne.
 1093.9. & to manegan mynstren land geuðe. ac þæt he
syððan ætbræd. þa him gebotad wæs. & ealle þa gode laga
forlæt. þe he us ær behet.
 1093.12. Ða æfter þisson sende se cyng of Scotlande. &
þære forewarde gyrnde þe him behaten wæs.
 1093.13. And se cing Willelm him steofnode to Gloweceastre. &
him to Scotlande gislas sende. & Eadgar æþeling æfter. & þa
men syððan ongean. þe hine mid mycclon wurðscipe to þam cynge
brohtan.
 1093.16. Ac þa ða he to þam cynge com ne mihte he beon
weorðe naðer ne ure cynges spæce. ne þæra forewarde þe him ær
behatene wæron. & forþi hi þa mid mycelon unsehte tohwurfon. &
se cyng Melcolm ham to Scotlande gewænde.
 1093.20. Ac hraðe þæs þe he ham com. he his fyrde
gegaderode. & into Englelande hergende mid maran unræde ferde þone him
abehofode. & hine þa Rodbeard se eorl of Norðhymbran mid his mannan
unwæres besyrede & ofsloh.
 1093.24. Hine sloh Moræl of Bæbbaburh. se wæs þæs
eorles stiward. & Melcolmes cynges godsib.
 1093.26. Mid him wæs eac Eadward his sune ofslagen. se æfter
him cyng beon sceolde. gif he hit gelifode.
 1093.27. Ða þa seo gode cwen Margarita þis gehyrde. hyre þa
leofstan hlaford & sunu þus beswikene. heo wearð oð deað on mode
geancsumed. & mid hire prestan to cyrcean eode. & hire gerihtan
underfeng. & æt Gode abæd. þæt heo hire gast ageaf.
 1093.31. & ða Scottas þa Dufenal to cynge gecuron Melcolmes
broðer. & ealle þa Englisce ut adræfdon. þe ær mid þam cynge
Melcolme wæron.
 1093.33. Ða þa Dunecan Melcolmes cynges sunu þis eall gehyrde
þus gefaren. se on þæs cynges hyrede Willelmes wæs. swa swa his
fæder hine ures cynges fæder ær to gisle geseald hæfde. & her
swa syððan belaf. he to þam cynge com.
 1093.37. & swilce getrywða dyde. swa se cyng æt him habban
wolde. & swa mid his unne to Scotlande for. mid þam fultume þe he
begytan mihte Engliscra & Frenciscra. and his mæge Dufenal þes rices
benam. & to cynge wearð underfangen.
 1093.41. Ac þa Scottas hi eft sume gegaderoden. & forneah
ealle his mænu ofslogan. & he sylf mid feawum ætbærst.
 1093.43. Syððan hi wurdon sehte. on þa gerad þæt he
næfre eft Englisce ne Frencisce into þam lande ne gelogige.
 1094.1. Her hæfde se cyng Willelm to Cristes mæssan his hired
æt Gleaweceastre. & him þider fram his broðer Rodbearde of Normandig
bodan coman.
 1094.3. Þa cyddon þæt his broðer grið & forewarde
eall æfter cwæð. butan se cyng gelæstan wolde eall þet hi on
forewarde hæfdon ær gewroht. & uppon þæt hine forsworenne &
trywleasne clypode. buton he þa forewarda geheolde. oððe þider ferde
& hine þær betealde þær seo forewarde ær wæs gewroht &
eac gesworen.
 1094.9. Ða ferde se cyng to Hæstingan to þam
Candelmæssan. & on mang þam þe he þær wederes abad. he let
halgian þæt mynster æt þære Bataille. & Herbearde Losange
þam biscop of þeotfordan his stæf benam.
 1094.12. & þær æfter to midlengtene ofer sæ for into
Normandige.
 1094.13. Syððan he þider com. he & his broðer Rodbeard
se eorl gecwæðan. þæt hi mid griðe togædere cuman sceoldan.
& swa dydon. & gesemede beon ne mihtan.
 1094.15. Syððan eft hi togædere coman mid þam ilcan mannan
þe ær þæt loc makedon. & eac þa aðas sworen. & ealne
þone bryce uppon þone cyng tealdon. ac he nolde þæs geþafa beon. ne
eac þa forewarde healdan. & forþam hi þa mid mycelon unsehte
tocyrdon.
 1094.21. And se cyng syððan þone castel æt Bures gewann.
& þes eorles men þær inne genam. þa sume hyder to lande sende.
 1094.23. Ðær togeanes se eorl mid þes cynges fultume of
France gewann þone castel æt Argentses . & þear inne Rogger Peiteuin
genam. & seofen hundred þes cynges cnihta mid him. & syððan
þone æt Hulme.
 1094.26. & Oft rædlice heora ægðer uppon oðerne tunas
bærnde. & eac menne læhte.
 1094.28. Ða sende se cyng hider to lande. & het abeodan ut
<foreign>xx</foreign> þusenda Engliscra manna him to fultume to Normandig. ac þa hi to sæ
coman. þa het hi man cyrran. & þæt feoh syllan to þæs cynges
behofe þe hi genumen hæfdon. þet wæs ælc man healf punda. & hi
swa dydon.
 1094.33. & se eorl innon Normandig æfter þison mid þam
cynge of France. & mid eallon þan þe hi gegaderian mihton ferdon
towardes Ou þær se cyng Willelm inne wæs. & þohtan hine inne to
besittanne. & swa foran oð hi coman to Lungeuile.
 1094.37. Ðær wearð se cyng of France þurh gesmeah
gecyrred. & swa syððan eall seo fyrding tohwearf.
 1094.38. Her onmang þison se cyng Willelm sende æfter his
broðer Heanrige. se wæs on þam castele æt Damfront. ac forþi þe
he mid friðe þurh Normandig faran ne mihte. he him sende scipon æfter.
& Hugo eorl of Ceastre.
 1094.42. Ac þa ða hi towardes Ou faran sceoldan þær se
cyng wæs. hi foran to Englelande. & up coman æt Hamtune on ealra
halgena mæsseæfne. & her syððon wunedon. & to Cristes
mæssan wæron on Lunden.
 1094.46. Eac on þisum ylcan geare þa Wylisce menn hi
gegaderodon. & wið þa Frencisce þe on Walon. oððe on þære
neawiste wæron & hi ær belandedon. gewinn upahofon. & manige
festena & castelas abræcon. & men ofslogon.
 1094.49. An syððan heora gefylce weox. hi hi on ma
todældon.
 1094.50. Wið sum þæra dæle gefeaht Hugo eorl of
Scrobscire & hi aflymde.
 1094.51. Ac þeah hweðer þa oðre. ealles þæs geares
nanes yfeles ne geswicon þe hi don mihton.
 1094.54. Ðises geares eac þa Scottas heora cyng Dunecan
besyredon & ofslogan. & heom syððan eft oðre syðe his
fæderan Dufenal to cynge genamon. þurh þes lare & to tihtinge he
wearð to deaðe beswicen.
 1095.1. On þisum geare wæs se cyng Willelm to Cristes
mæssan þa feower forewarde dagas on Hwitsand. & æfter þam
feorðan dæge hider to lande for. & upp com æt Doferan.
 1095.3. And Heanrig þes cynges broðer her on lande oð lengten
wunode. & þa ofer sæ for to Normandig mid mycclon gersuman. on
þæs cynges heldan uppon heora broðer Rodbeard eorl.
 1095.6. & gelomlice uppon þone eorl wann. & him mycelne
hearm ægðer on lande & on mannan dyde.
 1095.9. And þa to Eastran heold se cyng his hired on Winceastre.
& se eorl Rodbeard of Norðhymbran nolde to hirede cuman.
 1095.11. & se cyng forðan wearð wið hine swiðe astyrod.
& him to sænde & heardlice bead gif he griðes weorðe beon wolde.
þæt he to Pentecosten to hired come.
 1095.13. On þisum geare wæron Eastron on <foreign>viii kalendæ
Aprilis</foreign>.
 1095.14. & þa uppon Eastron on sancte Ambrosius mæsse
niht. þæt is <foreign>ii Nonæ Aprilis</foreign> wæs gesewen forneah ofer eall þis
land swilce forneah ealle þa niht swiðe mænifealdlice steorran of
heofenan feollan. naht be anan oððe twam. ac swa þiclice þæt hit nan
mann ateallan ne mihte.
 1095.18. Her æfter to Pentecosten wæs se cyng on Windlesoran.
& ealle his witan mid him. butan þam eorle of Norðhymbran. forþam se
cyng him naþer nolde ne gislas syllan. ne uppon trywðan geunnon þæt he
mid griðe cumon moste & faran.
 1095.23. & se cyng forþi his fyrde bead. & uppon þone
eorl to Norðhymbran for.
 1095.24. & sona þes þe he þider com. he manege &
forneah ealle þa betste of þes eorles hirede innan anan fæstene gewann.
& on hæftene gedyde.
 1095.26. & þone castel æt Tinemuðan besæt oððet
he hine gewann. & þæs eorles broðer þærinne & ealle þa
þe him mid wæron. and syððan ferde to Bebbaburh. & þone eorl
þærinne besæt.
 1095.29. Ac þa ða se cyng geseah þæt he hine gewinnan ne
mihte. þa het he makian ænne castel to foran Bebbaburh. & hine on his
spæce Malueisin het. þæt is on Englisc Yfel nehhebur.
 1095.32. & hine swiðe mid his mannan gesætte. &
syððan suðweard for.
 1095.33. Ða sona æfter þam þe se cyng wæs suð afaren.
feorde se eorl anre nihte ut of Bebbaburh towardes Tinemuðan.
 1095.35. Ac þa þe innan þam niwan castele wæron. his
gewær wurdon. & him æfter foran & onfuhton. & hine
gewundedon. & syððan gelæhton. & þa þe mid him wæron sume
ofslogan. sume lifes gefengon.
 1095.39. Onmang þison wearð þam cynge cuð. þæt þa
Wylisce men on Wealon sumne castel heafdon tobroken Muntgumni hatte. &
Hugon eorles menn ofslagene þe hine healdon sceoldan.
 1095.41. & he forþi oðre fyrde het fearlice abannan. &
æfter sancte Michaelesmæsse into Wealan ferde.
 1095.42. & his fyrde toscyfte. & þæt land eall
þurhfor. swa þæt seo fyrde eall togædere com to ealra halgena to
Snawdune.
 1095.45. Ac þa Wylisce a toforan into muntan and moran ferdan
þæt heom man to cuman ne mihte. & se cyng þa hamweard gewende
forþam he geseah þæt he þær þes wintres mare don ne mihte.
 1095.49. Ða þa se cyng ongean com. þa het he niman þone
eorl Rotbeard of Norðhymbran & to Bæbbaburh lædan. & ægðer
eage utadon. buton þa þe þær inne wæron þone castel agyfan
woldan.
 1095.52. Hine heoldan his wif. & Moreal se wæs stiward &
eac his mæg.
 1095.53. Ðurh þis wearð se castel þa agyfen. & Moreal
wearð þa on þes cynges hirede. & þurh hine wurdon manege ægðer
ge gehadode & eac læwede geypte. þe mid heora ræde on þes cynges
unheldan wæron.
 1095.56. Þa se cyng sume ær þære tide het on
hæftneðe gebringan. & syððan swiðe gemahlice ofer eall þis
land beodan. þæt ealle þa þe of þam cynge land heoldan. eall swa hi
friðes weorðe beon woldan. þæt hi on hirede to tide wæron.
 1095.60. And þone eorl Rotbert het se cyng to Windlesoran
lædan. & þær innan þam castele healdan.
 1095.62. Eac on þis ylcan geare togeanes Eastron com þæs
Papan sande hider to lande. þæt wæs Waltear bisceop swiðe god lifes
man of Albin þære ceastre. & þam arcebiscope Ansealme uppon
Pentecosten of þæs Papan healfe Urbanus his pallium geaf.
 1095.65. & he hine underfeng æt his arcestole on
Cantwarabyrig. and se biscop Waltear her on lande þæs geares syððan
lange wunode. & man syððan þæt Rom gesceot be him sende. swa man
manegan gearan æror ne dyde.
 1095.70. Ðises ylcan eac geares wæron swiðe untid gewidera.
& forþi geond eall þis land wurdon eorðwæstmas eall to medemlice
gewende.
 1096.1. On þison geare heold se cyng Willelm his hired to Cristes
mæssan on Windlesoran.
 1096.2. & Willelm biscop of Dunholme þær forðferde to
geares dæge.
 1096.3. And on Octabris Epiphanis wæs se cyng & ealle his
witan on Searbyrig.
 1096.4. Þær beteah Gosfrei Bainard Willelm of Ou þes cynges
mæg þæt he heafde gebeon on þes cynges swicdome. & hit him on
gefeaht. & hine on orreste ofercom.
 1096.7. & syððan he ofercumen wæs. him het se cyng þa
eagan utadon. & syþðan belisnian.
 1096.8. & his stiward Willelm hatte. se wæs his modrian
sunu. het se cyng on rode ahon.
 1096.10. Ðær wearð eac Eoda eorl of Campaine þæs cynges
aðum & manege oðre belende. & sumne man to Lundene lædde. &
þær spilde.
 1096.12. Ðises geares eac to þam Eastran wearð swiðe mycel
styrung geond ealle þas þeode. & fela oðra þeodan þurh Urbanus se
wæs Papa gehaten þeah þe he þæs setles naþing næfde on Rome.
 1096.14. & ferde unarimedlice folc mid wifan & cildan to
þi þæt hi uppon hæðene þeodan winnan woldan.
 1096.16. Ðurh þas fare wearð se cyng & his broðor
Rodbeard eorl sehte. swa þæt se cyng ofer sæ for. & eall Normandig
æt him mid feo alisde. swa swa hi þa sehte wæron.
 1096.19. And se eorl syððan ferde. & mid him se eorl of
Flandran. & se of Bunan. & eac manige oðre heafodmen. & se eorl
Rotbeard & þa þe mid him ferdon þone winter on Puille wunedon.
 1096.22. Ac þes folces þe be Hungrie for. fela þusenda
þær & be wæge earmlice forforan. & fela hreowlice &
hungerbitene ongean winterham tugon.
 1096.25. Ðis wæs swiðe hefigtime gear geond eall Angelcyn.
ægðer ge þurh mænigfealde gylda. & eac þurh swiðe hefigtymne
hunger. þe þisne eard þæs geares swiðe gedrehte.
 1096.28. Eac on þison geare þa heafodmen þe þis land
heoldan oft rædlice fyrde into Wealon sendon. & mænig man mid þam
swiðe gedrehtan. ac man þær ne gespædde. butan manmyrringe. &
feohspillinge.
 1097.1. Her on þison geare weas se cyng Willelm to Cristes
mæssan on Normandig. & þa togeanes Eastron hider to lande for.
forþam he þohte his hired on Winceastre to healdenne.
 1097.3. Ac he wearð þurh weder gelet. oððet Eastre æfen
þæt he up com ærost æt Arundel. & forþi his hired æt
Windlesoran heold.
 1097.6. & þær æfter mid mycclum here into Wealon ferde.
& þæt land swiðe mid his fyrde þurhfor. þurh sume þa Wyliscean
þe him to wæron cumen & his lædteowas wæron.
 1097.8. & þær innewunode fram middesumeran forneah oð
August. & mycel þær inne forleas on mannan & on horsan. & eac
on manegan oðran þingan.
 1097.10. Ða Wylisce men syððon hi fram þam cynge gebugon.
heom manege ealdras of heom sylfan gecuron. sum þæra wæs Caduugaun
gehaten þe heora weorðast wæs. se wæs Griffines broðer sunu
cynges.
 1097.14. Ac þa ða se cyng geseah þæt he nan þingc his
willes þær geforðian ne mihte. he ongean into þison lande for. &
hraðe æfter þam. he be þam gemæron castelas let gemakian.
 1097.17. Ða uppon sancte Michaeles mæssan <foreign>iiii Nonæ
Octobris</foreign> ætywde an selcuð steorra on æfen scynende & sona to setle
gangende.
 1097.18. He wæs gesewen suðweast. & se leoma þe him
ofstod. wæs swiðe lang geþuht suðeast scinende. & forneah ealle
þa wucan on þas wisan ætywde.
 1097.21. Manige men leton þæt hit cometa wære.
 1097.22. Sona æfter þyson. se arcebiscop Ansealm of
Cantwarbyrig. leafe æt þam cynge nam. þeah hit þam cynge unge will
wære þæs þe men leton. & ofer sæ for. forþam him þuhte
þæt man on þisne þeodan lytel æfter rihte & æfter his dyhte
dyde.
 1097.26. And se cyng þær æfter uppon sancte Martines
mæssan ofer sæ into Normandig for. ac þa hwile þe he wederes abad.
his hired innon þam sciran þær hi lagon. þone mæston hearm dydon
þe æfre hired oððe here innon friðlande don sceolde.
 1097.29. Ðis wæs on eallon þingan swiðe hefigtyme gear.
& ofer geswincfull. on ungewederan þa man oððe tilian sceolde.
oððe eft tilða gegaderian. & on ungyldan þa næfre ne ablunnon.
 1097.32. Eac manege sciran þe mid weorce to Lundenne belumpon.
wurdon þærle gedrehte. þurh þone weall þe hi worhton onbutan þone
tur. & þurh þa brycge þe forneah eall toflotan wæs. & þurh
þæs cynges healle geweorc þe man on Westmynstre worhte. & mænige
man þær mid gedrehte.
 1097.38. Eac on þysum ylcan geare sona uppon sancte Michaeles
mæssan ferde Eadgar æþeling mid fyrde þurh þæs cynges fultum
into Scotlande. & þet land mid stranglicum feohte gewann.
 1097.40. & þone cyng Dufenal ut adræfde. & his mæg
Eadgar se wæs Melcolmes sunu cynges & Margarite þære cwenan he
þær on þæs cynges Willelmes heldan to cynge gesette. & syððan
ongean into Engleland for.
 1098.1. On þysum geare to Cristes mæssan wæs se cyng
Willelm on Normandig.
 1098.2. & Walcelin biscop on Winceastre. & Baldewine abbod
on sancte Ædmund innan þære tide bægen forðferdan.
 1098.3. & On þisum geare eac Turold abbod of Burh
forðferde.
 1098.5. Ðises geares eac to þan sumeran innan Barrucscire æt
Finchamstæde an mere blod weoll. swa swa manige trywe men sædan þe hit
geseon sceoldan.
 1098.8. & Hugo eorl wearð ofslagen innan Anglesege fram
utwikingan. & his broðer Rodbert wearð his yrfenuma. swa swa he hit
æt þam cynge ofeode.
 1098.11. Toforan sancte Michaeles mæssan ætywde seo heofon
swilce heo forneah ealle þa niht byrnende wære.
 1098.12. Ðis wæs swiðe geswincfull gear þurh manigfealde
ungyld. & þurh mycele renas þe ealles geares ne ablunnon. forneah
ælc tilð on mersclande forferde.
 1099.1. Her wæs se cyng Willelm to midewintra on Normandig.
& to Eastron hider to lande com. & to Pentecosten forman siðe his
hired innan his niwan gebyttlan æt Westmynstre heold.
 1099.4. & þær Rannulfe his capellane þæt biscoprice
on Dunholme geaf. þe æror ealle his gemot ofer eall Engleland draf. &
bewiste.
 1099.5. & sona þær æfter ofer sæ for. & þone
eorl Elias of þære Manige adraf. & hy syððan on his geweald
gesætte. & swa to sancte Michaeles mæssan eft hider to lande com.
 1099.9. Ðises geares eac on sancte Martines mæssedæg.
asprang up to þan swiðe sæflod. & swa mycel to hearme gedyde. swa
nan man ne gemunet þæt hi æfre æror dyde.
 1099.11. & wæs ðæs ylcan dæges luna prima.
 1099.13. And Osmund biscop of Searbyrig innon Aduent forðferde.
 1100.1. On þison geare se cyng Willelm heold his hired to Cristes
mæssa on Gleaweceastre. & to Eastron on Winceastre. & to Pentecosten
on Westmynstre.
 1100.4. & to þam Pentecosten wæs gesewen innan Barrucscire
æt anan tune blod weallan of eorþan. swa swa mænige sædan þe hit
geseon sceoldan.
 1100.6. And þær æfter on morgen æfter hlam
mæssedæge wearð se cyng Willelm on huntnoðe fram his anan men mid
anre fla ofsceoten. & syððan to Winceastre gebroht. & on þam
biscoprice bebyrged. þæt wæs þæs þreotteðan geares þe he
rice onfeng.
 1100.11. He wæs swiðe strang & reðe ofer his land &
his mænn. & wið ealle his neahheburas. & swiðe ondrædendlic.
 1100.12. & þurh yfelra manna rædas þe him æfre
gecweme wæran. & þurh his agene gitsunga. he æfre þas leode mid
here & mid ungylde tyrwigende wæs.
 1100.15. Forþan þe on his dagan ælc riht afeoll. &
ælc unriht for Gode & for worulde up aras.
 1100.16. Godes cyrcean he nyðerade. & þa biscoprices &
abbotrices þe þa ealdras on his dagan feollan.
 1100.17. Ealle he hi oððe wið feo gesealde. oððe on his
agenre hand heold. & to gafle gesette. forþan þe he ælces mannes
gehadodes & læwedes yrfenuma beon wolde.
 1100.20. & swa þæt þæs dæges þe he gefeoll. he
heafde on his agenre hand þæt arcebiscoprice on Cantwarbyrig. &
þæt bisceoprice on Winceastre. & þæt on Searbyrig. & xi
abbodrices. ealle to gafle gesette.
 1100.23. And þeah þe ic hit læng ylde. eall þet þe Gode
wæs lað & rihtfullan mannan. eall þæt wæs gewunelic on þisan
lande on his tyman. & forþi he wæs forneah ealre his leode lað.
& Gode andsæte.
 1100.26. Swa swa his ænde ætywde. forþan þe he on
middewardan his unrihte buten behreowsunge & ælcere dædbote gewat.
 1100.29. On þæne þunresdæg he wæs ofslagen. &
þæs on morgen bebyrged.
 1100.30. & syðþan he bebyrged wæs. þa witan þe þa
neh handa wæron. his broðer Heanrig to cynge gecuran.
 1100.31. & he þærrihte þæt biscoprice on Winceastre
Willelme Giffarde geaf. & siþþan to Lundene for.
 1100.33. & on þan Sunnandæge þær æfter toforan
þam weofode on Westmynstre Gode & eallan folce behet ealle þa unriht to
aleggenne þe on his broðer timan wæran. & þa betstan lage to
healdene þe on æniges cynges dæge toforan him stodan.
 1100.37. And hine syððan æfter þam se biscop of Lundene
Mauricius to cynge gehalgode. & him ealle on þeosan lande to abugan.
& aðas sworan. & his men wurdon.
 1100.40. And se cyng sona æfter þam be þære ræde þe
him abutan wæran. þone biscop Rannulf of Dunholme let niman. & into
þam ture on Lundene let gebringon. & þær healdan.
 1100.42. Ða to foran Sancte Michaeles mæssan com se arcebiscop
Ansealm of Cantwarbyrig hider to lande. swa swa se cyng Heanrig be his witena
ræde him æfter sende. forþan þe he wæs ut of þis lande gefaren.
forþan mycelan unrihte þe se cyng Willelm him dyde.
 1100.47. And siðþan sona heræfter se cyng genam Mahalde him
to wife Malcolmes cynges dohter of Scotlande. & Margareta þære goda
cwæne Eadwardes cynges magan. & of þan rihtan Ængla landes
kynekynne.
 1100.50. & on sancte Martines mæssedæg heo wearð him
mid mycelan weorðscipe forgifen on Westmynstre. & se arcebiscop Ansealm
hi him bewæddade. & siððan to cwene gehalgode.
 1100.53. And se arcebiscop Thomas of Eoferwic her æfter sona
forðferde.
 1100.55. Ðeoses ylces geares eac innan hærfest com se eorl
Rotbert ham into Normandi. & se eorl Rotbert of Flandran. & Eustatius
eorl of Bunan fram Ierusalem.
 1100.57. & sona swa se eorl Rotbert into Normandig com. he
wearð fram eallan þam folce bliþelice underfangen. butan þam castelan
ðe wæron gesætte mid þæs cynges Heanriges manna. togeanes þan he
manega gewealc & gewinn hæfde.
 1101.1. Her on þisum geare to Cristes mæssan heold se cyng
Heanrig his hired on Westmynstre. & to Eastran on Winceastre.
 1101.3. & þa sona þæræfter wurdon þa heafodmen her
on lande wiðerræden togeanes þam cynge. ægðer ge for heoran agenan
mycelan ungetrywðan. & eac þurh þone eorl Rodbert of Normandig. þe
mid unfriðe hider to lande fundode.
 1101.6. And se cyng syððan scipa ut on sæ sende his broðer
to dære & to lættinge. ac hi sume æft æt þære neode
abruðon. & fram þam cynge gecyrdon. & to þam eorle Rotberte
gebugan.
 1101.9. Ða to midde sumeran ferde se cyng ut to Pefenesæ mid
eall his fyrde togeanes his broðer & his þær abad. ac onmanig
þison com se eorl Rotbert up æt Portesmuðan <foreign>xii</foreign> nihtan toforan
Hlafmæssan.
 1101.13. & se cyng mid ealre his fyrde him togeanes com. ac
þa heafod men heom betwenan foran.
 1101.14. & þa broðra gesehtodan on þa gerad. þet se
cyng forlet eall þæt he mid streangðe innan Normandig togeanes þam
eorle heold. & þæt ealle þa on Englelande heora land ongean heafdon.
þe hit ær þurh þone eorl forluron. & Eustaties eorl eac eall his
fæder land her on lande.
 1101.19. & þet se eorl Rotbert ælce geare sceolde of
Englalande þreo þusend marc seolfres habban. & loc hweðer þæra
gebroðra oðerne oferbide. wære yrfeweard ealles Englalandes & eac
Normandiges. buton se forðfarena yrfenuman heafde be rihtre æwe.
 1101.23. & þis þa mid aðe gefestnodan <foreign>xii</foreign> þa hihste
of ægðre healfe.
 1101.24. And se eorl syððan oð ðet ofer sancte Michaeles
mæsse her on lande wunode. & his men mycel to hearme æfre gedydon swa
hi geferdon. þa hwile þe se eorl her on lande wunode.
 1101.27. Ðises geares eac se biscop Rannulf to þam
Candelmæssan ut of þam ture on Lunden nihtes oðbærst þær he on
hæftneðe wæs. & to Normandige for. þurh þes macunge mæst
& to spryttinge se eorl Rotbert þises geares þis land mid unfriðe
gesohte.
 1102.1. On þisum geare to Natiuiteð wæs se cyng Heanrig on
Westmynstre. & to Eastron on Winceastre.
 1102.2. & sona þær æfter wurdon unsehte se cyng &
se eorl Rotbert of Bælæsme se hæfde þone eorldom her on lande on
Scrobbesbyrig þe his fæder Roger eorl ær ahte. & micel rice
þærto. ægðer ge beheonon sæ ge begeondon.
 1102.6. & se cyng ferde & besæt þone castel æt
Arundel. ac þa he hine swa hraðe gewinnan ne mihte. he let þær toforan
castelas gemakian. & hi mid his mannan gesette.
 1102.9. & syððan mid ealre his fyrde ferde to Brigge. &
þær wunode oððet he þone castel hæfde. & þone eorl Rotbert
belænde. & ealles benæmde. þes he on Englalande hæfde.
 1102.11. & se eorl swa ofer sæ gewat. & se fyrde
syððan ham cyrde.
 1102.13. Ða þær æfter to sancte Michaeles mæssan
wæs se cyng æt Wæstmynstre. & ealle þa hæfodmen on þis
lande gehadode & læwede.
 1102.15. & se arcebiscop Ansealm heold gehadodra manna sinoð.
& hi þær manega beboda setton þe to Cristendome belimpað.
 1102.16. & ægðer manige Frencisce & Englisce þær
heora stafas & rice forluron. þe hi mid unrihte begeaton. oððe mid
woge þær on lifedon.
 1102.19. & On ðisum ylcan geare on Pentecosten mæssan
wuce. þa coman þeofas sum of Aluearnie. sum of France. & sum of
Flandres. & breokan þa mynstre of Burh & þærinne naman mycel to
gode on golde & on seolfre. þet wæron roden & calicen &
candelsticcan.
 1103.1. Her on þisum geare to midewintra wæs se cyng Heanrig
æt Westmynstre.
 1103.2. & þær æfter sona ferde se biscop Willelm
Giffard ut of þis land. forþan þe he ongean riht nolde his hades onfon
æt þam arcebiscop Girarde of Eoferwic.
 1103.4. & þa to þan Eastran heold se cyng his hired on
Winceastre.
 1103.5. & þær æfter ferde se arcebiscop Ansealm of
Cantwarbyrig to Rome. swa swa him & þam cynge gewearð.
 1103.8. Ðises geares eac com se eorl Rotbert of Normandig to
sprecene wið þone cyng her on lande.
 1103.9. & ær he heonne ferde he forgeaf þa þreo þusend
marc þe him seo cyng Heanrig be foreweard ælce geare gifan sceolde.
 1103.12. On þisum geare eac æt Heamstede innan Barrucscire.
wæs gesewen blod of eorðan.
 1103.13. Ðis wæs swiðe gedeorfsum gear her on lande. þurh
mænifealde gyld.& þurh orfcwealm. & wæstma for weorþenesse
ægðer ge on corne. & eac on eallon treowwæstman.
 1103.16. Eac on morgen uppon sancte Laurenties mæssedæg
gedyde se wind swa mycel to hearme her on lande on eallon wæstman. swa nan
man ne gemunde þæt æfre ænig ær gedyde.
 1103.19. On ðisum ylcan geare Mathias abbod of Burh forðferde.
se ne lyfode na leng þan an geare. syððan he abbod wæs.
 1103.20. Æfter sancte Michaeles mæssan on <foreign>xii kalendæ
Novembris</foreign> he wæs mid procession underfangan to abbod. & on ðam ylcan
dæge þes oðres geares he wearð dead on Gleawceastre. & þær
bebyrged.
 1104.1. Her on þisum geare to Cristes mæssan heold se cyng
Heanrig his hired æt Wæstminstre. & to Eastron on Winceastre. &
to Pentecosten eft on Westmynstre.
 1104.4. Ðises geares wæs se forma Pentecostes dæg on
<foreign>Nonæ Iunii</foreign>.
 1104.4. & on þam Tiwæsdæge þæræfter ætywdan
feower circulas to þam mid dæge onbutan þære sunnan hwites hiwes.
ælc under oðran gebroiden. swylce hi gemette wæron.
 1104.7. Ealle þe hit gesawon wundredon. forþan hi næfre
ær swilce ne gemundon.
 1104.9. Heræfter wurdon sehte se eorl Rotbert of Normandig.
& Rotbert de Bælesme þe se cyng Heanri æror belænd hæfde
& of Englalande adrifen.
 1104.11. & þurh heora sehte wurdon wiðerræde se cyng of
Englalande & se eorl of Normandig.
 1104.12. & se cyng his folc ofer sæ into Normandig sende.
& þa heafodmen þær on lande hi underfengon.
 1104.14. & on heora hlafordes þæs eorles swicdome into
heora castelan gelogodan. þanon hi manige gedrecednissa on hergunga & on
bærninge þam eorle gedydon.
 1104.16. Eac þises geares Willelm eorl of Moretoin heonon of
lande into Normandig for.
 1104.18. Ac syððan he afaren wes. he wið þone cyng
geworhte. for hwan hine se cyng ealles benæmde. & belænde þæs
þe he her on lande hæfde.
 1104.21. Nis eaðe to asecgenne þises landes earmða þe hit
to þysan timan dreogende wæs. þurh mistlice & mænigfealdlice
unriht & gyld. þæ næfre ne geswican ne ne ateorodon.
 1104.23. & æfre ealswa se cyng for. full hergung þurh his
hired uppon his wreccea folc wæs. & þær onmang foroft bærneta.
& manslihtas.
 1104.26. Eall þis wæs God mid to gremienne. & þas arme
leode mid to tregienne.
 1105.1. On þisum geare to Natiuiteð heold se cyng Heanrig his
hired æt Windlesoran.
 1105.2. & þæræfter to þam lengtene he for ofer sæ
into Normandig uppon his broðer Rotbert eorl.
 1105.3. & onmang þam þe he þær wunode he gewann of his
broðer Caþum & Baius. & mæst ealle þa castelas & þa
heafodmen þær on lande him wurdon underþeodde. & se syððan to
herfest eft ongean hider to lande com.
 1105.7. & þæt he on Normandig gewunnen hæfde.
syððan on sibbe & him gebygle wunode. butan þa þe þam eorle
Willelme of Mortoin ahwær neah wunedon. þa he gelomlice geswæncte swa
he swiðost mihte. for his landlyre her on lande.
 1105.11. And þa toforan Cristes mæssan com Rotbert de
Bælesme hider to lande to þam cynge.
 1105.13. Ðis wæs swiðe gedyrfsum gear her on lande þurh
wæstma forwordenessa. & þurh þa mænigfealde gyld þe næfre ne
geswican ær se cyng oferfore. & þa hwile þe he þær wæs.
& eft syððan he ongean com.
 1106.1. Her on þison geare wæs se cyng Henrig to Natiuiteð
on Westmynstre. & þær his hired heold.
 1106.2. & uppon þære tide Rotbert de Bælesme mid
unsehte fram þam cynge ut of þison lande into Normandige for.
 1106.5. Ða her æfter onforan længtene wæs se cyng æt
Norðhamtune. & se eorl Rotbert his broðer of Normandig þyder to him
com.
 1106.7. & forþam se cyng him nolde agifan þæt þe he on
Normandige uppon him genumen hæfde. hi mid unsehte tohwurfon. & se eorl
ferde ofer se sona eft ongean.
 1106.10. On þære forman længten wucan on þone Frigedæg
<foreign>i xiiii kalendæ Marcii</foreign> on æfen ætywde an ungewunelic steorra. &
lange stunde þæræfter wæs ælce æfen gesewen hwile scinende.
 1106.12. Se steorra ætywde innon þæt suðwest. he wæs
litel geþuht. and deorc. ac se leoma þe him fram stod wæs swiðe
beorht. & swilce ormæte beam geþuht norðeast scinende.
 1106.15. & sumne æfen wæs gesæwen swilce se beam
ongeanweardes wið þes steorran ward fyrcliende wære.
 1106.17. Gehwylce sædon þæt hig ma on þison timon
uncuðra steorra gesawon. ac we hit openlicor ne awriton. forþam þe we hit
sylfe ne sawon.
 1106.19. On þa niht þe on morgen wæs <foreign>Cena Domini</foreign>. þæt
is se þunresdæg toforan Eastran. wæron gesewen twegen monan on
þære heofonan toforan þam dæge oðer beeastan. & se oðer be
westan begen fulle. & þæs ylcan dæges wæs se mona <foreign>xiiii</foreign>.
 1106.23. To Eastran wæs se cyng æt Baðan. & to
Pentecosten æt Searbyrig. forþam þe he nolde on his fundunge ofer sæ
hired healdan.
 1106.25. Ðær æfter toforan August ferde se cyng ofer sæ
into Normandig. & ealle mæst þe þær on lande wæron him on his
willan to gebugon. wiðuton Rotbert de Bælesme. & þam eorle of
Moretoin. & feawa oðre of þam heafodmannan þe mid þam eorle of
Normandige þe gyt heoldan.
 1106.29. & forþan se cyng syððan mid fyrde for. &
besæt þæs eorles ænne castel of Moretoin Tenercebrai hatte.
 1106.31. Onmang þam þe se cyng þone castel besæt. com se
eorl Rotbert of Normandig on sancte Michaeles mæsseæfen uppon þone cyng
mid his fyrde. & mid him Rotbert de Bælesme. & Willelm eorl of
Moretoin. & ealle þa þe mid heom woldan.
 1106.34. Ac seo streongðe & se sige wearð þæs cynges.
 1106.35. Ðær wearð se eorl of Normandig gefangen. & se

gesende. & on hæftneðe gebrohte.
 1106.38. Rotbert de Bælesme þær wearð aflymed. &

 1106.39. Eadgar æþeling þe litle ær fram þam cynge to

syððan sacleas faran.
 1106.41. Syððan geeode se cyng eall þæt on Normandige

þæs þe Francan þyses landes weoldan.

 1110.10. & swa þurhwunode fullneah oð dæg. &

 1110.13. Ealle þa niht wæs seo lyft swiðe clene. & þa

wurdon þære nihte þurh forste swiðe fornumene.
 1110.15. Ðær æfter on Iunies monðe ætywde an steorra
norðaneastan. & his leoma stod toforan him on þet suðwest. &
þus manega niht wæs gesæwen.
 1110.17. & furðor nihtes syððan he ufor astah. he wæs

 1110.20. Ðises geares wurdon belænde Philippus de Brause.

 1110.23. & æfter his forsiðe feng to se eorl of Angeow.
& hi togeanes þam cynge heold.
 1110.25. Ðis wæs swiðe gedeorfsum gear her on lande þurh

hwan eorðwestmas wurdon swiðe amyrde. & treowwestmas ofer eall þis
land forneah eall forwurdon.

 1114.20. On þæs ylcan tyme feorde se cyng toweard þone sæ

 1114.26. & he lange wiðstod. ac hit ne forheol naht.
 1114.27. & se cyng þa bebead þone arcebiscop þæt he

 1114.33. God ælmihtig wunie æfre mid him.
