 1122.3. & on þone lententyde þær toforen forbearn se
burch on Gleaweceastre.
 1122.4. Þa hwile þe þa munecas sungen þære messe. &
se dæcne hafde ongunnan þone godspel <foreign>Preteriens Ihesu</foreign>. þa com se fir
on ufenweard þone stepel. & forbearnde ealle þe minstre. & ealle
þa gersumes þe þær binnen wæron for uton feawe bec. & <foreign>iii</foreign>
messehakeles. þet wes þes dæies <foreign>viii idus Martii</foreign>.
 1122.9. & þæræfter þe Tywesdæi æfter Palmes
Sunendæi wæs swiðe micel wind on þæt dæi <foreign>xi kalendæ
Aprilis</foreign>.
 1122.10. Þæræfter comen feale tacne widehwear on Englaland
& feole dwild wearen geseogen & geheord.
 1122.12. & þes niht <foreign>viii kalendæ Augusti</foreign> wæs swiðe
micel eorðdyne ofer eal Sumersetescire & on Gleawecestrescire.
 1122.13. Siððon on þæs dæi <foreign>vi idus Septembris</foreign> þet
wæs on sancte Marie messedæi. þa wearð swiðe mycel wind fram
þa undern dæies to þa swarte nihte.
 1122.16. Þeos ilce geares forðferde Raulf seo ærcebiscop of
Cantwarbyrig. þæt wæs on þæs dæies <foreign>xiii kalendæ
Nouembris</foreign>.
 1122.17. Þæræfter wæron feole scipmen on sæ. & on
wæter. & saedon þæt hi sægon on norðeast fir micel & brad
wið þone eorðe. & weax on lengþe up on an to þam wolcne.
 1122.20. & se wolcne undide on fower healfe and faht þær
togeanes. swilc hit scolde acwencen. & se fir weax na þa ma up to þe
heouene.
 1122.22. Þæt fir hi seagon in ðe dæirime and læste swa
lange þæt hit wæs liht ofer eall. þet wæs þæs dæies <foreign>vii
IDVS Decembris</foreign>.
 1123.1. On þyssum geare wæs se king Henri on Cristes tyde
æt Dunestaple. & þær comen þes eorles sandermen of Angeow to
him.
 1123.3. & þeonen he ferde to Wudestoke. & his biscopes
& his hird eal mid him.
 1123.4. Þa tidde hit on an Wodnesdei. þet wæs on <foreign>iiii idus
Ianuarii</foreign>. þet se king rad in his derfald and se biscop Roger of Seresbyrig
on an half him. and se biscop Rotbert Bloet of Lincolne on oðer half him.
& riden þær sprecende.
 1123.7. Þa aseh dune se biscop of Lincolne & seide to þam
kyng. laferd kyng ic swelte.
 1123.9. & se kyng alihte dune of his hors & alehte hine
betwux his earmes. & let hine beran ham to his inne. & wearð þa
sone dead.
 1123.11. & man ferode hine to Lincolne mid micel wurðscipe.
& bebyrigde hine toforen sancte Marie wefod.
 1123.12. & hine bebyrigde se biscop of Ceastre Rotbert Pecceð
wæs gehaten.
 1123.14. Ða sone þæræfter sende se kyng hise write ofer
eall Englalande. & bed hise biscopes & hise abbates & hise
þeignes ealle þet hi scolden cumen to his gewitenemot on Candelmesse deig
to Gleawceastre him togeanes. & hi swa diden.
 1123.17. Ða hi wæran þær gegaderod. þa bed se cyng heom
þæt hi scoldon cesen hem ærcebiscop to Cantwarabyrig swa hwam swa swa
hi woldon. & he hem hit wolde tyþian.
 1123.20. Ða spræcon ða biscopas hem betwenan. and sæden
þæt hi næfre mare ne wolden hafen munechades man to ercebiscop ofer
hem.
 1123.22. Ac iedon ealle samodlice to þone kyng and ieornden
þæt hi mosten cesen of clerchades man swa hwam swa swa hi wolden to
ercebiscop. & se kyng hit hem tidde.
 1123.25. Ðis wæs eall ear gedon ðurh se biscop of
Seresbyrig. & þurh se biscop of Lincolne ær he wære dead. forði
þet næfre ne luueden hi munece regol. ac wæron æfre togænes
muneces & here regol.
 1123.28. And se prior & se munecas of Cantwarabyrig. &
ealle þa oðre þe ðær wæron munechades men hit wiðcwæðen
fulle twa dagas.
 1123.30. Ac hit naht ne beheld. for se biscop of Særesbyrig
wæs strang & wealde eall Engleland. & wæs þær togeanes eall
þæt he mihte & cuðe.
 1123.32. Ða cusen hi an clerc Willelm of Curboil wæs gehaten.
he was canonie of an mynstre Cicc hatte. & brohten him toforen se kyng.
 1123.35. & se kyng him geaf ðone ærcebiscoprice. &
ealle þa biscopas him underfengen.
 1123.36. Him wiðcwæðen muneces & eorles & þeignes
ealle mest þe þær wæron.
 1123.38. On þa ilca tyma ferden þes eorles sandermen mid
unsæhte fram kyng. na of his gyfe naht ne rohton.
 1123.40. On þa ilca tyma com an Legat of Rome Henri wæs
gehaten. he wæs abbot of Sancti Johannis mynstre of Anieli.
 1123.41. & he com æfter þe Rome scot. & he sæde
þone cyng þæt hit wæs togeanes riht þæt man scolde setten clerc
ofer muneces. & swa swa hi hæfden cosen ærcebiscop æror in here
capitele æfter rihte.
 1123.44. Ac se cyng hit nolde undon. for þes biscop luuen of
Særesbyrig.
 1123.45. Ða ferde se ærcebiscop sone þæræfter to
Cantwarabyrig & wæs þær underfangan þæh hit wære here
unþancas. & was þære sone gebletsod to biscop fram se biscop of
Lundene. & se biscop Ernulf of Roueceastre. & se biscop Willelm Gifard
of Winceastre. & se biscop Bernard of Wales. & se biscop Roger of
Searesbyrig.
 1123.50. Ða sone in þe lenten ferde se ærcebiscop to Rome
æfter his pallium.
 1123.51. & mid him ferde se biscop Bernard of Wales. &
Sefred abbot of Gleastingbyrig. & Anselm abbot os Sancti Ædmund. &
Iohan ærcedæcne of Cantwarabyrig. & Gifard wæs þes kinges
hirdclerc.
 1123.55. On þa ilca tima ferde se ærcebiscop ðurstan of
Eoferwic to Rome þurh þes papes hese.
 1123.56. & com þider ðre dagas ær se ærcebiscop of
Cantwarabyrig come. & wæs þære underfangan mid micel wurðscipe.
 1123.58. Ða com se ærcebiscop of Cantwarabyrig & wæs
ðære fulle seoueniht ær hi mihte cumen to þes papes spræce.
 1123.59. Þæt wæs forþan þæt hit wæs don ðone
pape to understanden þæt he hæfde underfangen ðone ærcebiscoprice
togeanes þa muneces of þe mynstre & togeanes rihte.
 1123.61. Ac þæt ofercom Rome þet ofercumeð eall weoruld
þæt is gold & seolure. & se pape sweðolode & gaf him his
pallium.
 1123.63. & se ærcebiscop swor him underþeodnysse of ealle
ða þing þæt se papa him on leide on Sancti Petres heuod and Sancti
Paules. & sende him ham ða mid his bletsunge.
 1123.67. Ða hwile þæt se ærcebiscop wæs ut of lande.
geaf se kyng ðone biscoprice of Baðe þes cwenes canceler Godefreið
wæs gehaten. he wæs boren of Luuein. þæt wæs þes dæiges
Annuntiatio Sancte Marie at Wudestoke.
 1123.70. Ða sone þæræfter ferde se king to Winceastre
& wæs ealle Eastrentyde þære.
 1123.71. & þa hwile þæt he þær wæs þa geaf he
þone biscoprice of Lincolne an clerc Alexander wæs gehaten. he wæs
þes biscopes nefe of Searesbyrig.
 1123.72. Þis he dyde eall for þes biscopes luuen.
 1123.75. Ða ferde se kyng þenen to Portesmuðe. & læi
þære eall ofer Pentecostewuce.
 1123.76. Þa sone swa he hæfde wind swa ferde he ofer into
Normandie. & betæhte þa eall Engleland to geamene & to wealden
þone biscop Roger of Searesbyrig.
 1123.78. Ða wæs se kyng eall þes geares in Normandie. &
weax þa micel unfrið betwux him & hise þeignas. swa þæt se eorl
Walaram of Mellant. & Hamalri. & Hugo of Mundford. & Willelm of
Romare. and fela oðre wendan fram him & helden here castles him
togeanes.
 1123.82. & se kyng held stranglice hem togeanes. & þes
ylces geares he wan of Walaram his castel Punt Aldemer. & of Hugo Mundford.
& siððen he spedde æfre leong þe bet.
 1123.86. Ðes ylce geares ær se biscop of Lincolne com to his
biscoprice forbearn eall meast se burh of Lincolne. & micel ungerime folces
wæpmen & wimmen forburnen.
 1123.88. & swa mycel hearm þær wæs gedon swa nan man
hit cuðe oþer secgen. þet wæs þes dæges <foreign>xiiii kalendæ
Iunii</foreign>.
 1124.1. Eall þis gear wes se king Heanri on Normandi. þæt
wes for se miccle unfrið þæt he heafde wið se king Loðewis of
France. & wið se eorl of Angeow. & wið his agene men alre mest.
 1124.4. Þa gelamp hit on þes dæges Annuntiatio sancte
Marie þæt se eorl Waleram of Mellant ferde fram his an castel Belmunt het
to his an oðer castel Watteuile.
 1124.6. Mid him ferde þes kinges stiward of France Amalri. &
Hugo Gerueises sunu. & Hugo of Munford. & fela oðre godre cnihte.
 1124.8. Þa comen hem togeanes þes kinges cnihtes of ealla þa
casteles ða þær abuton wæron & fuhton wið hem & aflemden
hem & namen þone eorl Waleram & Hugo Gerueises sunu. & Hugo of
Mundford. & fif & twenti oðre cnihtes & brohton hem to þone
kinge.
 1124.12. & se king let don þone eorl Waleram & Hugo
Gerueises sunu on heftnunge on ðone castel on Roðem.
 1124.14. & Hugo of Mundford he sende to Engleland. & let
hine don on ifele bendas on þone castel on Gleucestre.
 1124.15. & of þa oðre swa fela swa him þuhte he sende
norð & suð to hise casteles on heftnunge.
 1124.17. Ða siððon ferde se king & wan ealle þes eorles
castelas Waleram þa wæron on Normandi. & ealla þa oðre þa his
wiðrewines healden him togeanes.
 1124.20. Eall was þes unfrið for þes eorles sunu Rotbert of
Normandi Willelm het.
 1124.21. Se ilce Willelm hefde numen Fulkes eorles gingre dohter to
wife of Angeow.
 1124.22. & forði se king of France & ealle þas eorles
heolden mid him & ealle þa rice men. & sæidon þet se king heold
his broðer Rotbert mid wrange on heftnunge. & his sunu Willelm mid
unrihte aflemde ut of Normandi.
 1124.26. Ðes ilces geares wæron fæla untime on Englelande.
on corne & on ealle westme. swa þæt betweonen Cristesmesse &
Candelmesse man sælde þæt acersæd hwæte þæt is twegen
sedlæpas to six scillingas. & þæt bærlic þæt is þre
sedlæpas to six scillingas. & þæt acersæd aten þæt is
feower sedlæpas to feower scillingas.
 1124.30. Þet wæs forþi þæt corn wæs litel. & se
penig wæs swa ifel þæt se man þa hæfde at an market an pund he ne
mihte cysten þærof for nan þing twelfe penegas.
 1124.34. On þes ilces geares forðferde se eadig biscop Ernulf
of Roueceastre se æror wæs abbot on Burch. þet wæs þes dæies
<foreign>Idus Martii</foreign>.
 1124.36. & þæræfter forðferde se king Alexander of
Scotlande on þes dæies <foreign>ix kalendæ Mai</foreign>.
 1124.37. & Dauid his broðer þa wæs eorl on
Norðhamtunescire feng to rice and hæfde ða baðe togedere þone
kinerice on Scotlande. & þone eorldom on Englelande.
 1124.40. & On þæs dæies <foreign>xix kalendæ Ianuarii</foreign>
forðferde se pape on Rome Calistus wæs gehaten. & Honorius feng to
papedom.
 1124.42. Ðes ilces geares æfter sancti Andreas messe toforen
Cristes messe held Raulf Basset & þes kinges ðæines gewitenemot on
Leþecæstrescire at Hundehoge. & ahengen þær swa fela þefas swa
næfre ær ne wæron. þet wæron on þa litle hwile ealles feower
& feowerti manne, & six men spilde of here ægon & of here
stanes.
 1124.48. Fela soðfeste men sæidon þæt þær wæron
manege mid micel unrihte gespilde.
 1124.49. Oc ure Laford God ælmihtig þa eall digelnesse seð
& wat, he seoð þæt man læt þæt ærme folc mid ealle
unrihte. ærost man hem beræfoð her eahte and siþðon man hem
ofslæð.
 1124.52. Ful heui gær wæs hit se man þe æni god heafde.
him me hit beræfode mid strange geoldes & mid strange motes. þe nan ne
heafde stærf of hungor.
 1125.1. On þis gær sende se king Henri toforen Cristes messe
of Normandi to Englalande & bebead þet man scolde beniman ealle þa
minitere þe wæron on Englelande heora liman. þæt wæs here elces
riht hand & heora stanen beneðan.
 1125.4. Þæt wæs for se man ðe hafde an pund he ne mihte
cysten ænne peni at anne market.
 1125.6. & se biscop Roger of Særesbyrig sende ofer eall
Englalande & bebead hi ealle þæt hi scolden cumen to Winceastre to
Cristes messe.
 1125.8. Þa hi ðider coman ða nam man an & an & benam
ælc ðone riht hand & þa stanes beneðan.
 1125.9. Eall þis wæs gedon wið innon þa twelfniht. &
þæt wæs eall mid micel rihte forði þæt hi hafden fordon eall
þæt land mid here micele fals. þæt hi ealle abohton.
 1125.12. On þes ilces gæres sende se papa of Rome to ðise
lande an cardinal Iohan of Creme wæs gehaten.
 1125.13. He com first to þone king on Normandi. & se king
hine underfeng mid micel wurðscipe.
 1125.15. Beteahte hine siððon þone ærcebiscop Willelme of
Cantwarabyrig . & he hine ledde to Cantwarabyrig. & he wæs þær
underfangen mid micel wurðscipe & mid micel processionem.
 1125.17. & he sang ðone hehmesse on Eastren dæi æt
Cristes wefod.
 1125.18. & siððon he ferde ofer eall Englalande to ealle
þa biscoprices & abbotrices þa wæron on þis lande.
 1125.20. & ofer eall he wæs underfangen mid wurðscipe
& ealle hine iæfen micele gife & mære.
 1125.21. & siððon he heold his concilie on Lundene fulle
þreo dagas on natiuitas sancte Marie on Septembris mid ærcebiscopes
& mid leodbiscopas & abbotes & læred & lawed. bead þær
þa ilce lagas þa ANSELM ærcebiscop hæfde æror beboden & feala
ma þeah hit litel forstode.
 1125.25. & þeonon he for ofer sæ sone æfter sancte
Michaeles messe & swa to Rome. & se ærcebiscop Willelm of
Cantwarabyrig. & se ærcebiscop Turstein of Eferwic. & se biscop
Alexander of Lincolne. & se biscop of Loþene Iohan. & se abbot of
sancte Alban Gosfreið & wæran þær underfangen of þone pape
Honorius mid micel wurðscipe. & wæron þære eall þone wintre.
 1125.32. On ðes ilces geares wearð swa micel flod on sancte
Laurenties messedæig þæt feola tunes & men weorðan adrencte.
& brigges tobrokene. & corn & mædwe spilt mid ealle. &
hunger & cwealm on men & on erue. & on ealle westme swa micel
untime wearð swa hit ne wæs feola gear ær.
 1125.37. & þes ilces geares forðferde se abbot Iohan of
Burch on <foreign>ii IDus Octobris</foreign>.
 1126.1. Eall þis geare wæs se kyng Heanri on Normandi eall to
æfter heruest.
 1126.2. Þa com he to þis lande betwyx natiuitas sancte Marie
& Michaeles messe.
 1126.3. Mid him com se cwen & his dohter þæt he æror
hafde giuen þone kasere Heanri of Loherenge to wife.
 1126.5. & he brohte mid him þone eorl Waleram & Hugo
Gerueises sunu.
 1126.6. & þone eorl he sende to Brigge on heftnunge. &
þeonon he sende him to Walingeforde siððon. & Hugo to Windlesofra.
& let hine don on harde bande.
 1126.9. & þa æfter Michaeles messe com se Scotte kyng
Dauid of Scotlande hider to lande.
 1126.10. & se kyng Heanri underfeng hine mid micel
wurðscipe.
 1126.11. & he wunode þa eall þet gear on þis lande.
 1126.13. On þes ilces geares let se kyning nimen his broðer
Rotbert fram þone biscop Roger of Særesbyri. & betahte hine his sune
Rotbert eorl of Gleucæstre. & let hine læden to Bricstowe &
þær diden on þone castel.
 1126.16. Þæt wæs eall don ðurh his dohtres ræd. &
þurh se Scotte kyng DAUID hire eam.
 1127.1. Ðis gear heald se kyng Heanri his hird æt Cristes
mæsse on Windlesoure.
 1127.2. Þær wæs se Scotte kyng Dauid. & eall ða
heaued læred & læuued þæt wæs on Engleland.
 1127.3. & þær he let sweren ercebiscopes & biscopes
& abbotes & eorles & ealle þa ðeines ða þær wæron his
dohter Æðelic Englaland & Normandi to hande æfter his dæi. þe
ær wæs þes Caseres wif of Sexlande.
 1127.7. & sende hire siððen to Normandi. & mid hire
ferde hire broðer Rotbert eorl of Gleucestre. & BRIAN þes eorles sunu
Alein Fergan. & leot hire beweddan þes eorles sunu of Angeow Gosfreið
Martæl wæs gehaten.
 1127.10. Hit ofþuhte naþema ealle Frencisc & Englisc. oc se
kyng hit dide for to hauene sibbe of se eorl of Angeow. & for helpe to
hauene togænes his neue Willelm.
 1127.14. Ðes ilces gæres on þone lententide wæs se eorl
Karle of Flandres ofslagen on ane circe þær he læi & bæd hine to
Gode to for þone weofede amang þane messe fram his agene manne.
 1127.17. & se kyng of France brohte þone eorles sunu Willelm
of Normandi & iæf hine þone eorldom. & þet landfolc him
wiðtoc.
 1127.19. Þes ilce Willelm hæfde æror numen ðes eorles
dohter of Angeow to wife oc hi wæron siððen totweamde for sibreden.
þet wes eall ðurh þone kyng Heanri of Engleland.
 1127.21. Siððen þa nam he þes kynges wifes swuster of
France to wife. & forþi iæf se kyng him þone eorldom of Flandres.
 1127.24. Ðes ilce gæres he gæf þone abbotrice of Burch an
abbot Heanri wæs gehaten of Peitowe. se hæfde his abbotrice Sancti
Johannis of Angeli on hande.
 1127.26. & ealle þa ærcebiscopes & biscopes seidon
þæt hit wæs togeanes riht. & þæt he ne mihte hafen twa
abbotrices on hande.
 1127.28. Oc se ilce Heanri dide þone king to understandene
þæt he hæfde læten his abbotrice for þæt micele unsibbe
þæt wæs on þæt land. & þæt he dide ðurh þes papes
ræd & leue of Rome. & ðurh þes abbotes of Clunni. & þurh
þæt he wæs legat of ðone Rome scott.
 1127.32. Oc hit ne wæs naðema eallswa. oc he wolde hauen
baðe on hand. & swa hafde swa lange swa Godes wille wæs.
 1127.33. He wæs on his clærchade biscop on Scesscuns.
siððan warð he munec on Clunni. & siððon prior on þone seolue
minstre. & siððon he wærð prior on Sauenni.
 1127.36. Þaræftor þurh þæt he wæs ðes kynges
mæi of Engleland & þes eorles of Peitowe þa geaf se eorl him þone
abbotrice of Sancti Johannis minstre of Angeli.
 1127.38. Siððon þurh his micele wrences ða beiæt he
þone ærcebiscoprice of Besencun & hæfde hit þa on hande þre
dagas. þa forlæs he þæt mid rihte forþi þæt he hit hæfde
æror beieten mid unrihte.
 1127.41. Siððon þa beiet he þone biscoprice of Seintes
þæt wæs fif mile fram his abbotrice þæt he hæfde fulneah
seoueniht on hande. þenon brohte se abbot him of Clunni swa swa he æror
dide of Besencun.
 1127.44. Þa beþohte he him þæt gif he mihte ben rotfest on
Engleland þæt he mihte habben eal his wille.
 1127.46. Besohte þa ðone kyng & sæide him þæt he
wæs eald man & forbroken man, & þæt he ne mihte ðolen þa
micele unrihte & þa micele unsibbe ða wæron on here land.
 1127.48. & iærnde þa þurh him & ðurh ealle his
freond namcuðlice þone abbotrice of Burhc, & se kyng hit him iætte
forði þæt he wæs his mæi. & forþi þæt he wæs an
hæfod ða að to swerene & witnesse to berene þær ða eorles
sunu of Normandi & þes eorles dohter of Angeow wæron totwemde for
sibreden.
 1127.53. Þus earmlice wæs þone abbotrice gifen betwix
Cristesmesse & Candelmesse at Lundene.
 1127.55. & swa he ferde mid þe cyng to Wincestre &
þanon he com to Burch. & þær he wunede eall riht swa drane doð on
hiue.
 1127.57. Eall þæt þa beon dragen toward swa frett þa drane
& dragað fraward.
 1127.58. Swa dide he eall þæt he mihte tacen wiðinnen &

þær ne dide. ne na god ðær ne læuede.
 1127.60. Ne þince man na sellice þæt we soð seggen for hit
wæs ful cuð ofer eall land þæt swa radlice swa he þær com
þæt wæs þes Sunendæies þæt man singað <foreign>EXURGE QUARE O. D</foreign>.
þa son þær æfter þa sægon & herdon fela men feole huntes

 1127.64. Ða huntes wæron swarte & micele & ladlice.
& here hundes ealle swarte & bradegede & ladlice. & hi ridone
on swarte hors & on swarte bucces.
 1127.66. Þis wæs segon on þe selue derfald in þa tune on

Stanforde. & þa muneces herdon ða horn blawen þæt hi blewen on
nihtes.
 1127.69. Soðfestemen heom kepten on nihtes. sæidon þes þe
heom þuhte þæt þær mihte wel ben abuton twenti oðer þritti
hornblaweres.

 1127.72. Þis was his ingang. of his utgang ne cunne we iett noht
seggon.

 1137.1. Ðis gære for þe king Stephne ofer sæ to Normandi
& ther wes underfangen forþi ðæt hi uuenden ðæt he sculde ben
alsuic alse the eom wes. & for he hadde get his tresor. ac he todeld it
& scatered sotlice.
 1137.4. Micel hadde Henri king gadered gold & syluer. & na
god ne dide me for his saule thar of.
 1137.6. Þa þe king Stephne to Englalande com þa macod he his
gadering æt Oxeneford.
 1137.7. & þar he nam þe biscop Roger of Sereberi &
Alexander biscop of Lincol & te Canceler Roger hise neues. & dide
ælle in prisun. til hi iafen up here castles.
 1137.9. Þa the suikes undergæton ðæt he milde man was
& softe & god. & na iustise ne dide. þa diden hi alle wunder.
 1137.11. Hi hadden him manred maked & athes suoren. ac hi nan
treuthe ne heolden.
 1137.12. Alle he wæron forsworen & here treothes forloren.
for æuric riceman his castles makede & agænes him heolden. &
fylden þe land ful of castles.
 1137.15. Hi suencten suyðe þe uurecce men of þe land mid
castelweorces þa þe castles uuaren maked þa fylden hi mid deoules &
yuele men.
 1137.16. Þa namen hi þa men þe hi wenden ðæt ani god
hefden. bathe be nihtes & be dæies. carlmen & wimmen. & diden
heom in prisun efter gold & syluer. & pined heom. untellendlice pining.
for ne uuæren næure nan martyrs swa pined alse hi wæron.
 1137.21. Me henged up bi the fet & smoked heom. mid ful smoke.
 1137.22. Me henged bi the þumbes. other bi the hefed. &
hengen bryniges on her fet.
 1137.24. Me dide cnotted strenges abuton here hæued. &
uurythen to ðæt it gæde to þe hærnes.
 1137.25. Hi dyden heom in quarterne þar nadres & snakes &
pades wæron inne. & drapen heom swa.
 1137.27. Sume hi diden in crucethus ðæt is in an cæste
þat was scort & nareu. & un dep. & dide scærpe stanes
þerinne. & þrengde þe man þærinne. ðæt him bræcon alle
þe limes.
 1137.29. In mani of þe castles wæron lof & grin. ðæt
wæron rachenteges ðæt twa oþer thre men hadden onoh to bæron
onne.
 1137.31. Þat was sua maced. ðæt is fæstned to an beom.
& diden an scærp iren abuton þa mannes throte & his hals. ðæt
he ne myhte nowiderwardes. ne sitten ne lien ne slepen. oc bæron al ðæt
iren.
 1137.34. Mani þusen hi drapen mid hungær.
 1137.36. I ne can ne i ne mai tellen alle þe wunder ne alle þe
pines ðæt hi diden wreccemen on þis land. & ðæt lastede þa
<foreign>xix</foreign> wintre wile Stephne was king & æure it was uuerse & uuerse.
 1137.39. Hi læiden gæildes on the tunes æure um wile &
clepeden it tenserie.
 1137.40. Þa þe uurecce men ne hadden nan more to gyuen. þa
ræueden hi & brendon alle the tunes. ðæt wel þu myhtes faren all
adæis fare sculdest thu neure finden man in tune sittende. ne land tiled.
 1137.43. Þa was corn dære. & flec & cæse &
butere. for nan ne wæs o þe land.
 1137.44. Wreccemen sturuen of hungær. sume ieden on ælmes
þe waren sum wile ricemen. sume flugen ut of lande.
 1137.47. Wes næure gæt mare wreccehed on land. ne næure
hethen men werse ne diden þan hi diden.
 1137.48. For ouersithon ne for baren hi nouther circe ne
cyrceiærd. oc namen al þe god ðæt þarinne was. & brenden sythen
þe cyrce & altegædere.
 1137.50. Ne hi ne forbaren biscop land ne abbod ne preostes. ac
ræueden munekes & clerekes. & æuric man other þe ouermyhte.
 1137.52. Gif twa men oþer <foreign>iii</foreign> coman ridend to an tun. al þe
tunscipe flugæn for heom. wenden ðæt hi wæron ræueres.
 1137.54. Þe biscopes & lered men heom cursede æure. oc was
heom naht þar of. for hi uueron al forcursæd & forsuoren &
forloren.
 1137.57. Warsæ me tilede. þe erthe ne bar nan corn. for þe
land was al fordon. mid suilce dædes. & hi sæden openlice ðæt
Crist slep. & his halechen.
 1137.59. Suilc & mare þanne we cunnen sæin. we þolenden
<foreign>xix</foreign> wintre for ure sinnes.

 1137.79. Nu we willen sægen sumdel wat belamp on Stephnes kinges

war.
 1140.4. Þerefter in þe lengten þestrede þe sunne & te
dæi. abuton non tid dæies. þa men eten. ðæt me lihtede candles to
æten bi.
 1140.5. & þat was <foreign>xiii kalendæ Aprilis</foreign>. wæron men
suythe ofwundred.
 1140.7. Þerefter fordfeorde Willelm ærcebiscop of Cantwarberi.
& te king makede Teodbald ærcebiscop þe was abbot in the Bec.
 1140.9. Þerefter wæx suythe micel uuerre betuyx þe king
& Randolf eorl of Cæstre noht forþi ðæt he ne iaf him al ðæt
he cuthe axen him. alse he dide alle othre. oc æfre þe mare he iaf heom.
þe wærse hi wæron him.
 1140.12. Þe eorl heold Lincol agænes þe king. & benam
him al ðæt he ahte to hauen.
 1140.13. & te king for þider. & besætte him & his
brother Willelm de Romare in þe castel.
 1140.14. & te æorl stæl ut & ferde efter Rodbert eorl
of Gloucestre. & brohte him þider mid micel ferd.
 1140.16. & fuhten suythe on Candelmassedæi agenes heore
lauerd. & namen him, for his men him suyken & flugæn. & læd
him to Bristowe & diden þar in prisun. & feteres.
 1140.19. Þa was al Engleland styred mar þan ær wæs. &
al uyel wæs in lande.
 1140.21. Þerefter com þe kynges dohter Henries þe hefde ben
Emperice in Alamanie. & nu wæs cuntesse in Angou.
 1140.22. & com to Lundene & te Lundenissce folc hire wolde
tæcen. & scæ fleh & forles þar micel.
 1140.25. Þerefter þe biscop of Wincestre Henri þe kinges
brother Stephnes spac wid Rodbert eorl & wyd þemperice & suor heom
athas ðæt he neure ma mid te king his brother wolde halden. & cursede
alle þe men þe mid him heoldon.
 1140.28. & sæde heom ðæt he uuolde iiuen heom up
Wincestre. & dide heom cumen þider.
 1140.29. Þa hi þær inne wæren. þa com þe kinges cuen
mid al hire strengthe. & besæt heom. ðæt þer wæs inne micel
hungær.
 1140.31. Þa hi ne leng ne muhten þolen þa stali hi ut &
flugen. & hi wurthen war widuten & folecheden heom.
 1140.33. & namen Rodbert eorl of Gloucestre. & ledden him
to Rouecestre. & diden him þare in prisun. & te emperice fleh into an
minstre.
 1140.35. Þa feorden þe wise men betwyx þe kinges freond &
te eorles freond. & sahtlede sua ðæt me sculde leten ut þe king of
prisun for þe eorl. & te eorl for þe king. & sua diden.
 1140.39. Sithen þerefter sahtleden þe king & Randolf eorl
at Stanford. & athes suoren & treuthes fæston ðæt her nouþer
sculde besuiken other.
 1140.41. & it ne forstod naht. for þe king him sithen nam in
Hamtun. þurhc wicci ræd. & dide him in prisun.
 1140.42. & efsones he let him ut þurhc wærse red. to
ðæt forewarde ðæt he suor on halidom & gysles fand. þat he alle
his castles sculde iiuen up.
 1140.44. Sume he iaf up, & sume ne iaf he noht. & dide
þanne wærse þanne he hær sculde.
 1140.47. Þa was Engleland suythe todeled. sume helden mid te
king. & sume mid þemperice.
 1140.48. For þa þe king was in prisun þa wenden þe eorles
& te rice men þat he neure mare sculde cumen ut. & sæhtleden wyd
þemperice. & brohten hire into Oxenford.
 1140.50. & iauen hire þe burch.
 1140.51. Þa þe king was ute þa herde ðæt sægen. &
toc his feord & besæt hire in þe tur.
 1140.52. & me læt hire dun on niht of þe tur mid rapes.
& stal ut. & scæ fleh & iæde on fote to Walingford.
 1140.55. Þærefter scæ ferde ouer sæ.
 1140.55. & hi of Normandi wenden alle fra þe king. to þe
eorl of Angæu. sume here þankes & sume here unþankes. for he
besæt heom til hi aiauen up here castles. & hi nan helpe ne hæfden of
þe kinge.
 1140.59. Þa ferde Eustace þe kinges sune to France & nam
þe kinges suster of France to wife.
 1140.60. Wende to bigæton Normandi þær þurh. oc he spedde
litel. & be gode rihte for he was an yuel man.
 1140.62. For ware se he com he dide mare yuel þanne god. he
reuede þe landes & læide micele gildes on.
 1140.63. He brohte his wif to Engleland. & dide hire in þe
castel/ on Canteberi.
 1140.65. God wimman scæ wæs. oc scæ hedde litel blisse mid
him.
 1140.66. & Crist ne wolde ðæt he sculde lange rixan. &
wærd ded & his moder beien.
 1140.68. & te eorl of Angæu wærd ded. & his sune
Henri toc to þe rice.
 1140.69. & te cuen of France todælde fra þe king. &
scæ com to þe iunge eorl Henre. & he toc hire to wiue. & al
Peitou mid hire.
 1140.70. Þa ferde he mid micel færd into Engleland. & wan
castles.
 1140.71. & te king ferde agenes him mid micel mare ferd. &
þoþwæthere fuhtten hi noht. oc ferden þe ærcebiscop & te wise
men betwux heom. & makede ðæt sahte ðæt te king sculde ben lauerd
& king wile he liuede. & æfter his dæi ware Henri king. & he
helde him for fader & he him for sune. & sib & sæhte sculde ben
betwyx heom. & on al Engleland.
 1140.77. Þis & te othre foruuardes þet hi makeden. suoren
to halden þe king & te eorl & te biscop & te eorles & rice
men alle.
 1140.79. Þa was þe eorl underfangen æt Wincestre & æt
Lundene mid micel wurtscipe.
 1140.80. & alle diden him manred. & suoren þe pais to
halden.
 1140.81. & hit ward sone suythe god pais. sua ðæt neure
was here.
 1140.82. Þa was þe king strengere þanne he æuert her was.
& te eorl ferde ouer sæ. & al folc him luuede for he dide god
iustise & makede pais.
 1154.1. On þis gær wærd þe king Stephne ded &
bebyried þer. his wif & his sune wæron bebyried æt Fauresfeld.
þæt minster hi makeden.
 1154.3. Þa þe king was ded. þa was þe eorl beionde sæ.
& ne durste nan man don oþer bute god for þe micel eie of him.
 1154.5. Þa he to Engleland com. þa was he underfangen mid micel
wurtscipe. & to king bletcæd in Lundene on þe sunnen dæi beforen
midwinter dæi. & held þær micel curt.
 1154.9. Þat ilce dæi þat Martin abbod of Burch sculde
þider faren. þa sæclede he & ward ded <foreign>iiii Nonæ Ianuarii</foreign>.
 1154.12. & te munekes innen dæis cusen oþer of heom
sælf. Willelm de Walteuile is gehaten. god clerc & god man. & wæl
luued of þe kinge & of alle gode men.
 1154.13. & on cyricen byrieden þabbot hehlice; & sone
þe cosan abbod ferde & te muneces mid him to Oxenforde to þe king
& he iaf him þat abbodrice.
 1154.16. & he ferde him sone to Lincol & was þær
bletcæd/ to abbot ær he ham come.
 1154.17. & sithen was underfangen mid micel wurtscipe at
Burch. mid micel processiun.
 1154.18. & sua he was alsua at Ramesæie. & at Torn.
& at & Spall & at Sancte I. beres.
 1154.19. & nu is abbot. & fair haued begunnon. Cristes
him unne.

RevMon (Cockayne)
B17.11.
Revival of Monasticism: Cockayne 1864-6, III, 432-44.



 1. Geard mid þæm leoman þæs halgan geleafan
mildheortlice wearð gefylled þurh godes gyfe þe on ecnesse libbende eallu
þinc endemes ætgædere geworhte & eal þæt mid gecyndelicum hiwe
on fore sceawudum tidum synderlice to cyþþe & geswutulunge brohte.
 5. & se mæra wyrhta þe rihsigende wylt & gemetegaþ
eal þæt he geworhte no be þæm anum lætan wolde ac eornostlice ofer
þone garsecg þone ylecan leoman þæs fullan geleafan aspringan let
& fornean þæt ytemeste iglond ealles middangeardes mid ongolcynne
genihtsumlice gefylled wundorfullice anlyhte & mærsode.
 11. Soðlice þæt ylece iglond on ærum tydum mid
hæþengilde/ afylled, þearle swiþe beswicyn deofolgilde þeowude.
 13. Þeah hwæþewe þurh fultum þære þancweorþan
cristes gyfe & þurh sanctum gregorium þæs romaniscan setles bisceop
fram þæm þystrum heora geleafleaste wearþ genered.
 16. Mid gewisse se foresæda bisceop þurh myndgunge þære
halgan godes gyfe angan æt suman cyrre to befrinenne sume inlendisce ymbe
þæs iglondes gewunan & hwæþer hi cristene wæron.
 20. He wearð æfter þysse æscan swa swiþe mid þære
blæsan soþere lufe ontend þæt he swa wuldorfulle & gode swa
welweorþe leode geneosian & gefaran wolde & mid lare & gebysnunge
þæs soþan geleafan & mid þweale þæs halgan fulluhtes þurh
hine sylfne geclænsian wolde.
 25. Him forebod com fram eallum romanum þæt he þæt fær
beginnan moste ne him swa gecweme & swa licwyrþe folc gefaran.
 27. He þeah sanctum agustinum, þæt getreowuste bearn
þæs halgan geleafan, him to gespelian funde & hine hider asende
þæt he swa þæslic folc & him swa gecweme ælmihtegum drihtne
geornfullice gestrynde & embe þa gestreon swiþe gecneord wære.
 32. He georne þone his gespelian þurh ærendracan manode
& lærde þæt he georne mynstra timbryde criste to lofe &
weorþunge & þæm godes þeowum þone ylecan þeaw tæhte &
gesette þe þa apostolas mid heora geferrædene on þæm anginne ures
cristendomes heoldon.
 37. Him eallum wæs an heorte & an saul, ne heora nan
syndrige æhta næfde ne þæt furþum ne gecwæþ þæt he
ænige hæfde ac ealle þing heom gemæne wæron.
 40. Þæs sylfa þeaw for þy lange þurh myndgunge þæs
halgan weres on angelcynnes mynsterum forþweard wæs & wel þeonde.
 42. Ac.
 43. Understod & wiste getreowne dyhtnere his halegra cyricena
ær he gewurþe mannum geswutolod.
 44. He him forþy mænigfealde & genihtsume æhta &
mihta gesealde.
 46. Ne he lange ne elcode ne mihta ne ofteah.
 46. Næs lang to þy þæt his broþor þyses lænan
lifes timan geendode.
 48. Se þurh his cildhades nytenesse þis rice to stencte &
his annesse todælde & eac swa halegra cyricena land incuþum reaferum
todælde.
 50. Æfter his forðsiþe eadgar se foresæda cynincg þurh
godes gyfe ealne angelcynnes anweald begeat & þæs rices twislunge eft
to annesse brohte & swa gesundlice ealles weold þæt þa þe on
æran timan lifes wæron & his hyldran gemundon & heora dæda
gefyrn tocneowan þearle swiþe wundredon & wafiende cwædon, hit is,
la, for micel godes wunder þæt þysum cildgeongum cynincge þus
gesundfullice eallu þing underþeodde synt on his cynelicum anwealde.
 59. His foregengan þe geþungene wæron on ylde & on
gleawscype swiþe bescawede & forewittige on ænegum gewinne
earfoþwylde næfre þisne andweald on swa micelre sibbe smyltnesse
gehealdan ne mihton naþor ne mid gefeohte ne mid scette.
 64. Ac nis no to wundrienne swylce hit ungewunlic sy þonne god
ælmihtig mærlice leanaþ æghwylcum þara þe him god behet &
þæt eft fullice gelæst.
 66. Drihten crist is þearle swiþe on þysum þingum mid
ealles modes gledscype to herienne.
 68. Soþlice ælmihtig drihten þe is ealra þinga gewita þe
on ær wat eal þæt toweard is, þe wiste hu fremful he beon wolde him
æfre swiþe milde wæs & ealle god him symle fremfullice towearde
dyde.
 72. Swylce se rihtwisa & se arfæsta leangyfa no mid wordum
ac mid dædum bodede & þus cwæde, Nu þu minne naman and anwald
þæt mine cyricean þe ic rihtlice on minum synderlicum andwealde hæbbe
georne friþast & fyrþrast.
 76. Ic þe to leanes þinne noman mærsige & þin rice
þe þu under minum andwealde hyltst geeacnige & mid gode fyrþrige.
 79. Hwa is monna on angelcynne wuniende þæt nyte hu he godes
rice þæt is godes cyricean ægþær ge mid gastlicum gode ge mid
woroldcundum eallum mæge fyrþrode & friþode?
 82. Witodlice sona swa he to his cynedome gecoren wearþ wæs
swiþe gemundige his behates þe he on his æþelincghade cildgeong gode
behet & sancta marian þa se abbod hine gelaþode to þæm munuclife.
 86. Eal swa we wiþ ufan cwædon þurh þæs gehates
myngunge swiþe geþancol on anginne his rices began þa stowe to
fyrþrienne eal swa he ær behet on his cildgeogoðe & mid eallum
þingum godode to þan swiþe þæt heo næs nane oþor ne waccere
þonne formænig þara þe his yldran ær gefyrþredon on langsumum
fæce.
 92. He þær sona getimbrian het mærlic mynster on þreora
geara fæce.
 93. Þæt wile þincan ungeleaflic eallum þæm þe þa
stowe on uferum tidum geseoð & þis ne gemunaþ.
 95. He þæt ilce mynster þus gehradod het sancta marian
gehalgian gode to lofe & to weorþunge & þær to muneca micele
geferrædene/ gesomnode to þæm þæt hy gode hyrsumedon æfter
tæcinge þæs halgan regules.
 99. Ær þæm lyt muneca wæs on feawum storum on swa
miclum rice þe be rihtum regule lifdon.
 101. Næs þæt na fealdre þonne on are stowe seo is
glæstingabyrig gehaten ðær his fæder eadmund cynincg munecas
ærest gestaþolode.
 104. Of þære stowe wæs se foresprecena abbud genumen &
gehadod to þæm foresædan mynstre þe eadgar cyning gestaþolode &
mid munecum gesette.
 106. He þearle swiþe wearþ gegladod þurh þæt gastlice
munyca angin & geornlice angan to smeagenne ærest þinga hu he his agen
lif gerihtlæcan meahte mid rihtre æfestnesse.
 110. Hit eac swa on bocum awriten is, se þe god beginnan þence
he þæt angin on him sylfum astelle.
 111. Æfter þam þe he sylf geriht wearð began georne
mynstera wide geond his cynerice to rihtlæcynne & godes þeowdom to
arærenne.
 114. Þæt swa wearð gelæst þurh þa fultumigendan godes
gife.
 115. Breac þa gesinlice dunstanes his ercebisceopes rædes,
þurh his myndgunge he wæs smeagende embe his saule hæle & no
þæt an ac eac swylce be ealre æfestnesse & gesundfulnesse his
andwealdes.
 119. Halige stowa he geclænsode fram ealra manna fulnessum no
þæt an on wesseaxna rice ac eac swylce on myrcena lande.
 121. Witodlice he adref þa canonicas þe on þæm
foresædum gyltum ofer de genihtsumedon & on þam fyrmestum stowum
ealles his anwealdes munecas gestaþolode to weorþfulre þenunge
hælendes cristes.
 125. An sumum stowum eac swilce he mynecæna gestaþolode and
þa ælfþryþe his gebeddan betæhte þæt heo æt ælcere
neode hyra gehulpe.
 127. He sylf wæs a smeagende ymb muneca gesundfulnesse & wel
willende hi to þam myngode þæt heo hine geefenlæcende on þa ilcan
wisan ymbe mynecæna hogode.
 130. He began mid geornfulre scrudnunge smeagan & ahsian be
þam gebodum þæs halgan regules & witan wolde þæs sylfan regules
lare þurh þa biþ gegearwod rihtes lifes gewuna & arwyrþe gewilnung
& þa gesetednessa þe to halgum mægenum wæmaþ.
 135. He wolde eac swylce þurh þone regul oncnawan þa wislican
gefadunge þe snotorlice geset is be incuþra ðingra endebyrdnesse.
 137. Þurh þises wisdomes lust he het þisne regul of læden
gereorde on englisc geþeodan.
 139. Þeah þa scearpþanclan witan þe þone twydæledan
wisdom hlutorlice tocnawaþ þæt is andweardra þinga & gastlicra
wisdom & þara ægþer eft on þrim todalum gelyfedlice wunaþ
þisse engliscan geþeodnesse ne behofien.
 143. Is þeah niedbehefe ungelæredum woroldmonnum þy for
helle wites ogan & for cristes lufan þis earmfulle lif forlætaþ
& to hyra drihtne gecyrrað & þone halgan þeowdom þises regules
geceosaþ, þy læs þe ænig ungecyrred woroldman mid nytnesse &
ungewitte regules geboda abræce & þære tale bruce þæt he þy
dæge misfenge þy he hit selfe nyste.
 150. Ic þa þas geþeode to micclan gesceade telede.
 151. Wel mæg dugan hit naht mid hwylcan gereorde mon sy
gestryned & to þan soþan geleafan gewæmed butan þæt an sy
þæt he gode gegange.
 153. Hæbben for þi þa ungelæredan inlendisce þæs
halgan regules cyþþe þurh agenes gereordes anwrigennesse þæt hy þe
geornlicor gode þeowien and nane tale næbben þæt hy þurh nytennesse
misfon þurfen.
 157. For þi þonne ic mid ealre estfulnesse mine æftergengan
bidde & þurh drihtnes naman halsige þæt hy þyses halgan regules
bigenc a þurh cristæs gife geycen & godiende to fulfremedum ende
gebrencgen.
 161. Ne gedyrstlæce heora nan þurh deofles myndgunge oþþe
þurh ænige gitsunge þæt he godes are gewanige oþþe ænigre
incan sece hu heo gewanod weorþe oþþe on land are oþþe on ænegum
oþrum æhtum þe læs þe þurh wædle & hæfenleaste
þære halgan æfestnesse welm awlacige and mid ealle acolige, þæt,
la, næfre ne gelumpe.
 167. Þæs þe ic wene sio æfæstnes þæs halgan
regules on ærum tidum gewanod wearþ þurh reaflac yfelra manna &
þurh geþafunge þara cynenga þe to gode lytelne ege hæfdon.
 171. Is swiþe miclan us eallum to warnienne & ure drihten to
biddenne þæt sio yrmþ on ure æfestnesse næfre eft ne geweorðe.
 173. Abbodissum we eac tæcaþ þæt hi inholde sin and
þæs halgan regoles gebodum eallum mode þeowigen and godes ælmihtiges
bebode beodaþ, þæt heora nan ne gedyrstlæce þæt heo godes
landare naþor ne heora magum ne woroldricum mid ungesceade sellen ne for
sceatte ne lyffetunge, geþencen þæt hi gode to hyrdum sin gesette &
no to reafrum.
 180. Gif heora hwilc mid deofles costnunge beswicen for gode
oþþe for worulde gyltig biþ ne gladige on þæt noþer ne cyning ne
woruldrica/ swilce him gerymed sy & antimber geseald þæt he god
bereafige þe þa æhta ah & nænne gylt næfre ne geworhte.
 184. Ne sy la nan eorðcund cyning mid gitsunge to þæm
swiþe undergan þæt he þæm heofoncundum cyninge þe hine geworhte
ne læte beon þæs ylecan rihtes weorþne þe he sylf is.
 188. Gif cinges gerefena hwylc gyltig biþ wiþ gode oþþe
wiþ men hwa is manna to þam ungescead and ungewittig þæt he þæm
cyninge his are ætrecce for þi þe his gerefa forwyrht biþ?
 191. Stande for þi on þæt ilice gerad on ecnesse swa hwæt
swa þæm ecum criste geseald biþ on cyricena æhtum, gif hwa to
þæm gedyrstig biþ þæt he þis on oþer awende he biþ
ungesælig on ecum tintragum gewitnad.
 195. Þæt, la, ne geweorþe þæt minra æftergengenna
ænig þa yrmþe geearnige.

StWulf
B17.12.
Wulfstan II of Worcester: Thorpe 1865, 445.



 1. Her geswutelað hu Wlstan bisceop becom to biscoprice.
 3. Beforan gestihtiende ure drihtene hælende and Christe to
fultumiende þære eadigan fæmnan Sancta Marian & Sancte Oswaldes.
 7. Aldred bisceop ærest gesette Wulstan bisceop to ciricwearde
þære circean on Wihgeraceastre, for his clænnysse & fægrum
þeawum.
 12. And hine syþþan wurðodon cyningas & eorlas &
ealdormen, & rice & heane hine georne biddende wæron þæt he
heom fore to Gode geþingode heore life & sawle hæle & reste.
 18. And þæræfter hine God geuferade þæt he wearð
prior & fæder þæs bufan cweðenan mynstres.
 21. Betwyxs þissum him getyþade Leofric eorl mid erndunga
Godyfan his wifes II land Blækewællan & Wulfweardig lea þe wæron
bereafode þurh Densce men & wiðerwearde deman ut of þam mynstre.
 28. Syððan Ælfgar eorl him begeat & geaf þæt land
æt Ickacumbe.
 30. And þæræfter he wæs sona to bisceope gesett &
gehadod.
 32. And us is nu swyðe earfoðe to gehreccenne hu wel he þone
bisceopdom Gode likigende & eallum mannum geheold & gestihte oðð
his lifes ende.
 37. Þæt is twa & þrittig wintra & IIII monðas
& III wucan.
 39. Syððan Ælfstan prior his broðer begeat þæt land
æt Lenc & æt Dunhamstyde & æt þecesleage.
 42. And æfter þam þe he bisceop wæs he begeat æt
Willelme cyninge æt Cullaclif II hida landes, & æt Ælfestune XV
hida, & Myttun & Eastun & twegen linde hrycgeas, & Penhyll,
& Grimanleah, & II hina wican, & hit eal to me his priore beteahte,
þe þone anweald æfter Ælfstane underfeng.
 52. And gyt him mare geuðe, þa mylne æt Norðwican, & I
feorðen dæl landes.
 55. Þærto sume þara munecena comon to grindanne, &
þæt mynstre æt Westbyrig on Gleawecestrescire.
 59. Ðæt mynster se halga Oswald ærur arærde, & hit
mid landum gegodade, & þær munekas gesette, ac hit wearð æfter
his forðsiðe, þurh yfele men & wicingas eall awest, swa þæt
þær næs butan I preost, se þær seldan mæssan gesang.
 67. Ac syððan se arwurða bisceop Wulstan to biscoprice feng
he hit eft geedstaðalade, & hit mid reafum & lande gegodade, & to
Sancte Marian mynstre beteahte, & þær munekas gelohgode swa fela swa
hit aberan mæg, oððæt hit gyt God geyce swa his willa si.
